Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
kasyacit tv atha kālasya rājā daśarathaḥ sutam 
bharataṃ kekayīputram abravīd raghunandanaḥ  RamS 
ayaṃ kekayarājasya putro vasati putraka 
tvāṃ netum āgato vīra yudhājin mātulas tava  RamS 
śrutvā daśarathasyaitad bharataḥ kekayīsutaḥ 
gamanāyābhicakrāma śatrughnasahitas tadā  RamS 
āpṛcchya pitaraṃ śūro rāmaṃ cākliṣṭakāriṇam 
mātḥṃś cāpi naraśreṣṭhaḥ śatrughnasahito yayau  RamS 
yudhājit prāpya bharataṃ saśatrughnaṃ praharṣitaḥ 
svapuraṃ prāviśad vīraḥ pitā tasya tutoṣa ha  RamS 
sa tatra nyavasad bhrātrā saha satkārasatkṛtaḥ 
mātulenāśvapatinā putrasnehena lālitaḥ  RamS 
tatrāpi nivasantau tau tarpyamāṇau ca kāmataḥ 
bhrātarau smaratāṃ vīrau vṛddhaṃ daśarathaṃ nṛpam  RamS 
rājāpi tau mahātejāḥ sasmāra proṣitau sutau 
ubhau bharataśatrughnau mahendravaruṇopamau  RamS 
sarva eva tu tasyeṣṭāś catvāraḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ 
svaśarīrād vinirvṛttāś catvāra iva bāhavaḥ  RamS 
teṣām api mahātejā rāmo ratikaraḥ pituḥ 
svayambhūr iva bhūtānāṃ babhūva guṇavattaraḥ  RamS 
gate ca bharate rāmo lakṣmaṇaś ca mahābalaḥ 
pitaraṃ devasaṃkāśaṃ pūjayāmāsatus tadā  RamS 
pitur ājñāṃ puraskṛtya paurakāryāṇi sarvaśaḥ 
cakāra rāmo dharmātmā priyāṇi ca hitāni ca  RamS 
mātṛbhyo mātṛkāryāṇi kṛtvā paramayantritaḥ 
gurūṇāṃ gurukāryāṇi kāle kāle 'nvavaikṣata  RamS 
evaṃ daśarathaḥ prīto brāhmaṇā naigamās tathā 
rāmasya śīlavṛttena sarve viṣayavāsinaḥ  RamS 
sa hi nityaṃ praśāntātmā mṛdupūrvaṃ ca bhāṣate 
ucyamāno 'pi paruṣaṃ nottaraṃ pratipadyate  RamS 
kathaṃcid upakāreṇa kṛtenaikena tuṣyati 
na smaraty apakārāṇāṃ śatam apy ātmavattayā  RamS 
śīlavṛddhair jñānavṛddhair vayovṛddhaiś ca sajjanaiḥ 
kathayann āsta vai nityam astrayogyāntareṣv api  RamS 
kalyāṇābhijanaḥ sādhur adīnaḥ satyavāg ṛjuḥ 
vṛddhair abhivinītaś ca dvijair dharmārthadarśibhiḥ  RamS 
dharmārthakāmatattvajñaḥ smṛtimān pratibhāvanān 
laukike samayācare kṛtakalpo viśāradaḥ  RamS 
śāstrajñaś ca kṛtajñaś ca puruṣāntarakovidaḥ 
yaḥ pragrahānugrahayor yathānyāyaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ  RamS 
āyakarmaṇy upāyajñaḥ saṃdṛṣṭavyayakarmavit 
śraiṣṭhyaṃ śāstrasamūheṣu prāpto vyāmiśrakeṣv api  RamS 
arthadharmau ca saṃgṛhya sukhatantro na cālasaḥ 
vaihārikāṇāṃ śilpānāṃ vijñātārthavibhāgavit  RamS 
ārohe vinaye caiva yukto vāraṇavājinām 
dhanurvedavidāṃ śreṣṭho loke 'tirathasaṃmataḥ  RamS 
abhiyātā prahartā ca senānayaviśāradaḥ 
apradhṛṣyaś ca saṃgrāme kruddhair api surāsuraiḥ 
anasūyo jitakrodho na dṛpto na ca matsarī 
na cāvamantā bhūtānāṃ na ca kālavaśānugaḥ  RamS 
evaṃ śreṣṭhair guṇair yuktaḥ prajānāṃ pārthivātmajaḥ 
saṃmatas triṣu lokeṣu vasudhāyāḥ kṣamāguṇaiḥ 
buddhyā bṛhaspates tulyo vīryeṇāpi śacīpateḥ  RamS 
tathā sarvaprajākāntaiḥ prītisaṃjananaiḥ pituḥ 
guṇair viruruce rāmo dīptaḥ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥ  RamS 
tam evaṃvṛttasampannam apradhṛṣyaparākramam 
lokapālopamaṃ nātham akāmayata medinī  RamS 
etais tu bahubhir yuktaṃ guṇair anupamaiḥ sutam 
dṛṣṭvā daśaratho rājā cakre cintāṃ paraṃtapaḥ  RamS 
eṣā hy asya parā prītir hṛdi samparivartate 
kadā nāma sutaṃ drakṣyāmy abhiṣiktam ahaṃ priyam  RamS 
vṛddhikāmo hi lokasya sarvabhūtānukampanaḥ 
mattaḥ priyataro loke parjanya iva vṛṣṭimān  RamS 
yamaśakrasamo vīrye bṛhaspatisamo matau 
mahīdharasamo dhṛtyāṃ mattaś ca guṇavattaraḥ  RamS 
mahīm aham imāṃ kṛtsnām adhitiṣṭhantam ātmajam 
anena vayasā dṛṣṭvā yathā svargam avāpnuyām  RamS 
taṃ samīkṣya mahārājo yuktaṃ samuditair guṇaiḥ 
niścitya sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ yuvarājam amanyata  RamS 
nānānagaravāstavyān pṛthagjānapadān api 
samānināya medinyāḥ pradhānān pṛthivīpatiḥ  RamS 
atha rājavitīrṇeṣu vividheṣv āsaneṣu ca 
rājānam evābhimukhā niṣedur niyatā nṛpāḥ  RamS 
sa labdhamānair vinayānvitair nṛpaiḥ purālayair jānapadaiś ca mānavaiḥ 
upopaviṣṭair nṛpatir vṛto babhau sahasracakṣur bhagavān ivāmaraiḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tataḥ pariṣadaṃ sarvām āmantrya vasudhādhipaḥ 
hitam uddharṣaṇaṃ cedam uvācāpratimaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
dundubhisvanakalpena gambhīreṇānunādinā 
svareṇa mahatā rājā jīmūta iva nādayan  RamS 
so 'ham ikṣvākubhiḥ pūrvair narendraiḥ paripālitam 
śreyasā yoktukāmo 'smi sukhārham akhilaṃ jagat  RamS 
mayāpy ācaritaṃ pūrvaiḥ panthānam anugacchatā 
prajā nityam atandreṇa yathāśakty abhirakṣatā  RamS 
idaṃ śarīraṃ kṛtsnasya lokasya caratā hitam 
pāṇḍur asyātapatrasya chāyāyāṃ jaritaṃ mayā  RamS 
prāpya varṣasahasrāṇi bahūny āyūṃṣi jīvitaḥ 
jīrṇasyāsya śarīrasya viśrāntim abhirocaye  RamS 
rājaprabhāvajuṣṭāṃ hi durvahām ajitendriyaiḥ 
pariśrānto 'smi lokasya gurvīṃ dharmadhuraṃ vahan  RamS 
so 'haṃ viśramam icchāmi putraṃ kṛtvā prajāhite 
saṃnikṛṣṭān imān sarvān anumānya dvijarṣabhān  RamS 
anujāto hi me sarvair guṇair jyeṣṭho mamātmajaḥ 
puraṃdarasamo vīrye rāmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ  RamS 
taṃ candram iva puṣyeṇa yuktaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varam 
yauvarājyena yoktāsmi prītaḥ puruṣapuṃgavam  RamS 
anurūpaḥ sa vo nātho lakṣmīvāṃl lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ 
trailokyam api nāthena yena syān nāthavattaram  RamS 
anena śreyasā sadyaḥ saṃyojyāham imāṃ mahīm 
gatakleśo bhaviṣyāmi sute tasmin niveśya vai  RamS 
iti bruvantaṃ muditāḥ pratyanandan nṛpā nṛpam 
vṛṣṭimantaṃ mahāmeghaṃ nardantam iva barhiṇaḥ  RamS 
tasya dharmārthaviduṣo bhāvam ājñāya sarvaśaḥ 
ūcuś ca manasā jñātvā vṛddhaṃ daśarathaṃ nṛpam  RamS 
anekavarṣasāhasro vṛddhas tvam asi pārthiva 
sa rāmaṃ yuvarājānam abhiṣiñcasva pārthivam  RamS 
iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rājā teṣāṃ manaḥpriyam 
ajānann iva jijñāsur idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
kathaṃ nu mayi dharmeṇa pṛthivīm anuśāsati 
bhavanto draṣṭum icchanti yuvarājaṃ mamātmajam  RamS 
te tam ūcur mahātmānaṃ paurajānapadaiḥ saha 
bahavo nṛpa kalyāṇā guṇāḥ putrasya santi te  RamS 
divyair guṇaiḥ śakrasamo rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ 
ikṣvākubhyo hi sarvebhyo 'py atirakto viśāmpate  RamS 
rāmaḥ satpuruṣo loke satyadharmaparāyaṇaḥ 
dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca śīlavān anasūyakaḥ  RamS 
kṣāntaḥ sāntvayitā ślakṣṇaḥ kṛtajño vijitendriyaḥ 
mṛduś ca sthiracittaś ca sadā bhavyo 'nasūyakaḥ  RamS 
priyavādī ca bhūtānāṃ satyavādī ca rāghavaḥ 
bahuśrutānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ brāhmaṇānām upāsitā  RamS 
tenāsyehātulā kīrtir yaśas tejaś ca vardhate 
devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ sarvāstreṣu viśāradaḥ  RamS 
yadā vrajati saṃgrāmaṃ grāmārthe nagarasya vā 
gatvā saumitrisahito nāvijitya nivartate  RamS 
saṃgrāmāt punar āgamya kuñjareṇa rathena vā 
paurān svajanavan nityaṃ kuśalaṃ paripṛcchati  RamS 
putreṣv agniṣu dāreṣu preṣyaśiṣyagaṇeṣu ca 
nikhilenānupūrvyā ca pitā putrān ivaurasān  RamS 
śuśrūṣante ca vaḥ śiṣyāḥ kaccit karmasu daṃśitāḥ 
iti naḥ puruṣavyāghraḥ sadā rāmo 'bhibhāṣate  RamS 
vyasaneṣu manuṣyāṇāṃ bhṛśaṃ bhavati duḥkhitaḥ 
utsaveṣu ca sarveṣu piteva parituṣyati  RamS 
satyavādī maheṣvāso vṛddhasevī jitendriyaḥ 
vatsaḥ śreyasi jātas te diṣṭyāsau tava rāghavaḥ 
diṣṭyā putraguṇair yukto mārīca iva kaśyapaḥ  RamS 
balam ārogyam āyuś ca rāmasya viditātmanaḥ 
āśaṃsate janaḥ sarvo rāṣṭre puravare tathā  RamS 
abhyantaraś ca bāhyaś ca paurajānapado janaḥ 
striyo vṛddhās taruṇyaś ca sāyamprātaḥ samāhitāḥ  RamS 
sarvān devān namasyanti rāmasyārthe yaśasvinaḥ 
teṣām āyācitaṃ deva tvatprasādāt samṛdhyatām  RamS 
rāmam indīvaraśyāmaṃ sarvaśatrunibarhaṇam 
paśyāmo yauvarājyasthaṃ tava rājottamātmajam  RamS 
taṃ devadevopamam ātmajaṃ te sarvasya lokasya hite niviṣṭam 
hitāya naḥ kṣipram udārajuṣṭaṃ mudābhiṣektuṃ varada tvam arhasi  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
teṣām añjalipadmāni pragṛhītāni sarvaśaḥ 
pratigṛhyābravīd rājā tebhyaḥ priyahitaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
aho 'smi paramaprītaḥ prabhāvaś cātulo mama 
yan me jyeṣṭhaṃ priyaṃ putraṃ yauvarājyastham icchatha  RamS 
iti pratyarcya tān rājā brāhmaṇān idam abravīt 
vasiṣṭhaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca teṣām evopaśṛṇvatām  RamS 
caitraḥ śrīmān ayaṃ māsaḥ puṇyaḥ puṣpitakānanaḥ 
yauvarājyāya rāmasya sarvam evopakalpyatām  RamS 
kṛtam ity eva cābrūtām abhigamya jagatpatim 
yathoktavacanaṃ prītau harṣayuktau dvijarṣabhau  RamS 
tataḥ sumantraṃ dyutimān rājā vacanam abravīt 
rāmaḥ kṛtātmā bhavatā śīghram ānīyatām iti  RamS 
sa tatheti pratijñāya sumantro rājaśāsanāt 
rāmaṃ tatrānayāṃcakre rathena rathināṃ varam  RamS 
atha tatra samāsīnās tadā daśarathaṃ nṛpam 
prācyodīcyāḥ pratīcyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca bhūmipāḥ  RamS 
mlecchāś cāryāś ca ye cānye vanaśailāntavāsinaḥ 
upāsāṃcakrire sarve taṃ devā iva vāsavam  RamS 
teṣāṃ madhye sa rājarṣir marutām iva vāsavaḥ 
prāsādastho rathagataṃ dadarśāyāntam ātmajam  RamS 
gandharvarājapratimaṃ loke vikhyātapauruṣam 
dīrghabāhuṃ mahāsattvaṃ mattamātaṃgagāminam  RamS 
candrakāntānanaṃ rāmam atīva priyadarśanam 
rūpaudāryaguṇaiḥ puṃsāṃ dṛṣṭicittāpahāriṇam  RamS 
gharmābhitaptāḥ parjanyaṃ hlādayantam iva prajāḥ 
na tatarpa samāyāntaṃ paśyamāno narādhipaḥ  RamS 
avatārya sumantras taṃ rāghavaṃ syandanottamāt 
pituḥ samīpaṃ gacchantaṃ prāñjaliḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nvagāt  RamS 
sa taṃ kailāsaśṛṅgābhaṃ prāsādaṃ narapuṃgavaḥ 
āruroha nṛpaṃ draṣṭuṃ saha sūtena rāghavaḥ  RamS 
sa prāñjalir abhipretya praṇataḥ pitur antike 
nāma svaṃ śrāvayan rāmo vavande caraṇau pituḥ  RamS 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā praṇataṃ pārśve kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ nṛpaḥ 
gṛhyāñjalau samākṛṣya sasvaje priyam ātmajam  RamS 
tasmai cābhyudyataṃ śrīmān maṇikāñcanabhūṣitam 
dideśa rājā ruciraṃ rāmāya paramāsanam  RamS 
tad āsanavaraṃ prāpya vyadīpayata rāghavaḥ 
svayeva prabhayā merum udaye vimalo raviḥ  RamS 
tena vibhrājitā tatra sā sabhābhivyarocata 
vimalagrahanakṣatrā śāradī dyaur ivendunā  RamS 
taṃ paśyamāno nṛpatis tutoṣa priyam ātmajam 
alaṃkṛtam ivātmānam ādarśatalasaṃsthitam  RamS 
sa taṃ sasmitam ābhāṣya putraṃ putravatāṃ varaḥ 
uvācedaṃ vaco rājā devendram iva kaśyapaḥ  RamS 
jyeṣṭhāyām asi me patnyāṃ sadṛśyāṃ sadṛśaḥ sutaḥ 
utpannas tvaṃ guṇaśreṣṭho mama rāmātmajaḥ priyaḥ  RamS 
tvayā yataḥ prajāś cemāḥ svaguṇair anurañjitāḥ 
tasmāt tvaṃ puṣyayogena yauvarājyam avāpnuhi  RamS 
kāmatas tvaṃ prakṛtyaiva vinīto guṇavān asi 
guṇavaty api tu snehāt putra vakṣyāmi te hitam  RamS 
bhūyo vinayam āsthāya bhava nityaṃ jitendriyaḥ 
kāmakrodhasamutthāni tyajethā vyasanāni ca  RamS 
parokṣayā vartamāno vṛttyā pratyakṣayā tathā 
amātyaprabhṛtīḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtīś cānurañjaya  RamS 
tuṣṭānuraktaprakṛtir yaḥ pālayati medinīm 
tasya nandanti mitrāṇi labdhvāmṛtam ivāmarāḥ 
tasmāt putra tvam ātmānaṃ niyamyaiva samācara  RamS 
tac chrutvā suhṛdas tasya rāmasya priyakāriṇaḥ 
tvaritāḥ śīghram abhyetya kausalyāyai nyavedayan  RamS 
sā hiraṇyaṃ ca gāś caiva ratnāni vividhāni ca 
vyādideśa priyākhyebhyaḥ kausalyā pramadottamā  RamS 
athābhivādya rājānaṃ ratham āruhya rāghavaḥ 
yayau svaṃ dyutimad veśma janaughaiḥ pratipūjitaḥ  RamS 
te cāpi paurā nṛpater vacas tacchrutvā tadā lābham iveṣṭam āpya 
narendram āmantrya gṛhāṇi gatvā devān samānarcur atīva hṛṣṭāḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
gateṣv atha nṛpo bhūyaḥ paureṣu saha mantribhiḥ 
mantrayitvā tataś cakre niścayajñaḥ sa niścayam  RamS 
śva eva puṣyo bhavitā śvo 'bhiṣecyas tu me sutaḥ 
rāmo rājīvatāmrākṣo yauvarājya iti prabhuḥ  RamS 
athāntargṛham āviśya rājā daśarathas tadā 
sūtam ājñāpayāmāsa rāmaṃ punar ihānaya  RamS 
pratigṛhya sa tadvākyaṃ sūtaḥ punar upāyayau 
rāmasya bhavanaṃ śīghraṃ rāmam ānayituṃ punaḥ  RamS 
dvāḥsthair āveditaṃ tasya rāmāyāgamanaṃ punaḥ 
śrutvaiva cāpi rāmas taṃ prāptaṃ śaṅkānvito 'bhavat  RamS 
praveśya cainaṃ tvaritaṃ rāmo vacanam abravīt 
yad āgamanakṛtyaṃ te bhūyas tad brūhy aśeṣataḥ  RamS 
tam uvāca tataḥ sūto rājā tvāṃ draṣṭum icchati 
śrutvā pramāṇam atra tvaṃ gamanāyetarāya vā  RamS 
iti sūtavacaḥ śrutvā rāmo 'tha tvarayānvitaḥ 
prayayau rājabhavanaṃ punar draṣṭuṃ nareśvaram  RamS 
taṃ śrutvā samanuprāptaṃ rāmaṃ daśaratho nṛpaḥ 
praveśayāmāsa gṛhaṃ vivikṣuḥ priyam uttamam  RamS 
praviśann eva ca śrīmān rāghavo bhavanaṃ pituḥ 
dadarśa pitaraṃ dūrāt praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ  RamS 
praṇamantaṃ samutthāpya taṃ pariṣvajya bhūmipaḥ 
pradiśya cāsmai ruciram āsanaṃ punar abravīt  RamS 
rāma vṛddho 'smi dīrghāyur bhuktā bhogā mayepsitāḥ 
annavadbhiḥ kratuśatais tatheṣṭaṃ bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ  RamS 
jātam iṣṭam apatyaṃ me tvam adyānupamaṃ bhuvi 
dattam iṣṭam adhītaṃ ca mayā puruṣasattama  RamS 
anubhūtāni ceṣṭāni mayā vīra sukhāni ca 
devarṣipitṛviprāṇām anṛṇo 'smi tathātmanaḥ  RamS 
na kiṃcin mama kartavyaṃ tavānyatrābhiṣecanāt 
ato yat tvām ahaṃ brūyāṃ tan me tvaṃ kartum arhasi  RamS 
adya prakṛtayaḥ sarvās tvām icchanti narādhipam 
atas tvāṃ yuvarājānam abhiṣekṣyāmi putraka  RamS 
api cādyāśubhān rāma svapnān paśyāmi dāruṇān 
sanirghātā maholkāś ca patantīha mahāsvanāḥ  RamS 
avaṣṭabdhaṃ ca me rāma nakṣatraṃ dāruṇair grahaiḥ 
āvedayanti daivajñāḥ sūryāṅgārakarāhubhiḥ  RamS 
prāyeṇa hi nimittānām īdṛśānāṃ samudbhave 
rājā vā mṛtyum āpnoti ghorāṃ vāpadam ṛcchati  RamS 
tad yāvad eva me ceto na vimuhyati rāghava 
tāvad evābhiṣiñcasva calā hi prāṇināṃ matiḥ  RamS 
adya candro 'bhyupagataḥ puṣyāt pūrvaṃ punar vasum 
śvaḥ puṣyayogaṃ niyataṃ vakṣyante daivacintakāḥ  RamS 
tatra puṣye 'bhiṣiñcasva manas tvarayatīva mām 
śvas tvāham abhiṣekṣyāmi yauvarājye paraṃtapa  RamS 
tasmāt tvayādya vratinā niśeyaṃ niyatātmanā 
saha vadhvopavastavyā darbhaprastaraśāyinā  RamS 
suhṛdaś cāpramattās tvāṃ rakṣantv adya samantataḥ 
bhavanti bahuvighnāni kāryāṇy evaṃvidhāni hi  RamS 
viproṣitaś ca bharato yāvad eva purād itaḥ 
tāvad evābhiṣekas te prāptakālo mato mama  RamS 
kāmaṃ khalu satāṃ vṛtte bhrātā te bharataḥ sthitaḥ 
jyeṣṭhānuvartī dharmātmā sānukrośo jitendriyaḥ  RamS 
kiṃ tu cittaṃ manuṣyāṇām anityam iti me matiḥ 
satāṃ ca dharmanityānāṃ kṛtaśobhi ca rāghava  RamS 
ity uktaḥ so 'bhyanujñātaḥ śvobhāviny abhiṣecane 
vrajeti rāmaḥ pitaram abhivādyābhyayād gṛham  RamS 
praviśya cātmano veśma rājñoddiṣṭe 'bhiṣecane 
tasmin kṣaṇe vinirgatya mātur antaḥpuraṃ yayau  RamS 
tatra tāṃ pravaṇām eva mātaraṃ kṣaumavāsinīm 
vāgyatāṃ devatāgāre dadarśa yācatīṃ śriyam  RamS 
prāg eva cāgatā tatra sumitrā lakṣmaṇas tathā 
sītā cānāyitā śrutvā priyaṃ rāmābhiṣecanam  RamS 
tasmin kāle hi kausalyā tasthāv āmīlitekṣaṇā 
sumitrayānvāsyamānā sītayā lakṣmaṇena ca  RamS 
śrutvā puṣyeṇa putrasya yauvarājyābhiṣecanam 
prāṇāyāmena puruṣaṃ dhyāyamānā janārdanam  RamS 
tathā saniyamām eva so 'bhigamyābhivādya ca 
uvāca vacanaṃ rāmo harṣayaṃs tām idaṃ tadā  RamS 
amba pitrā niyukto 'smi prajāpālanakarmaṇi 
bhavitā śvo 'bhiṣeko me yathā me śāsanaṃ pituḥ  RamS 
sītayāpy upavastavyā rajanīyaṃ mayā saha 
evam ṛtvigupādhyāyaiḥ saha mām uktavān pitā  RamS 
yāni yāny atra yogyāni śvobhāviny abhiṣecane 
tāni me maṅgalāny adya vaidehyāś caiva kāraya  RamS 
etac chrutvā tu kausalyā cirakālābhikāṅkṣitam 
harṣabāṣpakalaṃ vākyam idaṃ rāmam abhāṣata  RamS 
vatsa rāma ciraṃ jīva hatās te paripanthinaḥ 
jñātīn me tvaṃ śriyā yuktaḥ sumitrāyāś ca nandaya  RamS 
kalyāṇe bata nakṣatre mayi jāto 'si putraka 
yena tvayā daśaratho guṇair ārādhitaḥ pitā  RamS 
amoghaṃ bata me kṣāntaṃ puruṣe puṣkarekṣaṇe 
yeyam ikṣvākurājyaśrīḥ putra tvāṃ saṃśrayiṣyati  RamS 
ity evam ukto mātredaṃ rāmo bhrātaram abravīt 
prāñjaliṃ prahvam āsīnam abhivīkṣya smayann iva  RamS 
lakṣmaṇemāṃ mayā sārdhaṃ praśādhi tvaṃ vasuṃdharām 
dvitīyaṃ me 'ntarātmānaṃ tvām iyaṃ śrīr upasthitā  RamS 
saumitre bhuṅkṣva bhogāṃs tvam iṣṭān rājyaphalāni ca 
jīvitaṃ ca hi rājyaṃ ca tvadartham abhikāmaye  RamS 
ity uktvā lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo mātarāv abhivādya ca 
abhyanujñāpya sītāṃ ca jagāma svaṃ niveśanam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
saṃdiśya rāmaṃ nṛpatiḥ śvobhāviny abhiṣecane 
purohitaṃ samāhūya vasiṣṭham idam abravīt  RamS 
gacchopavāsaṃ kākutsthaṃ kārayādya tapodhana 
śrīyaśorājyalābhāya vadhvā saha yatavratam  RamS 
tatheti ca sa rājānam uktvā vedavidāṃ varaḥ 
svayaṃ vasiṣṭho bhagavān yayau rāmaniveśanam  RamS 
sa rāmabhavanaṃ prāpya pāṇḍurābhraghanaprabham 
tisraḥ kakṣyā rathenaiva viveśa munisattamaḥ  RamS 
tam āgatam ṛṣiṃ rāmas tvarann iva sasaṃbhramaḥ 
mānayiṣyan sa mānārhaṃ niścakrāma niveśanāt  RamS 
abhyetya tvaramāṇaś ca rathābhyāśaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ 
tato 'vatārayāmāsa parigṛhya rathāt svayam  RamS 
sa cainaṃ praśritaṃ dṛṣṭvā sambhāṣyābhiprasādya ca 
priyārhaṃ harṣayan rāmam ity uvāca purohitaḥ  RamS 
prasannas te pitā rāma yauvarājyam avāpsyasi 
upavāsaṃ bhavān adya karotu saha sītayā  RamS 
prātas tvām abhiṣektā hi yauvarājye narādhipaḥ 
pitā daśarathaḥ prītyā yayātiṃ nahuṣo yathā  RamS 
ity uktvā sa tadā rāmam upavāsaṃ yatavratam 
mantravat kārayāmāsa vaidehyā sahitaṃ muniḥ  RamS 
tato yathāvad rāmeṇa sa rājño gurur arcitaḥ 
abhyanujñāpya kākutsthaṃ yayau rāmaniveśanāt  RamS 
suhṛdbhis tatra rāmo 'pi tān anujñāpya sarvaśaḥ 
sabhājito viveśātha tān anujñāpya sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
hṛṣṭanārīnarayutaṃ rāmaveśma tadā babhau 
yathā mattadvijagaṇaṃ praphullanalinaṃ saraḥ  RamS 
sa rājabhavanaprakhyāt tasmād rāmaniveśanāt 
nirgatya dadṛśe mārgaṃ vasiṣṭho janasaṃvṛtam  RamS 
vṛndavṛndair ayodhyāyāṃ rājamārgāḥ samantataḥ 
babhūvur abhisaṃbādhāḥ kutūhalajanair vṛtāḥ  RamS 
janavṛndormisaṃgharṣaharṣasvanavatas tadā 
babhūva rājamārgasya sāgarasyeva nisvanaḥ  RamS 
siktasaṃmṛṣṭarathyā hi tad ahar vanamālinī 
āsīd ayodhyā nagarī samucchritagṛhadhvajā  RamS 
tadā hy ayodhyānilayaḥ sastrībālābalo janaḥ 
rāmābhiṣekam ākāṅkṣann ākāṅkṣann udayaṃ raveḥ  RamS 
prajālaṃkārabhūtaṃ ca janasyānandavardhanam 
utsuko 'bhūj jano draṣṭuṃ tam ayodhyāmahotsavam  RamS 
evaṃ taṃ janasambādhaṃ rājamārgaṃ purohitaḥ 
vyūhann iva janaughaṃ taṃ śanai rājakulaṃ yayau  RamS 
sitābhraśikharaprakhyaṃ prāsādam adhiruhya saḥ 
samiyāya narendreṇa śakreṇeva bṛhaspatiḥ  RamS 
tam āgatam abhiprekṣya hitvā rājāsanaṃ nṛpaḥ 
papraccha sa ca tasmai tat kṛtam ity abhyavedayat  RamS 
guruṇā tv abhyanujñāto manujaughaṃ visṛjya tam 
viveśāntaḥpuraṃ rājā siṃho giriguhām iva  RamS 
tad agryaveṣapramadājanākulaṃ mahendraveśmapratimaṃ niveśanam 
vidīpayaṃś cāru viveśa pārthivaḥ śaśīva tārāgaṇasaṃkulaṃ nabhaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
gate purohite rāmaḥ snāto niyatamānasaḥ 
saha patnyā viśālākṣyā nārāyaṇam upāgamat  RamS 
pragṛhya śirasā pātrīṃ haviṣo vidhivat tadā 
mahate daivatāyājyaṃ juhāva jvalite 'nale  RamS 
śeṣaṃ ca haviṣas tasya prāśyāśāsyātmanaḥ priyam 
dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ svāstīrṇe kuśasaṃstare  RamS 
vāgyataḥ saha vaidehyā bhūtvā niyatamānasaḥ 
śrīmaty āyatane viṣṇoḥ śiśye naravarātmajaḥ  RamS 
ekayāmāvaśiṣṭāyāṃ rātryāṃ prativibudhya saḥ 
alaṃkāravidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ kārayāmāsa veśmanaḥ  RamS 
tatra śṛṇvan sukhā vācaḥ sūtamāgadhabandinām 
pūrvāṃ saṃdhyām upāsīno jajāpa yatamānasaḥ  RamS 
tuṣṭāva praṇataś caiva śirasā madhusūdanam 
vimalakṣaumasaṃvīto vācayāmāsa ca dvijān  RamS 
teṣāṃ puṇyāhaghoṣo 'tha gambhīramadhuras tadā 
ayodhyāṃ pūrayāmāsa tūryaghoṣānunāditaḥ  RamS 
kṛtopavāsaṃ tu tadā vaidehyā saha rāghavam 
ayodhyānilayaḥ śrutvā sarvaḥ pramudito janaḥ  RamS 
tataḥ paurajanaḥ sarvaḥ śrutvā rāmābhiṣecanam 
prabhātāṃ rajanīṃ dṛṣṭvā cakre śobhāṃ parāṃ punaḥ  RamS 
sitābhraśikharābheṣu devatāyataneṣu ca 
catuṣpatheṣu rathyāsu caityeṣv aṭṭālakeṣu ca  RamS 
nānāpaṇyasamṛddheṣu vaṇijām āpaṇeṣu ca 
kuṭumbināṃ samṛddheṣu śrīmatsu bhavaneṣu ca  RamS 
sabhāsu caiva sarvāsu vṛkṣeṣv ālakṣiteṣu ca 
dhvajāḥ samucchritāś citrāḥ patākāś cābhavaṃs tadā  RamS 
naṭanartakasaṃghānāṃ gāyakānāṃ ca gāyatām 
manaḥkarṇasukhā vācaḥ śuśruvuś ca tatas tataḥ  RamS 
rāmābhiṣekayuktāś ca kathāś cakrur mitho janāḥ 
rāmābhiṣeke samprāpte catvareṣu gṛheṣu ca  RamS 
bālā api krīḍamānā gṛhadvāreṣu saṃghaśaḥ 
rāmābhiṣekasaṃyuktāś cakrur eva mithaḥ kathāḥ  RamS 
kṛtapuṣpopahāraś ca dhūpagandhādhivāsitaḥ 
rājamārgaḥ kṛtaḥ śrīmān paurai rāmābhiṣecane  RamS 
prakāśakaraṇārthaṃ ca niśāgamanaśaṅkayā 
dīpavṛkṣāṃs tathā cakrur anu rathyāsu sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
alaṃkāraṃ purasyaivaṃ kṛtvā tatpuravāsinaḥ 
ākāṅkṣamāṇā rāmasya yauvarājyābhiṣecanam  RamS 
sametya saṃghaśaḥ sarve catvareṣu sabhāsu ca 
kathayanto mithas tatra praśaśaṃsur janādhipam  RamS 
aho mahātmā rājāyam ikṣvākukulanandanaḥ 
jñātvā yo vṛddham ātmānaṃ rāmaṃ rājye 'hbiṣekṣyati  RamS 
sarve hy anugṛhītāḥ sma yan no rāmo mahīpatiḥ 
cirāya bhavitā goptā dṛṣṭalokaparāvaraḥ  RamS 
anuddhatamanā vidvān dharmātmā bhrātṛvatsalaḥ 
yathā ca bhrātṛṣu snigdhas tathāsmāsv api rāghavaḥ  RamS 
ciraṃ jīvatu dharmātmā rājā daśaratho 'naghaḥ 
yatprasādenābhiṣiktaṃ rāmaṃ drakṣyāmahe vayam  RamS 
evaṃvidhaṃ kathayatāṃ paurāṇāṃ śuśruvus tadā 
digbhyo 'pi śrutavṛttāntāḥ prāptā jānapadā janāḥ  RamS 
te tu digbhyaḥ purīṃ prāptā draṣṭuṃ rāmābhiṣecanam 
rāmasya pūrayāmāsuḥ purīṃ jānapadā janāḥ  RamS 
janaughais tair visarpadbhiḥ śuśruve tatra nisvanaḥ 
parvasūdīrṇavegasya sāgarasyeva nisvanaḥ  RamS 
tatas tad indrakṣayasaṃnibhaṃ puraṃ didṛkṣubhir jānapadair upāgataiḥ 
samantataḥ sasvanam ākulaṃ babhau samudrayādobhir ivārṇavodakam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
jñātidāsī yato jātā kaikeyyās tu sahoṣitā 
prāsādaṃ candrasaṃkāśam āruroha yadṛcchayā  RamS 
siktarājapathāṃ kṛtsnāṃ prakīrṇakamalotpalām 
ayodhyāṃ mantharā tasmāt prāsādād anvavaikṣata  RamS 
patākābhir varārhābhir dhvajaiś ca samalaṃkṛtām 
siktāṃ candanatoyaiś ca śiraḥsnātajanair vṛtām  RamS 
avidūre sthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā dhātrīṃ papraccha mantharā 
uttamenābhisaṃyuktā harṣeṇārthaparā satī  RamS 
rāmamātā dhanaṃ kiṃ nu janebhyaḥ samprayacchati 
atimātraṃ praharṣo 'yaṃ kiṃ janasya ca śaṃsa me 
kārayiṣyati kiṃ vāpi samprahṛṣṭo mahīpatiḥ  RamS 
vidīryamāṇā harṣeṇa dhātrī paramayā mudā 
ācacakṣe 'tha kubjāyai bhūyasīṃ rāghave śriyam  RamS 
śvaḥ puṣyeṇa jitakrodhaṃ yauvarājyena rāghavam 
rājā daśaratho rāmam abhiṣecayitānagham  RamS 
dhātryās tu vacanaṃ śrutvā kubjā kṣipram amarṣitā 
kailāsaśikharākārāt prāsādād avarohata  RamS 
sā dahyamānā kopena mantharā pāpadarśinī 
śayānām etya kaikeyīm idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
uttiṣṭha mūḍhe kiṃ śeṣe bhayaṃ tvām abhivartate 
upaplutamahaughena kim ātmānaṃ na budhyase  RamS 
aniṣṭe subhagākāre saubhāgyena vikatthase 
calaṃ hi tava saubhāgyaṃ nadyāḥ srota ivoṣṇage  RamS 
evam uktā tu kaikeyī ruṣṭayā paruṣaṃ vacaḥ 
kubjayā pāpadarśinyā viṣādam agamat param  RamS 
kaikeyī tv abravīt kubjāṃ kaccit kṣemaṃ na manthare 
viṣaṇṇavadanāṃ hi tvāṃ lakṣaye bhṛśaduḥkhitām  RamS 
mantharā tu vacaḥ śrutvā kaikeyyā madhurākṣaram 
uvāca krodhasaṃyuktā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradā  RamS 
sā viṣaṇṇatarā bhūtvā kubjā tasyā hitaiṣiṇī 
viṣādayantī provāca bhedayantī ca rāghavam  RamS 
akṣemaṃ sumahad devi pravṛttaṃ tvadvināśanam 
rāmaṃ daśaratho rājā yauvarājye 'bhiṣekṣyati  RamS 
sāsmy agādhe bhaye magnā duḥkhaśokasamanvitā 
dahyamānānaleneva tvaddhitārtham ihāgatā  RamS 
tava duḥkhena kaikeyi mama duḥkhaṃ mahad bhavet 
tvadvṛddhau mama vṛddhiś ca bhaved atra na saṃśayaḥ  RamS 
narādhipakule jātā mahiṣī tvaṃ mahīpateḥ 
ugratvaṃ rājadharmāṇāṃ kathaṃ devi na budhyase  RamS 
dharmavādī śaṭho bhartā ślakṣṇavādī ca dāruṇaḥ 
śuddhabhāve na jānīṣe tenaivam atisaṃdhitā  RamS 
upasthitaṃ prayuñjānas tvayi sāntvam anarthakam 
arthenaivādya te bhartā kausalyāṃ yojayiṣyati  RamS 
apavāhya sa duṣṭātmā bharataṃ tava bandhuṣu 
kālyaṃ sthāpayitā rāmaṃ rājye nihatakaṇṭake  RamS 
śatruḥ patipravādena mātreva hitakāmyayā 
āśīviṣa ivāṅkena bāle paridhṛtas tvayā  RamS 
yathā hi kuryāt sarpo vā śatrur vā pratyupekṣitaḥ 
rājñā daśarathenādya saputrā tvaṃ tathā kṛtā  RamS 
pāpenānṛtasāntvena bāle nityaṃ sukhocite 
rāmaṃ sthāpayatā rājye sānubandhā hatā hy asi  RamS 
sā prāptakālaṃ kaikeyi kṣipraṃ kuru hitaṃ tava 
trāyasva putram ātmānaṃ māṃ ca vismayadarśane  RamS 
mantharāyā vacaḥ śrutvā śayanāt sa śubhānanā 
evam ābharaṇaṃ tasyai kubjāyai pradadau śubham  RamS 
dattvā tv ābharaṇaṃ tasyai kubjāyai pramadottamā 
kaikeyī mantharāṃ hṛṣṭā punar evābravīd idam  RamS 
idaṃ tu manthare mahyam ākhyāsi paramaṃ priyam 
etan me priyam ākhyātuḥ kiṃ vā bhūyaḥ karomi te  RamS 
rāme vā bharate vāhaṃ viśeṣaṃ nopalakṣaye 
tasmāt tuṣṭāsmi yad rājā rāmaṃ rājye 'bhiṣekṣyati  RamS 
na me paraṃ kiṃcid itas tvayā punaḥ priyaṃ priyārhe suvacaṃ vaco varam 
tathā hy avocas tvam ataḥ priyottaraṃ varaṃ paraṃ te pradadāmi taṃ vṛṇu  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
mantharā tv abhyasūyyainām utsṛjyābharaṇaṃ ca tat 
uvācedaṃ tato vākyaṃ kopaduḥkhasamanvitā  RamS 
harṣaṃ kim idam asthāne kṛtavaty asi bāliśe 
śokasāgaramadhyastham ātmānaṃ nāvabudhyase  RamS 
subhagā khalu kausalyā yasyāḥ putro 'bhiṣekṣyate 
yauvarājyena mahatā śvaḥ puṣyeṇa dvijottamaiḥ  RamS 
prāptāṃ sumahatīṃ prītiṃ pratītāṃ tāṃ hatadviṣam 
upasthāsyasi kausalyāṃ dāsīva tvaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ  RamS 
hṛṣṭāḥ khalu bhaviṣyanti rāmasya paramāḥ striyaḥ 
aprahṛṣṭā bhaviṣyanti snuṣās te bharatakṣaye  RamS 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā paramaprītāṃ bruvantīṃ mantharāṃ tataḥ 
rāmasyaiva guṇān devī kaikeyī praśaśaṃsa ha  RamS 
dharmajño gurubhir dāntaḥ kṛtajñaḥ satyavāk śuciḥ 
rāmo rājñaḥ suto jyeṣṭho yauvarājyam ato 'rhati  RamS 
bhrātḥn bhṛtyāṃś ca dīrghāyuḥ pitṛvat pālayiṣyati 
saṃtapyase kathaṃ kubje śrutvā rāmābhiṣecanam  RamS 
bharataś cāpi rāmasya dhruvaṃ varṣaśatāt param 
pitṛpaitāmahaṃ rājyam avāpsyati nararṣabhaḥ  RamS 
sā tvam abhyudaye prāpte vartamāne ca manthare 
bhaviṣyati ca kalyāṇe kimarthaṃ paritapyase 
kausalyāto 'tiriktaṃ ca sa tu śuśrūṣate hi mām  RamS 
kaikeyyā vacanaṃ śrutvā mantharā bhṛśaduḥkhitā 
dīrgham uṣṇaṃ viniḥśvasya kaikeyīm idam abravīt  RamS 
anarthadarśinī maurkhyān nātmānam avabudhyase 
śokavyasanavistīrṇe majjantī duḥkhasāgare  RamS 
bhavitā rāghavo rājā rāghavasya ca yaḥ sutaḥ 
rājavaṃśāt tu bharataḥ kaikeyi parihāsyate  RamS 
na hi rājñaḥ sutāḥ sarve rājye tiṣṭhanti bhāmini 
sthāpyamāneṣu sarveṣu sumahān anayo bhavet  RamS 
tasmāj jyeṣṭhe hi kaikeyi rājyatantrāṇi pārthivāḥ 
sthāpayanty anavadyāṅgi guṇavatsv itareṣv api  RamS 
asāv atyantanirbhagnas tava putro bhaviṣyati 
anāthavat sukhebhyaś ca rājavaṃśāc ca vatsale  RamS 
sāhaṃ tvadarthe samprāptā tvaṃ tu māṃ nāvabudhyase 
sapatnivṛddhau yā me tvaṃ pradeyaṃ dātum icchasi  RamS 
dhruvaṃ tu bharataṃ rāmaḥ prāpya rājyam akaṇṭakam 
deśāntaraṃ nāyayitvā lokāntaram athāpi vā  RamS 
bāla eva hi mātulyaṃ bharato nāyitas tvayā 
saṃnikarṣāc ca sauhārdaṃ jāyate sthāvareṣv api  RamS 
goptā hi rāmaṃ saumitrir lakṣmaṇaṃ cāpi rāghavaḥ 
aśvinor iva saubhrātraṃ tayor lokeṣu viśrutam  RamS 
tasmān na lakṣmaṇe rāmaḥ pāpaṃ kiṃcit kariṣyati 
rāmas tu bharate pāpaṃ kuryād iti na saṃśayaḥ  RamS 
tasmād rājagṛhād eva vanaṃ gacchatu te sutaḥ 
etaddhi rocate mahyaṃ bhṛśaṃ cāpi hitaṃ tava  RamS 
evaṃ te jñātipakṣasya śreyaś caiva bhaviṣyati 
yadi ced bharato dharmāt pitryaṃ rājyam avāpsyati  RamS 
sa te sukhocito bālo rāmasya sahajo ripuḥ 
samṛddhārthasya naṣṭārtho jīviṣyati kathaṃ vaśe  RamS 
abhidrutam ivāraṇye siṃhena gajayūthapam 
pracchādyamānaṃ rāmeṇa bharataṃ trātum arhasi  RamS 
darpān nirākṛtā pūrvaṃ tvayā saubhāgyavattayā 
rāmamātā sapatnī te kathaṃ vairaṃ na yātayet  RamS 
yadā hi rāmaḥ pṛthivīm avāpsyati dhruvaṃ pranaṣṭo bharato bhaviṣyati 
ato hi saṃcintaya rājyam ātmaje parasya cādyaiva vivāsakāraṇam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
evam uktā tu kaikeyī krodhena jvalitānanā 
dīrgham uṣṇaṃ viniḥśvasya mantharām idam abravīt  RamS 
adya rāmam itaḥ kṣipraṃ vanaṃ prasthāpayāmy aham 
yauvarājyena bharataṃ kṣipram evābhiṣecaye  RamS 
idaṃ tv idānīṃ saṃpaśya kenopāyena manthare 
bharataḥ prāpnuyād rājyaṃ na tu rāmaḥ kathaṃcana  RamS 
evam uktā tayā devyā mantharā pāpadarśinī 
rāmārtham upahiṃsantī kaikeyīm idam abravīt  RamS 
hantedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi kaikeyi śrūyatāṃ ca me 
yathā te bharato rājyaṃ putraḥ prāpsyati kevalam  RamS 
śrutvaivaṃ vacanaṃ tasyā mantharāyās tu kaikayī 
kiṃcid utthāya śayanāt svāstīrṇād idam abravīt  RamS 
kathaya tvaṃ mamopāyaṃ kenopāyena manthare 
bharataḥ prāpnuyād rājyaṃ na tu rāmaḥ kathaṃcana  RamS 
evam uktā tayā devyā mantharā pāpadarśinī 
rāmārtham upahiṃsantī kubjā vacanam abravīt  RamS 
tava devāsure yuddhe saha rājarṣibhiḥ patiḥ 
agacchat tvām upādāya devarājasya sāhyakṛt  RamS 
diśam āsthāya kaikeyi dakṣiṇāṃ daṇḍakān prati 
vaijayantam iti khyātaṃ puraṃ yatra timidhvajaḥ  RamS 
sa śambara iti khyātaḥ śatamāyo mahāsuraḥ 
dadau śakrasya saṃgrāmaṃ devasaṃghair anirjitaḥ  RamS 
tasmin mahati saṃgrāme rājā daśarathas tadā 
apavāhya tvayā devi saṃgrāmān naṣṭacetanaḥ  RamS 
tatrāpi vikṣataḥ śastraiḥ patis te rakṣitas tvayā 
tuṣṭena tena dattau te dvau varau śubhadarśane  RamS 
sa tvayoktaḥ patir devi yadeccheyaṃ tadā varau 
gṛhṇīyām iti tat tena tathety uktaṃ mahātmanā 
anabhijñā hy ahaṃ devi tvayaiva kathitaṃ purā  RamS 
tau varau yāca bhartāraṃ bharatasyābhiṣecanam 
pravrājanaṃ ca rāmasya tvaṃ varṣāṇi caturdaśa  RamS 
krodhāgāraṃ praviśyādya kruddhevāśvapateḥ sute 
śeṣvān antarhitāyāṃ tvaṃ bhūmau malinavāsinī 
mā smainaṃ pratyudīkṣethā mā cainam abhibhāṣathāḥ  RamS 
dayitā tvaṃ sadā bhartur atra me nāsti saṃśayaḥ 
tvatkṛte ca mahārājo viśed api hutāśanam  RamS 
na tvāṃ krodhayituṃ śakto na kruddhāṃ pratyudīkṣitum 
tava priyārthaṃ rājā hi prāṇān api parityajet  RamS 
na hy atikramituṃ śaktas tava vākyaṃ mahīpatiḥ 
mandasvabhāve budhyasva saubhāgyabalam ātmanaḥ  RamS 
maṇimuktāsuvarṇāni ratnāni vividhāni ca 
dadyād daśaratho rājā mā sma teṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥ  RamS 
yau tau devāsure yuddhe varau daśaratho 'dadāt 
tau smāraya mahābhāge so 'rtho mā tvām atikramet  RamS 
yadā tu te varaṃ dadyāt svayam utthāpya rāghavaḥ 
vyavasthāpya mahārājaṃ tvam imaṃ vṛṇuyā varam  RamS 
rāmaṃ pravrājayāraṇye nava varṣāṇi pañca ca 
bharataḥ kriyatāṃ rājā pṛthivyāṃ pārthivarṣabhaḥ  RamS 
evaṃ pravrājitaś caiva rāmo 'rāmo bhaviṣyati 
bharataś ca hatāmitras tava rājā bhaviṣyati  RamS 
yena kālena rāmaś ca vanāt pratyāgamiṣyati 
tena kālena putras te kṛtamūlo bhaviṣyati 
saṃgṛhītamanuṣyaś ca suhṛdbhiḥ sārdham ātmavān  RamS 
prāptakālaṃ tu te manye rājānaṃ vītasādhvasā 
rāmābhiṣekasaṃkalpān nigṛhya vinivartaya  RamS 
anartham artharūpeṇa grāhitā sā tatas tayā 
hṛṣṭā pratītā kaikeyī mantharām idam abravīt  RamS 
kubje tvāṃ nābhijānāmi śreṣṭhāṃ śreṣṭhābhidhāyinīm 
pṛthivyām asi kubjānām uttamā buddhiniścaye  RamS 
tvam eva tu mamārtheṣu nityayuktā hitaiṣiṇī 
nāhaṃ samavabudhyeyaṃ kubje rājñaś cikīrṣitam  RamS 
santi duḥsaṃsthitāḥ kubjā vakrāḥ paramapāpikāḥ 
tvaṃ padmam iva vātena saṃnatā priyadarśanā  RamS 
uras te 'bhiniviṣṭaṃ vai yāvat skandhāt samunnatam 
adhastāc codaraṃ śāntaṃ sunābham iva lajjitam  RamS 
jaghanaṃ tava nirghuṣṭaṃ raśanādāmaśobhitam 
jaṅghe bhṛśam upanyaste pādau cāpy āyatāv ubhau  RamS 
tvam āyatābhyāṃ sakthibhyāṃ manthare kṣaumavāsini 
agrato mama gacchantī rājahaṃsīva rājase  RamS 
tavedaṃ sthagu yad dīrghaṃ rathaghoṇam ivāyatam 
matayaḥ kṣatravidyāś ca māyāś cātra vasanti te  RamS 
atra te pratimokṣyāmi mālāṃ kubje hiraṇmayīm 
abhiṣikte ca bharate rāghave ca vanaṃ gate  RamS 
jātyena ca suvarṇena suniṣṭaptena sundari 
labdhārthā ca pratītā ca lepayiṣyāmi te sthagu  RamS 
mukhe ca tilakaṃ citraṃ jātarūpamayaṃ śubham 
kārayiṣyāmi te kubje śubhāny ābharaṇāni ca  RamS 
paridhāya śubhe vastre devateva cariṣyasi 
candram āhvayamānena mukhenāpratimānanā 
gamiṣyasi gatiṃ mukhyāṃ garvayantī dviṣajjanam  RamS 
tavāpi kubjāḥ kubjāyāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ 
pādau paricariṣyanti yathaiva tvaṃ sadā mama  RamS 
iti praśasyamānā sā kaikeyīm idam abravīt 
śayānāṃ śayane śubhre vedyām agniśikhām iva  RamS 
gatodake setubandho na kalyāṇi vidhīyate 
uttiṣṭha kuru kalyāṇaṃ rājānam anudarśaya  RamS 
tathā protsāhitā devī gatvā mantharayā saha 
krodhāgāraṃ viśālākṣī saubhāgyamadagarvitā  RamS 
anekaśatasāhasraṃ muktāhāraṃ varāṅganā 
avamucya varārhāṇi śubhāny ābharaṇāni ca  RamS 
tato hemopamā tatra kubjā vākyavaśaṃ gatā 
saṃviśya bhūmau kaikeyī mantharām idam abravīt  RamS 
iha vā māṃ mṛtāṃ kubje nṛpāyāvedayiṣyasi 
vanaṃ tu rāghave prāpte bharataḥ prāpsyati kṣitim  RamS 
athaitad uktvā vacanaṃ sudāruṇaṃ nidhāya sarvābharaṇāni bhāminī 
asaṃvṛtām āstaraṇena medinīṃ tadādhiśiśye patiteva kiṃnarī  RamS 
udīrṇasaṃrambhatamovṛtānanā tathāvamuktottamamālyabhūṣaṇā 
narendrapatnī vimanā babhūva sā tamovṛtā dyaur iva magnatārakā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
ājñāpya tu mahārājo rāghavasyābhiṣecanam 
priyārhāṃ priyam ākhyātuṃ viveśāntaḥpuraṃ vaśī  RamS 
tāṃ tatra patitāṃ bhūmau śayānām atathocitām 
pratapta iva duḥkhena so 'paśyaj jagatīpatiḥ  RamS 
sa vṛddhas taruṇīṃ bhāryāṃ prāṇebhyo 'pi garīyasīm 
apāpaḥ pāpasaṃkalpāṃ dadarśa dharaṇītale  RamS 
kareṇum iva digdhena viddhāṃ mṛgayuṇā vane 
mahāgaja ivāraṇye snehāt parimamarśa tām  RamS 
parimṛśya ca pāṇibhyām abhisaṃtrastacetanaḥ 
kāmī kamalapattrākṣīm uvāca vanitām idam  RamS 
na te 'ham abhijānāmi krodham ātmani saṃśritam 
devi kenābhiyuktāsi kena vāsi vimānitā  RamS 
yad idaṃ mama duḥkhāya śeṣe kalyāṇi pāṃsuṣu 
bhūmau śeṣe kimarthaṃ tvaṃ mayi kalyāṇacetasi 
bhūtopahatacitteva mama cittapramāthinī  RamS 
santi me kuśalā vaidyā abhituṣṭāś ca sarvaśaḥ 
sukhitāṃ tvāṃ kariṣyanti vyādhim ācakṣva bhāmini  RamS 
kasya vā te priyaṃ kāryaṃ kena vā vipriyaṃ kṛtam 
kaḥ priyaṃ labhatām adya ko vā sumahad apriyam  RamS 
avadhyo vadhyatāṃ ko vā vadhyaḥ ko vā vimucyatām 
daridraḥ ko bhavatv āḍhyo dravyavān vāpy akiñcanaḥ  RamS 
ahaṃ caiva madīyāś ca sarve tava vaśānugāḥ 
na te kaṃcid abhiprāyaṃ vyāhantum aham utsahe  RamS 
ātmano jīvitenāpi brūhi yan manasecchasi 
yāvad āvartate cakraṃ tāvatī me vasuṃdharā  RamS 
tathoktā sā samāśvastā vaktukāmā tad apriyam 
paripīḍayituṃ bhūyo bhartāram upacakrame  RamS 
nāsmi viprakṛtā deva kenacin na vimānitā 
abhiprāyas tu me kaścit tam icchāmi tvayā kṛtam  RamS 
pratijñāṃ pratijānīṣva yadi tvaṃ kartum icchasi 
atha tad vyāhariṣyāmi yad abhiprārthitaṃ mayā  RamS 
evam uktas tayā rājā priyayā strīvaśaṃ gataḥ 
tām uvāca mahātejāḥ kaikeyīm īṣadutsmitaḥ  RamS 
avalipte na jānāsi tvattaḥ priyataro mama 
manujo manujavyāghrād rāmād anyo na vidyate  RamS 
bhadre hṛdayam apy etad anumṛśyoddharasva me 
etat samīkṣya kaikeyi brūhi yat sādhu manyase  RamS 
balam ātmani paśyantī na māṃ śaṅkitum arhasi 
kariṣyāmi tava prītiṃ sukṛtenāpi te śape  RamS 
tena vākyena saṃhṛṣṭā tam abhiprāyam ātmanaḥ 
vyājahāra mahāghoram abhyāgatam ivāntakam  RamS 
yathākrameṇa śapasi varaṃ mama dadāsi ca 
tac chṛṇvantu trayastriṃśad devāḥ sendrapurogamāḥ  RamS 
candrādityau nabhaś caiva grahā rātryahanī diśaḥ 
jagac ca pṛthivī caiva sagandharvā sarākṣasā  RamS 
niśācarāṇi bhūtāni gṛheṣu gṛhadevatāḥ 
yāni cānyāni bhūtāni jānīyur bhāṣitaṃ tava  RamS 
satyasaṃdho mahātejā dharmajñaḥ susamāhitaḥ 
varaṃ mama dadāty eṣa tan me śṛṇvantu devatāḥ  RamS 
iti devī maheṣvāsaṃ parigṛhyābhiśasya ca 
tataḥ param uvācedaṃ varadaṃ kāmamohitam  RamS 
varau yau me tvayā deva tadā dattau mahīpate 
tau tāvad aham adyaiva vakṣyāmi śṛṇu me vacaḥ  RamS 
abhiṣekasamārambho rāghavasyopakalpitaḥ 
anenaivābhiṣekeṇa bharato me 'bhiṣicyatām  RamS 
nava pañca ca varṣāṇi daṇḍakāraṇyam āśritaḥ 
cīrājinajaṭādhārī rāmo bhavatu tāpasaḥ  RamS 
bharato bhajatām adya yauvarājyam akaṇṭakam 
adya caiva hi paśyeyaṃ prayāntaṃ rāghavaṃ vane  RamS 
tataḥ śrutvā mahārāja kaikeyyā dāruṇaṃ vacaḥ 
vyathito vilavaś caiva vyāghrīṃ dṛṣṭvā yathā mṛgaḥ  RamS 
asaṃvṛtāyām āsīno jagatyāṃ dīrgham ucchvasan 
aho dhig iti sāmarṣo vācam uktvā narādhipaḥ 
moham āpedivān bhūyaḥ śokopahatacetanaḥ  RamS 
cireṇa tu nṛpaḥ saṃjñāṃ pratilabhya suduḥkhitaḥ 
kaikeyīm abravīt kruddhaḥ pradahann iva cakṣuṣā  RamS 
nṛśaṃse duṣṭacāritre kulasyāsya vināśini 
kiṃ kṛtaṃ tava rāmeṇa pāpe pāpaṃ mayāpi vā  RamS 
sadā te jananītulyāṃ vṛttiṃ vahati rāghavaḥ 
tasyaiva tvam anarthāya kiṃnimittam ihodyatā  RamS 
tvaṃ mayātmavināśāya bhavanaṃ svaṃ praveśitā 
avijñānān nṛpasutā vyālī tīkṣṇaviṣā yathā  RamS 
jīvaloko yadā sarvo rāmasyeha guṇastavam 
aparādhaṃ kam uddiśya tyakṣyāmīṣṭam ahaṃ sutam  RamS 
kausalyāṃ vā sumitrāṃ vā tyajeyam api vā śriyam 
jīvitaṃ vātmano rāmaṃ na tv eva pitṛvatsalam  RamS 
parā bhavati me prītir dṛṣṭvā tanayam agrajam 
apaśyatas tu me rāmaṃ naṣṭā bhavati cetanā  RamS 
tiṣṭhel loko vinā sūryaṃ sasyaṃ vā salilaṃ vinā 
na tu rāmaṃ vinā dehe tiṣṭhet tu mama jīvitam  RamS 
tad alaṃ tyajyatām eṣa niścayaḥ pāpaniścaye 
api te caraṇau mūrdhnā spṛśāmy eṣa prasīda me  RamS 
sa bhūmipālo vilapann anāthavat striyā gṛhīto hṛdaye 'timātrayā 
papāta devyāś caraṇau prasāritāv ubhāv asaṃspṛśya yathāturas tathā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
atadarhaṃ mahārājaṃ śayānam atathocitam 
yayātim iva puṇyānte devalokāt paricyutam  RamS 
anartharūpā siddhārthā abhītā bhayadarśinī 
punar ākārayāmāsa tam eva varam aṅganā  RamS 
tvaṃ katthase mahārāja satyavādī dṛḍhavrataḥ 
mama cemaṃ varaṃ kasmād vidhārayitum icchasi  RamS 
evam uktas tu kaikeyyā rājā daśarathas tadā 
pratyuvāca tataḥ kruddho muhūrtaṃ vihvalann iva  RamS 
mṛte mayi gate rāme vanaṃ manujapuṃgave 
hantānārye mamāmitre rāmaḥ pravrājito vanam  RamS 
yadi satyaṃ bravīmy etat tad asatyaṃ bhaviṣyati 
akīrtir atulā loke dhruvaṃ paribhavaś ca me  RamS 
tathā vilapatas tasya paribhramitacetasaḥ 
astam abhyagamat sūryo rajanī cābhyavartata  RamS 
sa triyāmā tathārtasya candramaṇḍalamaṇḍitā 
rājño vilapamānasya na vyabhāsata śarvarī  RamS 
tathaivoṣṇaṃ viniḥśvasya vṛddho daśaratho nṛpaḥ 
vilalāpārtavad duḥkhaṃ gaganāsaktalocanaḥ  RamS 
na prabhātaṃ tvayecchāmi mayāyaṃ racito 'ñjaliḥ 
atha vā gamyatāṃ śīghraṃ nāham icchāmi nirghṛṇām 
nṛśaṃsāṃ kaikeyīṃ draṣṭuṃ yatkṛte vyasanaṃ mahat  RamS 
evam uktvā tato rājā kaikeyīṃ saṃyatāñjaliḥ 
prasādayāmāsa punaḥ kaikeyīṃ cedam abravīt  RamS 
sādhuvṛttasya dīnasya tvadgatasya gatāyuṣaḥ 
prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ devi bhadre rājño viśeṣataḥ  RamS 
śūnyena khalu suśroṇi mayedaṃ samudāhṛtam 
kuru sādhu prasādaṃ me bāle sahṛdayā hy asi  RamS 
viśuddhabhāvasya hi duṣṭabhāvā tāmrekṣaṇasyāśrukalasya rājñaḥ 
śrutvā vicitraṃ karuṇaṃ vilāpaṃ bhartur nṛśaṃsā na cakāra vākyam  RamS 
tataḥ sa rājā punar eva mūrchitaḥ priyām atuṣṭāṃ pratikūlabhāṣiṇīm 
samīkṣya putrasya vivāsanaṃ prati kṣitau visaṃjño nipapāta duḥkhitaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
putraśokārditaṃ pāpā visaṃjñaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi 
viveṣṭamānam udīkṣya saikṣvākam idam abravīt  RamS 
pāpaṃ kṛtveva kim idaṃ mama saṃśrutya saṃśravam 
śeṣe kṣititale sannaḥ sthityāṃ sthātuṃ tvam arhasi  RamS 
āhuḥ satyaṃ hi paramaṃ dharmaṃ dharmavido janāḥ 
satyam āśritya hi mayā tvaṃ ca dharmaṃ pracoditaḥ  RamS 
saṃśrutya śaibyaḥ śyenāya svāṃ tanuṃ jagatīpatiḥ 
pradāya pakṣiṇo rājañ jagāma gatim uttamām  RamS 
tathā hy alarkas tejasvī brāhmaṇe vedapārage 
yācamāne svake netre uddhṛtyāvimanā dadau  RamS 
saritāṃ tu patiḥ svalpāṃ maryādāṃ satyam anvitaḥ 
satyānurodhāt samaye velāṃ svāṃ nātivartate  RamS 
samayaṃ ca mamāryemaṃ yadi tvaṃ na kariṣyasi 
agratas te parityaktā parityakṣyāmi jīvitam  RamS 
evaṃ pracodito rājā kaikeyyā nirviśaṅkayā 
nāśakat pāśam unmoktuṃ balir indrakṛtaṃ yathā  RamS 
udbhrāntahṛdayaś cāpi vivarṇavadano 'bhavat 
sa dhuryo vai parispandan yugacakrāntaraṃ yathā  RamS 
vihvalābhyāṃ ca netrābhyām apaśyann iva bhūmipaḥ 
kṛcchrād dhairyeṇa saṃstabhya kaikeyīm idam abravīt  RamS 
yas te mantrakṛtaḥ pāṇir agnau pāpe mayā dhṛtaḥ 
taṃ tyajāmi svajaṃ caiva tava putraṃ saha tvayā  RamS 
tataḥ pāpasamācārā kaikeyī pārthivaṃ punaḥ 
uvāca paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ vākyajñā roṣamūrchitā  RamS 
kim idaṃ bhāṣase rājan vākyaṃ gararujopamam 
ānāyayitum akliṣṭaṃ putraṃ rāmam ihārhasi  RamS 
sthāpya rājye mama sutaṃ kṛtvā rāmaṃ vanecaram 
niḥsapatnāṃ ca māṃ kṛtvā kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasi  RamS 
sa nunna iva tīkṣṇeṇa pratodena hayottamaḥ 
rājā pracodito 'bhīkṣṇaṃ kaikeyīm idam abravīt  RamS 
dharmabandhena baddho 'smi naṣṭā ca mama cetanā 
jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ priyaṃ rāmaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi dhārmikam  RamS 
iti rājño vacaḥ śrutvā kaikeyī tadanantaram 
svayam evābravīt sūtaṃ gaccha tvaṃ rāmam ānaya  RamS 
tataḥ sa rājā taṃ sūtaṃ sannaharṣaḥ sutaṃ prati 
śokāraktekṣaṇaḥ śrīmān udvīkṣyovāca dhārmikaḥ  RamS 
sumantraḥ karuṇaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā dīnaṃ ca pārthivam 
pragṛhītāñjaliḥ kiṃcit tasmād deśād apākraman  RamS 
yadā vaktuṃ svayaṃ dainyān na śaśāka mahīpatiḥ 
tadā sumantraṃ mantrajñā kaikeyī pratyuvāca ha  RamS 
sumantra rāmaṃ drakṣyāmi śīghram ānaya sundaram 
sa manyamānaḥ kalyāṇaṃ hṛdayena nananda ca  RamS 
sumantraś cintayāmāsa tvaritaṃ coditas tayā 
vyaktaṃ rāmo 'bhiṣekārtham ihāyāsyati dharmavit  RamS 
iti sūto matiṃ kṛtvā harṣeṇa mahatā punaḥ 
nirjagāma mahātejā rāghavasya didṛkṣayā  RamS 
tataḥ purastāt sahasā vinirgato mahīpatīn dvāragatān vilokayan 
dadarśa paurān vividhān mahādhanān upasthitān dvāram upetya viṣṭhitān  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
te tu tāṃ rajanīm uṣya brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ 
upatasthur upasthānaṃ saharājapurohitāḥ  RamS 
amātyā balamukhyāś ca mukhyā ye nigamasya ca 
rāghavasyābhiṣekārthe prīyamāṇās tu saṃgatāḥ  RamS 
udite vimale sūrye puṣye cābhyāgate 'hani 
abhiṣekāya rāmasya dvijendrair upakalpitam  RamS 
kāñcanā jalakumbhāś ca bhadrapīṭhaṃ svalaṃkṛtam 
rāmaś ca samyagāstīrṇo bhāsvatā vyāghracarmaṇā  RamS 
gaṅgāyamunayoḥ puṇyāt saṃgamād āhṛtaṃ jalam 
yāś cānyāḥ saritaḥ puṇyā hradāḥ kūpāḥ sarāṃsi ca  RamS 
prāgvāhāś cordhvavāhāś ca tiryagvāhāḥ samāhitāḥ 
tābhyaś caivāhṛtaṃ toyaṃ samudrebhyaś ca sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
kṣaudraṃ dadhighṛtaṃ lājā darbhāḥ sumanasaḥ payaḥ 
salājāḥ kṣīribhiś channā ghaṭāḥ kāñcanarājatāḥ 
padmotpalayutā bhānti pūrṇāḥ paramavāriṇā  RamS 
candrāṃśuvikacaprakhyaṃ pāṇḍuraṃ ratnabhūṣitam 
sajjaṃ tiṣṭhati rāmasya vālavyajanam uttamam  RamS 
candramaṇḍalasaṃkāśam ātapatraṃ ca pāṇḍuram 
sajjaṃ dyutikaraṃ śrīmad abhiṣekapuraskṛtam  RamS 
pāṇḍuraś ca vṛṣaḥ sajjaḥ pāṇḍurāśvaś ca susthitaḥ 
prasrutaś ca gajaḥ śrīmān aupavāhyaḥ pratīkṣate  RamS 
aṣṭau kanyāś ca maṅgalyāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ 
vāditrāṇi ca sarvāṇi bandinaś ca tathāpare  RamS 
ikṣvākūṇāṃ yathā rājye saṃbhriyetābhiṣecanam 
tathā jātīyam ādāya rājaputrābhiṣecanam  RamS 
te rājavacanāt tatra samavetā mahīpatim 
apaśyanto 'bruvan ko nu rājño naḥ prativedayet  RamS 
na paśyāmaś ca rājānam uditaś ca divākaraḥ 
yauvarājyābhiṣekaś ca sajjo rāmasya dhīmataḥ  RamS 
iti teṣu bruvāṇeṣu sārvabhaumān mahīpatīn 
abravīt tān idaṃ sarvān sumantro rājasatkṛtaḥ  RamS 
ayaṃ pṛcchāmi vacanāt sukham āyuṣmatām aham 
rājñaḥ saṃpratibuddhasya yac cāgamanakāraṇam  RamS 
ity uktvāntaḥpuradvāram ājagāma purāṇavit 
āśirbhir guṇayuktābhir abhituṣṭāva rāghavam  RamS 
gatā bhagavatī rātrirahaḥ śivam upasthitam 
budhyasva nṛpaśārdūla kuru kāryam anantaram  RamS 
brāhmaṇā balamukhyāś ca naigamāś cāgatā nṛpa 
darśanaṃ pratikāṅkṣante pratibudhyasva rāghava  RamS 
stuvantaṃ taṃ tadā sūtaṃ sumantraṃ mantrakovidam 
pratibudhya tato rājā idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
na caiva saṃprasupto 'ham ānayed āśu rāghavam 
iti rājā daśarathaḥ sūtaṃ tatrānvaśāt punaḥ  RamS 
sa rājavacanaṃ śrutvā śirasā pratipūjya tam 
nirjagāma nṛpāvāsān manyamānaḥ priyaṃ mahat  RamS 
prapanno rājamārgaṃ ca patākādhvajaśobhitam 
sa sūtas tatra śuśrāva rāmādhikaraṇāḥ kathāḥ  RamS 
tato dadarśa ruciraṃ kailāsasadṛśaprabham 
rāmaveśma sumantras tu śakraveśmasamaprabham  RamS 
mahākapāṭapihitaṃ vitardiśataśobhitam 
kāñcanapratimaikāgraṃ maṇividrumatoraṇam  RamS 
śāradābhraghanaprakhyaṃ dīptaṃ meruguhopamam 
dāmabhir varamālyānāṃ sumahadbhir alaṃkṛtam  RamS 
sa vājiyuktena rathena sārathir narākulaṃ rājakulaṃ vilokayan 
tataḥ samāsādya mahādhanaṃ mahat prahṛṣṭaromā sa babhūva sārathiḥ  RamS 
tad adrikūṭācalameghasaṃnibhaṃ mahāvimānottamaveśmasaṃghavat 
avāryamāṇaḥ praviveśa sārathiḥ prabhūtaratnaṃ makaro yathārṇavam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
sa tadantaḥpuradvāraṃ samatītya janākulam 
praviviktāṃ tataḥ kakṣyām āsasāda purāṇavit  RamS 
prāsakārmukabibhradbhir yuvabhir mṛṣṭakuṇḍalaiḥ 
apramādibhir ekāgraiḥ svanuraktair adhiṣṭhitām  RamS 
tatra kāṣāyiṇo vṛddhān vetrapāṇīn svalaṃkṛtān 
dadarśa viṣṭhitān dvāri stryadhyakṣān susamāhitān  RamS 
te samīkṣya samāyāntaṃ rāmapriyacikīrṣavaḥ 
sahabhāryāya rāmāya kṣipram evācacakṣire  RamS 
prativeditam ājñāya sūtam abhyantaraṃ pituḥ 
tatraivānāyayāmāsa rāghavaḥ priyakāmyayā  RamS 
taṃ vaiśravaṇasaṃkāśam upaviṣṭaṃ svalaṃkṛtam 
dadarśa sūtaḥ paryaṅke sauvarṇe sottaracchade  RamS 
varāharudhirābheṇa śucinā ca sugandhinā 
anuliptaṃ parārdhyena candanena paraṃtapam  RamS 
sthitayā pārśvataś cāpi vālavyajanahastayā 
upetaṃ sītayā bhūyaś citrayā śaśinaṃ yathā  RamS 
taṃ tapantam ivādityam upapannaṃ svatejasā 
vavande varadaṃ bandī niyamajño vinītavat  RamS 
prāñjalis tu sukhaṃ pṛṣṭvā vihāraśayanāsane 
rājaputram uvācedaṃ sumantro rājasatkṛtaḥ  RamS 
kausalyā suprabhā deva pitā tvāṃ draṣṭum icchati 
mahiṣyā saha kaikeyyā gamyatāṃ tatra māciram  RamS 
evam uktas tu saṃhṛṣṭo narasiṃho mahādyutiḥ 
tataḥ saṃmānayāmāsa sītām idam uvāca ha  RamS 
devi devaś ca devī ca samāgamya madantare 
mantrayete dhruvaṃ kiṃcid abhiṣecanasaṃhitam  RamS 
lakṣayitvā hy abhiprāyaṃ priyakāmā sudakṣiṇā 
saṃcodayati rājānaṃ madarthaṃ madirekṣaṇā  RamS 
yādṛśī pariṣat tatra tādṛśo dūta āgataḥ 
dhruvam adyaiva māṃ rājā yauvarājye 'bhiṣekṣyati  RamS 
hanta śīghram ito gatvā drakṣyāmi ca mahīpatim 
saha tvaṃ parivāreṇa sukham āsva ramasva ca  RamS 
patisaṃmānitā sītā bhartāram asitekṣaṇā 
ādvāram anuvavrāja maṅgalāny abhidadhyuṣī  RamS 
sa sarvān arthino dṛṣṭvā sametya pratinandya ca 
tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśam āruroha rathottamam  RamS 
muṣṇantam iva cakṣūṃṣi prabhayā hemavarcasam 
kareṇuśiśukalpaiś ca yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ  RamS 
hariyuktaṃ sahasrākṣo ratham indra ivāśugam 
prayayau tūrṇam āsthāya rāghavo jvalitaḥ śriyā  RamS 
sa parjanya ivākāśe svanavān abhinādayan 
niketān niryayau śrīmān mahābhrād iva candramāḥ  RamS 
chattracāmarapāṇis tu lakṣmaṇo rāghavānujaḥ 
jugopa bhrātaraṃ bhrātā ratham āsthāya pṛṣṭhataḥ  RamS 
tato halahalāśabdas tumulaḥ samajāyata 
tasya niṣkramamāṇasya janaughasya samantataḥ  RamS 
sa rāghavas tatra kathāpralāpaṃ śuśrāva lokasya samāgatasya 
ātmādhikārā vividhāś ca vācaḥ prahṛṣṭarūpasya pure janasya  RamS 
eṣa śriyaṃ gacchati rāghavo 'dya rājaprasādād vipulāṅgam iṣyan 
ete vayaṃ sarvasamṛddhakāmā yeṣām ayaṃ no bhavitā praśāstā 
lābho janasyāsya yad eṣa sarvaṃ prapatsyate rāṣṭram idaṃ cirāya  RamS 
sa ghoṣavadbhiś ca hayaiḥ sanāgaiḥ puraḥsaraiḥ svastikasūtamāgadhaiḥ 
mahīyamānaḥ pravaraiś ca vādakair abhiṣṭuto vaiśravaṇo yathā yayau  RamS 
kareṇumātaṃgarathāśvasaṃkulaṃ mahājanaughaiḥ paripūrṇacatvaram 
prabhūtaratnaṃ bahupaṇyasaṃcayaṃ dadarśa rāmo ruciraṃ mahāpatham  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
sa rāmo ratham āsthāya samprahṛṣṭasuhṛjjanaḥ 
apaśyan nagaraṃ śrīmān nānājanasamākulam  RamS 
sa gṛhair abhrasaṃkāśaiḥ pāṇḍurair upaśobhitam 
rājamārgaṃ yayau rāmo madhyenāgarudhūpitam  RamS 
śobhamānam asaṃbādhaṃ taṃ rājapatham uttamam 
saṃvṛtaṃ vividhaiḥ paṇyair bhakṣyair uccāvacair api  RamS 
āśīrvādān bahūñ śṛṇvan suhṛdbhiḥ samudīritān 
yathārhaṃ cāpi sampūjya sarvān eva narān yayau  RamS 
pitāmahair ācaritaṃ tathaiva prapitāmahaiḥ 
adyopādāya taṃ mārgam abhiṣikto 'nupālaya  RamS 
yathā sma lālitāḥ pitrā yathā pūrvaiḥ pitāmahaiḥ 
tataḥ sukhataraṃ sarve rāme vatsyāma rājani  RamS 
alam adya hi bhuktena paramārthair alaṃ ca naḥ 
yathā paśyāma niryāntaṃ rāmaṃ rājye pratiṣṭhitam  RamS 
ato hi na priyataraṃ nānyat kiṃcid bhaviṣyati 
yathābhiṣeko rāmasya rājyenāmitatejasaḥ  RamS 
etāś cānyāś ca suhṛdām udāsīnaḥ kathāḥ śubhāḥ 
ātmasaṃpūjanīḥ śṛṇvan yayau rāmo mahāpatham  RamS 
na hi tasmān manaḥ kaścic cakṣuṣī vā narottamāt 
naraḥ śaknoty apākraṣṭum atikrānte 'pi rāghave  RamS 
sarveṣāṃ sa hi dharmātmā varṇānāṃ kurute dayām 
caturṇāṃ hi vayaḥsthānāṃ tena te tam anuvratāḥ  RamS 
sa rājakulam āsādya mahendrabhavanopamam 
rājaputraḥ pitur veśma praviveśa śriyā jvalan  RamS 
sa sarvāḥ samatikramya kakṣyā daśarathātmajaḥ 
saṃnivartya janaṃ sarvaṃ śuddhāntaḥpuram abhyagāt  RamS 
tataḥ praviṣṭe pitur antikaṃ tadā janaḥ sa sarvo mudito nṛpātmaje 
pratīkṣate tasya punaḥ sma nirgamaṃ yathodayaṃ candramasaḥ saritpatiḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
sa dadarśāsane rāmo niṣaṇṇaṃ pitaraṃ śubhe 
kaikeyīsahitaṃ dīnaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā  RamS 
sa pituś caraṇau pūrvam abhivādya vinītavat 
tato vavande caraṇau kaikeyyāḥ susamāhitaḥ  RamS 
rāmety uktvā ca vacanaṃ bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ 
śaśāka nṛpatir dīno nekṣituṃ nābhibhāṣitum  RamS 
tad apūrvaṃ narapater dṛṣṭvā rūpaṃ bhayāvaham 
rāmo 'pi bhayam āpannaḥ padā spṛṣṭveva pannagam  RamS 
indriyair aprahṛṣṭais taṃ śokasaṃtāpakarśitam 
niḥśvasantaṃ mahārājaṃ vyathitākulacetasam  RamS 
ūrmimālinam akṣobhyaṃ kṣubhyantam iva sāgaram 
upaplutam ivādityam uktānṛtam ṛṣiṃ yathā  RamS 
acintyakalpaṃ hi pitus taṃ śokam upadhārayan 
babhūva saṃrabdhataraḥ samudra iva parvaṇi  RamS 
cintayāmāsa ca tadā rāmaḥ pitṛhite rataḥ 
kiṃsvid adyaiva nṛpatir na māṃ pratyabhinandati  RamS 
anyadā māṃ pitā dṛṣṭvā kupito 'pi prasīdati 
tasya mām adya samprekṣya kimāyāsaḥ pravartate  RamS 
sa dīna iva śokārto viṣaṇṇavadanadyutiḥ 
kaikeyīm abhivādyaiva rāmo vacanam abravīt  RamS 
kaccin mayā nāparādham ajñānād yena me pitā 
kupitas tan mamācakṣva tvaṃ caivainaṃ prasādaya  RamS 
vivarṇavadano dīno na hi mām abhibhāṣate 
śārīro mānaso vāpi kaccid enaṃ na bādhate 
saṃtāpo vābhitāpo vā durlabhaṃ hi sadā sukham  RamS 
kaccin na kiṃcid bharate kumāre priyadarśane 
śatrughne vā mahāsattve mātḥṇāṃ vā mamāśubham  RamS 
atoṣayan mahārājam akurvan vā pitur vacaḥ 
muhūrtam api neccheyaṃ jīvituṃ kupite nṛpe  RamS 
yatomūlaṃ naraḥ paśyet prādurbhāvam ihātmanaḥ 
kathaṃ tasmin na varteta pratyakṣe sati daivate  RamS 
kaccit te paruṣaṃ kiṃcid abhimānāt pitā mama 
ukto bhavatyā kopena yatrāsya lulitaṃ manaḥ  RamS 
etad ācakṣva me devi tattvena paripṛcchataḥ 
kiṃnimittam apūrvo 'yaṃ vikāro manujādhipe  RamS 
ahaṃ hi vacanād rājñaḥ pateyam api pāvake 
bhakṣayeyaṃ viṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ majjeyam api cārṇave 
niyukto guruṇā pitrā nṛpeṇa ca hitena ca  RamS 
tad brūhi vacanaṃ devi rājño yad abhikāṅkṣitam 
kariṣye pratijāne ca rāmo dvir nābhibhāṣate  RamS 
tam ārjavasamāyuktam anāryā satyavādinam 
uvāca rāmaṃ kaikeyī vacanaṃ bhṛśadāruṇam  RamS 
purā devāsure yuddhe pitrā te mama rāghava 
rakṣitena varau dattau saśalyena mahāraṇe  RamS 
tatra me yācito rājā bharatasyābhiṣecanam 
gamanaṃ daṇḍakāraṇye tava cādyaiva rāghava  RamS 
yadi satyapratijñaṃ tvaṃ pitaraṃ kartum icchasi 
ātmānaṃ ca naraśreṣṭha mama vākyam idaṃ śṛṇu  RamS 
sa nideśe pitus tiṣṭha yathā tena pratiśrutam 
tvayāraṇyaṃ praveṣṭavyaṃ nava varṣāṇi pañca ca  RamS 
sapta sapta ca varṣāṇi daṇḍakāraṇyam āśritaḥ 
abhiṣekam imaṃ tyaktvā jaṭācīradharo vasa  RamS 
bharataḥ kosalapure praśāstu vasudhām imām 
nānāratnasamākīrṇāṃ savājirathakuñjarām  RamS 
tad apriyam amitraghno vacanaṃ maraṇopamam 
śrutvā na vivyathe rāmaḥ kaikeyīṃ cedam abravīt  RamS 
evam astu gamiṣyāmi vanaṃ vastum ahaṃ tv ataḥ 
jaṭācīradharo rājñaḥ pratijñām anupālayan  RamS 
idaṃ tu jñātum icchāmi kimarthaṃ māṃ mahīpatiḥ 
nābhinandati durdharṣo yathāpuram ariṃdamaḥ  RamS 
manyur na ca tvayā kāryo devi brūhi tavāgrataḥ 
yāsyāmi bhava suprītā vanaṃ cīrajaṭādharaḥ  RamS 
hitena guruṇā pitrā kṛtajñena nṛpeṇa ca 
niyujyamāno viśrabdhaṃ kiṃ na kuryād ahaṃ priyam  RamS 
alīkaṃ mānasaṃ tv ekaṃ hṛdayaṃ dahatīva me 
svayaṃ yan nāha māṃ rājā bharatasyābhiṣecanam  RamS 
ahaṃ hi sītāṃ rājyaṃ ca prāṇān iṣṭān dhanāni ca 
hṛṣṭo bhrātre svayaṃ dadyāṃ bharatāyāpracoditaḥ  RamS 
kiṃ punar manujendreṇa svayaṃ pitrā pracoditaḥ 
tava ca priyakāmārthaṃ pratijñām anupālayan  RamS 
tad āśvāsaya hīmaṃ tvaṃ kiṃ nv idaṃ yan mahīpatiḥ 
vasudhāsaktanayano mandam aśrūṇi muñcati  RamS 
gacchantu caivānayituṃ dūtāḥ śīghrajavair hayaiḥ 
bharataṃ mātulakulād adyaiva nṛpaśāsanāt  RamS 
daṇḍakāraṇyam eṣo 'ham ito gacchāmi satvaraḥ 
avicārya pitur vākyaṃ samāvastuṃ caturdaśa  RamS 
sā hṛṣṭā tasya tadvākyaṃ śrutvā rāmasya kaikeyī 
prasthānaṃ śraddadhānā hi tvarayāmāsa rāghavam  RamS 
evaṃ bhavatu yāsyanti dūtāḥ śīghrajavair hayaiḥ 
bharataṃ mātulakulād upāvartayituṃ narāḥ  RamS 
tava tv ahaṃ kṣamaṃ manye notsukasya vilambanam 
rāma tasmād itaḥ śīghraṃ vanaṃ tvaṃ gantum arhasi  RamS 
vrīḍānvitaḥ svayaṃ yac ca nṛpas tvāṃ nābhibhāṣate 
naitat kiṃcin naraśreṣṭha manyur eṣo 'panīyatām  RamS 
yāvat tvaṃ na vanaṃ yātaḥ purād asmād abhitvaran 
pitā tāvan na te rāma snāsyate bhokṣyate 'pi vā  RamS 
dhik kaṣṭam iti niḥśvasya rājā śokapariplutaḥ 
mūrchito nyapatat tasmin paryaṅke hemabhūṣite  RamS 
rāmo 'py utthāpya rājānaṃ kaikeyyābhipracoditaḥ 
kaśayevāhato vājī vanaṃ gantuṃ kṛtatvaraḥ  RamS 
tad apriyam anāryāyā vacanaṃ dāruṇodaram 
śrutvā gatavyatho rāmaḥ kaikeyīṃ vākyam abravīt  RamS 
nāham arthaparo devi lokam āvastum utsahe 
viddhi mām ṛṣibhis tulyaṃ kevalaṃ dharmam āsthitam  RamS 
yad atrabhavataḥ kiṃcic chakyaṃ kartuṃ priyaṃ mayā 
prāṇān api parityajya sarvathā kṛtam eva tat  RamS 
na hy ato dharmacaraṇaṃ kiṃcid asti mahattaram 
yathā pitari śuśrūṣā tasya vā vacanakriyā  RamS 
anukto 'py atrabhavatā bhavatyā vacanād aham 
vane vatsyāmi vijane varṣāṇīha caturdaśa  RamS 
na nūnaṃ mayi kaikeyi kiṃcid āśaṃsase guṇam 
yad rājānam avocas tvaṃ mameśvaratarā satī  RamS 
yāvan mātaram āpṛcche sītāṃ cānunayāmy aham 
tato 'dyaiva gamiṣyāmi daṇḍakānāṃ mahad vanam  RamS 
bharataḥ pālayed rājyaṃ śuśrūṣec ca pitur yathā 
tathā bhavatyā kartavyaṃ sa hi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ  RamS 
sa rāmasya vacaḥ śrutvā bhṛśaṃ duḥkhahataḥ pitā 
śokād aśaknuvan bāṣpaṃ praruroda mahāsvanam  RamS 
vanditvā caraṇau rāmo visaṃjñasya pitus tadā 
kaikeyyāś cāpy anāryāyā niṣpapāta mahādyutiḥ  RamS 
sa rāmaḥ pitaraṃ kṛtvā kaikeyīṃ ca pradakṣiṇam 
niṣkramyāntaḥpurāt tasmāt svaṃ dadarśa suhṛjjanam  RamS 
taṃ bāṣpaparipūrṇākṣaḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nujagāma ha 
lakṣmaṇaḥ paramakruddhaḥ sumitrānandavardhanaḥ  RamS 
ābhiṣecanikaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ kṛtvā rāmaḥ pradakṣiṇam 
śanair jagāma sāpekṣo dṛṣṭiṃ tatrāvicālayan  RamS 
na cāsya mahatīṃ lakṣmīṃ rājyanāśo 'pakarṣati 
lokakāntasya kāntatvaṃ śītaraśmer iva kṣapā  RamS 
na vanaṃ gantukāmasya tyajataś ca vasuṃdharām 
sarvalokātigasyeva lakṣyate cittavikriyā  RamS 
dhārayan manasā duḥkham indriyāṇi nigṛhya ca 
praviveśātmavān veśma mātur apriyaśaṃsivān  RamS 
praviśya veśmātibhṛśaṃ mudānvitaṃ samīkṣya tāṃ cārthavipattim āgatām 
na caiva rāmo 'tra jagāma vikriyāṃ suhṛjjanasyātmavipattiśaṅkayā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
rāmas tu bhṛśam āyasto niḥśvasann iva kuñjaraḥ 
jagāma sahito bhrātrā mātur antaḥpuraṃ vaśī  RamS 
so 'paśyat puruṣaṃ tatra vṛddhaṃ paramapūjitam 
upaviṣṭaṃ gṛhadvāri tiṣṭhataś cāparān bahūn  RamS 
praviśya prathamāṃ kakṣyāṃ dvitīyāyāṃ dadarśa saḥ 
brāhmaṇān vedasampannān vṛddhān rājñābhisatkṛtān  RamS 
praṇamya rāmas tān vṛddhāṃs tṛtīyāyāṃ dadarśa saḥ 
striyo vṛddhāś ca bālāś ca dvārarakṣaṇatatparāḥ  RamS 
vardhayitvā prahṛṣṭās tāḥ praviśya ca gṛhaṃ striyaḥ 
nyavedayanta tvaritā rāmamātuḥ priyaṃ tadā  RamS 
kausalyāpi tadā devī rātriṃ sthitvā samāhitā 
prabhāte tv akarot pūjāṃ viṣṇoḥ putrahitaiṣiṇī  RamS 
sā kṣaumavasanā hṛṣṭā nityaṃ vrataparāyaṇā 
agniṃ juhoti sma tadā mantravat kṛtamaṅgalā  RamS 
praviśya ca tadā rāmo mātur antaḥpuraṃ śubham 
dadarśa mātaraṃ tatra hāvayantīṃ hutāśanam  RamS 
sā cirasyātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā mātṛnandanam āgatam 
abhicakrāma saṃhṛṣṭā kiśoraṃ vaḍabā yathā  RamS 
tam uvāca durādharṣaṃ rāghavaṃ sutam ātmanaḥ 
kausalyā putravātsalyād idaṃ priyahitaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
vṛddhānāṃ dharmaśīlānāṃ rājarṣīṇāṃ mahātmanām 
prāpnuhy āyuś ca kīrtiṃ ca dharmaṃ copahitaṃ kule  RamS 
satyapratijñaṃ pitaraṃ rājānaṃ paśya rāghava 
adyaiva hi tvāṃ dharmātmā yauvarājye 'bhiṣekṣyati  RamS 
mātaraṃ rāghavaḥ kiṃcit prasāryāñjalim abravīt 
sa svabhāvavinītaś ca gauravāc ca tadānataḥ  RamS 
devi nūnaṃ na jānīṣe mahad bhayam upasthitam 
idaṃ tava ca duḥkhāya vaidehyā lakṣmaṇasya ca  RamS 
caturdaśa hi varṣāṇi vatsyāmi vijane vane 
madhumūlaphalair jīvan hitvā munivad āmiṣam  RamS 
bharatāya mahārājo yauvarājyaṃ prayacchati 
māṃ punar daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ vivāsayati tāpasam  RamS 
tām aduḥkhocitāṃ dṛṣṭvā patitāṃ kadalīm iva 
rāmas tūtthāpayāmāsa mātaraṃ gatacetasam  RamS 
upāvṛtyotthitāṃ dīnāṃ vaḍabām iva vāhitām 
pāṃśuguṇṭhitasarvāṅgīṃ vimamarśa ca pāṇinā  RamS 
sā rāghavam upāsīnam asukhārtā sukhocitā 
uvāca puruṣavyāghram upaśṛṇvati lakṣmaṇe  RamS 
yadi putra na jāyethā mama śokāya rāghava 
na sma duḥkham ato bhūyaḥ paśyeyam aham aprajā  RamS 
eka eva hi vandhyāyāḥ śoko bhavati mānavaḥ 
aprajāsmīti saṃtāpo na hy anyaḥ putra vidyate  RamS 
na dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ kalyāṇaṃ sukhaṃ vā patipauruṣe 
api putre vipaśyeyam iti rāmāsthitaṃ mayā  RamS 
sā bahūny amanojñāni vākyāni hṛdayacchidām 
ahaṃ śroṣye sapatnīnām avarāṇāṃ varā satī 
ato duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ nu pramadānāṃ bhaviṣyati  RamS 
tvayi saṃnihite 'py evam aham āsaṃ nirākṛtā 
kiṃ punaḥ proṣite tāta dhruvaṃ maraṇam eva me  RamS 
yo hi māṃ sevate kaścid atha vāpy anuvartate 
kaikeyyāḥ putram anvīkṣya sa jano nābhibhāṣate  RamS 
daśa sapta ca varṣāṇi tava jātasya rāghava 
atītāni prakāṅkṣantyā mayā duḥkhaparikṣayam  RamS 
upavāsaiś ca yogaiś ca bahubhiś ca pariśramaiḥ 
duḥkhaṃ saṃvardhito moghaṃ tvaṃ hi durgatayā mayā  RamS 
sthiraṃ tu hṛdayaṃ manye mamedaṃ yan na dīryate 
prāvṛṣīva mahānadyāḥ spṛṣṭaṃ kūlaṃ navāmbhasā  RamS 
mamaiva nūnaṃ maraṇaṃ na vidyate na cāvakāśo 'sti yamakṣaye mama 
yad antako 'dyaiva na māṃ jihīrṣati prasahya siṃho rudatīṃ mṛgīm iva  RamS 
sthiraṃ hi nūnaṃ hṛdayaṃ mamāyasaṃ na bhidyate yad bhuvi nāvadīryate 
anena duḥkhena ca deham arpitaṃ dhruvaṃ hy akāle maraṇaṃ na vidyate  RamS 
idaṃ tu duḥkhaṃ yad anarthakāni me vratāni dānāni ca saṃyamāś ca hi 
tapaś ca taptaṃ yad apatyakāraṇāt suniṣphalaṃ bījam ivoptam ūṣare  RamS 
yadi hy akāle maraṇaṃ svayecchayā labheta kaścid guruduḥkhakarśitaḥ 
gatāham adyaiva paretasaṃsadaṃ vinā tvayā dhenur ivātmajena vai  RamS 
bhṛśam asukham amarṣitā tadā bahu vilalāpa samīkṣya rāghavam 
vyasanam upaniśāmya sā mahat sutam iva baddham avekṣya kiṃnarī  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tathā tu vilapantīṃ tāṃ kausalyāṃ rāmamātaram 
uvāca lakṣmaṇo dīnas tat kālasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
na rocate mamāpy etad ārye yad rāghavo vanam 
tyaktvā rājyaśriyaṃ gacchet striyā vākyavaśaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
viparītaś ca vṛddhaś ca viṣayaiś ca pradharṣitaḥ 
nṛpaḥ kim iva na brūyāc codyamānaḥ samanmathaḥ  RamS 
nāsyāparādhaṃ paśyāmi nāpi doṣaṃ tathāvidham 
yena nirvāsyate rāṣṭrād vanavāsāya rāghavaḥ  RamS 
na taṃ paśyāmy ahaṃ loke parokṣam api yo naraḥ 
amitro 'pi nirasto 'pi yo 'sya doṣam udāharet  RamS 
devakalpam ṛjuṃ dāntaṃ ripūṇām api vatsalam 
avekṣamāṇaḥ ko dharmaṃ tyajet putram akāraṇāt  RamS 
tad idaṃ vacanaṃ rājñaḥ punar bālyam upeyuṣaḥ 
putraḥ ko hṛdaye kuryād rājavṛttam anusmaran  RamS 
yāvad eva na jānāti kaścid artham imaṃ naraḥ 
tāvad eva mayā sārdham ātmasthaṃ kuru śāsanam  RamS 
mayā pārśve sadhanuṣā tava guptasya rāghava 
kaḥ samartho 'dhikaṃ kartuṃ kṛtāntasyeva tiṣṭhataḥ  RamS 
nirmanuṣyām imāṃ sarvām ayodhyāṃ manujarṣabha 
kariṣyāmi śarais tīkṣṇair yadi sthāsyati vipriye  RamS 
bharatasyātha pakṣyo vā yo vāsya hitam icchati 
sarvān etān vadhiṣyāmi mṛdur hi paribhūyate  RamS 
tvayā caiva mayā caiva kṛtvā vairam anuttamam 
kasya śaktiḥ śriyaṃ dātuṃ bharatāyāriśāsana  RamS 
anurakto 'smi bhāvena bhrātaraṃ devi tattvataḥ 
satyena dhanuṣā caiva datteneṣṭena te śape  RamS 
dīptam agnim araṇyaṃ vā yadi rāmaḥ pravekṣyate 
praviṣṭaṃ tatra māṃ devi tvaṃ pūrvam avadhāraya  RamS 
harāmi vīryād duḥkhaṃ te tamaḥ sūrya ivoditaḥ 
devī paśyatu me vīryaṃ rāghavaś caiva paśyatu  RamS 
etat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā lakṣmaṇasya mahātmanaḥ 
uvāca rāmaṃ kausalyā rudantī śokalālasā  RamS 
bhrātus te vadataḥ putra lakṣmaṇasya śrutaṃ tvayā 
yad atrānantaraṃ tat tvaṃ kuruṣva yadi rocate  RamS 
na cādharmyaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā sapatnyā mama bhāṣitam 
vihāya śokasaṃtaptāṃ gantum arhasi mām itaḥ  RamS 
dharmajña yadi dharmiṣṭho dharmaṃ caritum icchasi 
śuśrūṣa mām ihasthas tvaṃ cara dharmam anuttamam  RamS 
śuśrūṣur jananīṃ putra svagṛhe niyato vasan 
pareṇa tapasā yuktaḥ kāśyapas tridivaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
yathaiva rājā pūjyas te gauraveṇa tathā hy aham 
tvāṃ nāham anujānāmi na gantavyam ito vanam  RamS 
tvadviyogān na me kāryaṃ jīvitena sukhena vā 
tvayā saha mama śreyas tṛṇānām api bhakṣaṇam  RamS 
yadi tvaṃ yāsyasi vanaṃ tyaktvā māṃ śokalālasām 
ahaṃ prāyam ihāsiṣye na hi śakṣyāmi jīvitum  RamS 
tatas tvaṃ prāpsyase putra nirayaṃ lokaviśrutam 
brahmahatyām ivādharmāt samudraḥ saritāṃ patiḥ  RamS 
vilapantīṃ tathā dīnāṃ kausalyāṃ jananīṃ tataḥ 
uvāca rāmo dharmātmā vacanaṃ dharmasaṃhitam  RamS 
nāsti śaktiḥ pitur vākyaṃ samatikramituṃ mama 
prasādaye tvāṃ śirasā gantum icchāmy ahaṃ vanam  RamS 
ṛṣiṇā ca pitur vākyaṃ kurvatā vratacāriṇā 
gaur hatā jānatā dharmaṃ kaṇḍunāpi vipaścitā  RamS 
asmākaṃ ca kule pūrvaṃ sagarasyājñayā pituḥ 
khanadbhiḥ sāgarair bhūtim avāptaḥ sumahān vadhaḥ  RamS 
jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa reṇukā jananī svayam 
kṛttā paraśunāraṇye pitur vacanakāriṇā  RamS 
na khalv etan mayaikena kriyate pitṛśāsanam 
pūrvair ayam abhipreto gato mārgo 'nugamyate  RamS 
tad etat tu mayā kāryaṃ kriyate bhuvi nānyathā 
pitur hi vacanaṃ kurvan na kaścin nāma hīyate  RamS 
tām evam uktvā jananīṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ punar abravīt 
tava lakṣmaṇa jānāmi mayi sneham anuttamam 
abhiprāyam avijñāya satyasya ca śamasya ca  RamS 
dharmo hi paramo loke dharme satyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam 
dharmasaṃśritam etac ca pitur vacanam uttamam  RamS 
saṃśrutya ca pitur vākyaṃ mātur vā brāhmaṇasya vā 
na kartavyaṃ vṛthā vīra dharmam āśritya tiṣṭhatā  RamS 
so 'haṃ na śakṣyāmi pitur niyogam ativartitum 
pitur hi vacanād vīra kaikeyyāhaṃ pracoditaḥ  RamS 
tad enāṃ visṛjānāryāṃ kṣatradharmāśritāṃ matim 
dharmam āśraya mā taikṣṇyaṃ madbuddhir anugamyatām  RamS 
tam evam uktvā sauhārdād bhrātaraṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ 
uvāca bhūyaḥ kausalyāṃ prāñjaliḥ śirasānataḥ  RamS 
anumanyasva māṃ devi gamiṣyantam ito vanam 
śāpitāsi mama prāṇaiḥ kuru svastyayanāni me 
tīrṇapratijñaś ca vanāt punar eṣyāmy ahaṃ purīm  RamS 
yaśo hy ahaṃ kevalarājyakāraṇān na pṛṣṭhataḥ kartum alaṃ mahodayam 
adīrghakāle na tu devi jīvite vṛṇe 'varām adya mahīm adharmataḥ  RamS 
prasādayan naravṛṣabhaḥ sa mātaraṃ parākramāj jigamiṣur eva daṇḍakān 
athānujaṃ bhṛśam anuśāsya darśanaṃ cakāra tāṃ hṛdi jananīṃ pradakṣiṇam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
atha taṃ vyathayā dīnaṃ saviśeṣam amarṣitam 
śvasantam iva nāgendraṃ roṣavisphāritekṣaṇam  RamS 
āsādya rāmaḥ saumitriṃ suhṛdaṃ bhrātaraṃ priyam 
uvācedaṃ sa dhairyeṇa dhārayan sattvam ātmavān  RamS 
saumitre yo 'bhiṣekārthe mama sambhārasambhramaḥ 
abhiṣekanivṛttyarthe so 'stu sambhārasambhramaḥ  RamS 
yasyā madabhiṣekārthaṃ mānasaṃ paritapyate 
mātā naḥ sā yathā na syāt saviśaṅkā tathā kuru  RamS 
tasyāḥ śaṅkāmayaṃ duḥkhaṃ muhūrtam api notsahe 
manasi pratisaṃjātaṃ saumitre 'ham upekṣitum  RamS 
na buddhipūrvaṃ nābuddhaṃ smarāmīha kadācana 
mātḥṇāṃ vā pitur vāhaṃ kṛtam alpaṃ ca vipriyam  RamS 
satyaḥ satyābhisaṃdhaś ca nityaṃ satyaparākramaḥ 
paralokabhayād bhīto nirbhayo 'stu pitā mama  RamS 
tasyāpi hi bhaved asmin karmaṇy apratisaṃhṛte 
satyaṃ neti manastāpas tasya tāpas tapec ca mām  RamS 
abhiṣekavidhānaṃ tu tasmāt saṃhṛtya lakṣmaṇa 
anvag evāham icchāmi vanaṃ gantum itaḥ punaḥ  RamS 
mama pravrājanād adya kṛtakṛtyā nṛpātmajā 
sutaṃ bharatam avyagram abhiṣecayitā tataḥ  RamS 
mayi cīrājinadhare jaṭāmaṇḍaladhāriṇi 
gate 'raṇyaṃ ca kaikeyyā bhaviṣyati manaḥsukham  RamS 
buddhiḥ praṇītā yeneyaṃ manaś ca susamāhitam 
tat tu nārhāmi saṃkleṣṭuṃ pravrajiṣyāmi māciram  RamS 
kṛtāntas tv eva saumitre draṣṭavyo matpravāsane 
rājyasya ca vitīrṇasya punar eva nivartane  RamS 
kaikeyyāḥ pratipattir hi kathaṃ syān mama pīḍane 
yadi bhāvo na daivo 'yaṃ kṛtāntavihito bhavet  RamS 
jānāsi hi yathā saumya na mātṛṣu mamāntaram 
bhūtapūrvaṃ viśeṣo vā tasyā mayi sute 'pi vā  RamS 
so 'bhiṣekanivṛttyarthaiḥ pravāsārthaiś ca durvacaiḥ 
ugrair vākyair ahaṃ tasyā nānyad daivāt samarthaye  RamS 
kathaṃ prakṛtisampannā rājaputrī tathāguṇā 
brūyāt sā prākṛteva strī matpīḍāṃ bhartṛsaṃnidhau  RamS 
yad acintyaṃ tu tad daivaṃ bhūteṣv api na hanyate 
vyaktaṃ mayi ca tasyāṃ ca patito hi viparyayaḥ  RamS 
kaścid daivena saumitre yoddhum utsahate pumān 
yasya na grahaṇaṃ kiṃcit karmaṇo 'nyatra dṛśyate  RamS 
sukhaduḥkhe bhayakrodhau lābhālābhau bhavābhavau 
yasya kiṃcit tathā bhūtaṃ nanu daivasya karma tat  RamS 
vyāhate 'py abhiṣeke me paritāpo na vidyate 
tasmād aparitāpaḥ saṃs tvam apy anuvidhāya mām 
pratisaṃhāraya kṣipram ābhiṣecanikīṃ kriyām  RamS 
na lakṣmaṇāsmin mama rājyavighne mātā yavīyasy atiśaṅkanīyā 
daivābhipannā hi vadanty aniṣṭaṃ jānāsi daivaṃ ca tathā prabhāvam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
iti bruvati rāme tu lakṣmaṇo 'dhaḥśirā muhuḥ 
śrutvā madhyaṃ jagāmeva manasā duḥkhaharṣayoḥ  RamS 
tadā tu baddhvā bhrukuṭīṃ bhruvor madhye nararṣabhaḥ 
niśaśvāsa mahāsarpo bilastha iva roṣitaḥ  RamS 
tasya duṣprativīkṣyaṃ tad bhrukuṭīsahitaṃ tadā 
babhau kruddhasya siṃhasya mukhasya sadṛśaṃ mukham  RamS 
agrahas taṃ vidhunvaṃs tu hastī hastam ivātmanaḥ 
tiryag ūrdhvaṃ śarīre ca pātayitvā śirodharām  RamS 
agrākṣṇā vīkṣamāṇas tu tiryag bhrātaram abravīt 
asthāne sambhramo yasya jāto vai sumahān ayam  RamS 
dharmadoṣaprasaṅgena lokasyānatiśaṅkayā 
kathaṃ hy etad asambhrāntas tvadvidho vaktum arhati  RamS 
yathā daivam aśauṇḍīraṃ śauṇḍīraḥ kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ 
kiṃ nāma kṛpaṇaṃ daivam aśaktam abhiśaṃsasi  RamS 
pāpayos tu kathaṃ nāma tayoḥ śaṅkā na vidyate 
santi dharmopadhāḥ ślakṣṇā dharmātman kiṃ na budhyase  RamS 
lokavidviṣṭam ārabdhaṃ tvadanyasyābhiṣecanam 
yeneyam āgatā dvaidhaṃ tava buddhir mahīpate 
sa hi dharmo mama dveṣyaḥ prasaṅgād yasya muhyasi  RamS 
yady api pratipattis te daivī cāpi tayor matam 
tathāpy upekṣaṇīyaṃ te na me tad api rocate  RamS 
viklavo vīryahīno yaḥ sa daivam anuvartate 
vīrāḥ saṃbhāvitātmāno na daivaṃ paryupāsate  RamS 
daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa yaḥ samarthaḥ prabādhitum 
na daivena vipannārthaḥ puruṣaḥ so 'vasīdati  RamS 
drakṣyanti tv adya daivasya pauruṣaṃ puruṣasya ca 
daivamānuṣayor adya vyaktā vyaktir bhaviṣyati  RamS 
adya matpauruṣahataṃ daivaṃ drakṣyanti vai janāḥ 
yad daivād āhataṃ te 'dya dṛṣṭaṃ rājyābhiṣecanam  RamS 
atyaṅkuśam ivoddāmaṃ gajaṃ madabaloddhatam 
pradhāvitam ahaṃ daivaṃ pauruṣeṇa nivartaye  RamS 
lokapālāḥ samastās te nādya rāmābhiṣecanam 
na ca kṛtsnās trayo lokā vihanyuḥ kiṃ punaḥ pitā  RamS 
yair vivāsas tavāraṇye mitho rājan samarthitaḥ 
araṇye te vivatsyanti caturdaśa samās tathā  RamS 
ahaṃ tadāśāṃ chetsyāmi pitus tasyāś ca yā tava 
abhiṣekavighātena putrarājyāya vartate  RamS 
madbalena viruddhāya na syād daivabalaṃ tathā 
prabhaviṣyati duḥkhāya yathograṃ pauruṣaṃ mama  RamS 
ūrdhvaṃ varṣasahasrānte prajāpālyam anantaram 
āryaputrāḥ kariṣyanti vanavāsaṃ gate tvayi  RamS 
pūrvarājarṣivṛttyā hi vanavāso vidhīyate 
prajā nikṣipya putreṣu putravat paripālane  RamS 
sa ced rājany anekāgre rājyavibhramaśaṅkayā 
naivam icchasi dharmātman rājyaṃ rāma tvam ātmani  RamS 
pratijāne ca te vīra mā bhūvaṃ vīralokabhāk 
rājyaṃ ca tava rakṣeyam ahaṃ veleva sāgaram  RamS 
maṅgalair abhiṣiñcasva tatra tvaṃ vyāpṛto bhava 
aham eko mahīpālān alaṃ vārayituṃ balāt  RamS 
na śobhārthāv imau bāhū na dhanur bhūṣaṇāya me 
nāsirābandhanārthāya na śarāḥ stambhahetavaḥ  RamS 
amitradamanārthaṃ me sarvam etac catuṣṭayam 
na cāhaṃ kāmaye 'tyarthaṃ yaḥ syāc chatrur mato mama  RamS 
asinā tīkṣṇadhāreṇa vidyuccalitavarcasā 
pragṛhītena vai śatruṃ vajriṇaṃ vā na kalpaye  RamS 
khaḍganiṣpeṣaniṣpiṣṭair gahanā duścarā ca me 
hastyaśvanarahastoruśirobhir bhavitā mahī  RamS 
khaḍgadhārā hatā me 'dya dīpyamānā ivādrayaḥ 
patiṣyanti dvipā bhūmau meghā iva savidyutaḥ  RamS 
baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṇe pragṛhītaśarāsane 
kathaṃ puruṣamānī syāt puruṣāṇāṃ mayi sthite  RamS 
bahubhiś caikam atyasyann ekena ca bahūñ janān 
viniyokṣyāmy ahaṃ bāṇān nṛvājigajamarmasu  RamS 
adya me 'straprabhāvasya prabhāvaḥ prabhaviṣyati 
rājñaś cāprabhutāṃ kartuṃ prabhutvaṃ ca tava prabho  RamS 
adya candanasārasya keyūrāmokṣaṇasya ca 
vasūnāṃ ca vimokṣasya suhṛdāṃ pālanasya ca  RamS 
anurūpāv imau bāhū rāma karma kariṣyataḥ 
abhiṣecanavighnasya kartḥṇāṃ te nivāraṇe  RamS 
bravīhi ko 'dyaiva mayā viyujyatāṃ tavāsuhṛt prāṇayaśaḥ suhṛjjanaiḥ 
yathā taveyaṃ vasudhā vaśe bhavet tathaiva māṃ śādhi tavāsmi kiṃkaraḥ  RamS 
vimṛjya bāṣpaṃ parisāntvya cāsakṛt sa lakṣmaṇaṃ rāghavavaṃśavardhanaḥ 
uvāca pitrye vacane vyavasthitaṃ nibodha mām eṣa hi saumya satpathaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
taṃ samīkṣya tv avahitaṃ pitur nirdeśapālane 
kausalyā bāṣpasaṃruddhā vaco dharmiṣṭham abravīt  RamS 
adṛṣṭaduḥkho dharmātmā sarvabhūtapriyaṃvadaḥ 
mayi jāto daśarathāt katham uñchena vartayet  RamS 
yasya bhṛtyāś ca dāsāś ca mṛṣṭāny annāni bhuñjate 
kathaṃ sa bhokṣyate nātho vane mūlaphalāny ayam  RamS 
ka etacchraddadhecchrutvā kasya vā na bhaved bhayam 
guṇavān dayito rājño rāghavo yad vivāsyate  RamS 
tvayā vihīnām iha māṃ śokāgnir atulo mahān 
pradhakṣyati yathā kakṣaṃ citrabhānur himātyaye  RamS 
kathaṃ hi dhenuḥ svaṃ vatsaṃ gacchantaṃ nānugacchati 
ahaṃ tvānugamiṣyāmi yatra putra gamiṣyasi  RamS 
tathā nigaditaṃ mātrā tad vākyaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ 
śrutvā rāmo 'bravīd vākyaṃ mātaraṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitām  RamS 
kaikeyyā vañcito rājā mayi cāraṇyam āśrite 
bhavatyā ca parityakto na nūnaṃ vartayiṣyati  RamS 
bhartuḥ kila parityāgo nṛśaṃsaḥ kevalaṃ striyāḥ 
sa bhavatyā na kartavyo manasāpi vigarhitaḥ  RamS 
yāvaj jīvati kākutsthaḥ pitā me jagatīpatiḥ 
śuśrūṣā kriyatāṃ tāvat sa hi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ  RamS 
evam uktā tu rāmeṇa kausalyā śubhadarśanā 
tathety uvāca suprītā rāmam akliṣṭakāriṇam  RamS 
evam uktas tu vacanaṃ rāmo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ 
bhūyas tām abravīd vākyaṃ mātaraṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitām  RamS 
mayā caiva bhavatyā ca kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ pituḥ 
rājā bhartā guruḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarveṣām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ  RamS 
imāni tu mahāraṇye vihṛtya nava pañca ca 
varṣāṇi paramaprītaḥ sthāsyāmi vacane tava  RamS 
evam uktā priyaṃ putraṃ bāṣpapūrṇānanā tadā 
uvāca paramārtā tu kausalyā putravatsalā  RamS 
āsāṃ rāma sapatnīnāṃ vastuṃ madhye na me kṣamam 
naya mām api kākutstha vanaṃ vanyāṃ mṛgīṃ yathā 
yadi te gamane buddhiḥ kṛtā pitur apekṣayā  RamS 
tāṃ tathā rudatīṃ rāmo rudan vacanam abravīt 
jīvantyā hi striyā bhartā daivataṃ prabhur eva ca 
bhavatyā mama caivādya rājā prabhavati prabhuḥ  RamS 
bharataś cāpi dharmātmā sarvabhūtapriyaṃvadaḥ 
bhavatīm anuvarteta sa hi dharmarataḥ sadā  RamS 
yathā mayi tu niṣkrānte putraśokena pārthivaḥ 
śramaṃ nāvāpnuyāt kiṃcid apramattā tathā kuru  RamS 
vratopavāsaniratā yā nārī paramottamā 
bhartāraṃ nānuvarteta sā ca pāpagatir bhavet  RamS 
śuśrūṣām eva kurvīta bhartuḥ priyahite ratā 
eṣa dharmaḥ purā dṛṣṭo loke vede śrutaḥ smṛtaḥ  RamS 
pūjyās te matkṛte devi brāhmaṇāś caiva suvratāḥ 
evaṃ kālaṃ pratīkṣasva mamāgamanakāṅkṣiṇī  RamS 
prāpsyase paramaṃ kāmaṃ mayi pratyāgate sati 
yadi dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho dhārayiṣyati jīvitam  RamS 
evam uktā tu rāmeṇa bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇā 
kausalyā putraśokārtā rāmaṃ vacanam abravīt 
gaccha putra tvam ekāgro bhadraṃ te 'stu sadā vibho  RamS 
tathā hi rāmaṃ vanavāsaniścitaṃ samīkṣya devī parameṇa cetasā 
uvāca rāmaṃ śubhalakṣaṇaṃ vaco babhūva ca svastyayanābhikāṅkṣiṇī  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
sāpanīya tam āyāsam upaspṛśya jalaṃ śuci 
cakāra mātā rāmasya maṅgalāni manasvinī  RamS 
svasti sādhyāś ca viśve ca marutaś ca maharṣayaḥ 
svasti dhātā vidhātā ca svasti pūṣā bhago 'ryamā  RamS 
ṛtavaś caiva pakṣāś ca māsāḥ saṃvatsarāḥ kṣapāḥ 
dināni ca muhūrtāś ca svasti kurvantu te sadā  RamS 
smṛtir dhṛtiś ca dharmaś ca pāntu tvāṃ putra sarvataḥ 
skandaś ca bhagavān devaḥ somaś ca sabṛhaspatiḥ  RamS 
saptarṣayo nāradaś ca te tvāṃ rakṣantu sarvataḥ 
nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvāṇi grahāś ca sahadevatāḥ 
mahāvanāni carato muniveṣasya dhīmataḥ  RamS 
plavagā vṛścikā daṃśā maśakāś caiva kānane 
sarīsṛpāś ca kīṭāś ca mā bhūvan gahane tava  RamS 
mahādvipāś ca siṃhāś ca vyāghrā ṛkṣāś ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ 
mahiṣāḥ śṛṅgiṇo raudrā na te druhyantu putraka  RamS 
nṛmāṃsabhojanā raudrā ye cānye sattvajātayaḥ 
mā ca tvāṃ hiṃsiṣuḥ putra mayā sampūjitās tv iha  RamS 
āgamās te śivāḥ santu sidhyantu ca parākramāḥ 
sarvasampattayo rāma svastimān gaccha putraka  RamS 
svasti te 'stv āntarikṣebhyaḥ pārthivebhyaḥ punaḥ punaḥ 
sarvebhyaś caiva devebhyo ye ca te paripanthinaḥ  RamS 
sarvalokaprabhur brahmā bhūtabhartā tatharṣayaḥ 
ye ca śeṣāḥ surās te tvāṃ rakṣantu vanavāsinam  RamS 
iti mālyaiḥ suragaṇān gandhaiś cāpi yaśasvinī 
stutibhiś cānurūpābhir ānarcāyatalocanā  RamS 
yan maṅgalaṃ sahasrākṣe sarvadevanamaskṛte 
vṛtranāśe samabhavat tat te bhavatu maṅgalam  RamS 
yan maṅgalaṃ suparṇasya vinatākalpayat purā 
amṛtaṃ prārthayānasya tat te bhavatu maṅgalam  RamS 
oṣadhīṃ cāpi siddhārthāṃ viśalyakaraṇīṃ śubhām 
cakāra rakṣāṃ kausalyā mantrair abhijajāpa ca  RamS 
ānamya mūrdhni cāghrāya pariṣvajya yaśasvinī 
avadat putra siddhārtho gaccha rāma yathāsukham  RamS 
arogaṃ sarvasiddhārtham ayodhyāṃ punar āgatam 
paśyāmi tvāṃ sukhaṃ vatsa susthitaṃ rājaveśmani  RamS 
mayārcitā devagaṇāḥ śivādayo maharṣayo bhūtamahāsuroragāḥ 
abhiprayātasya vanaṃ cirāya te hitāni kāṅkṣantu diśaś ca rāghava  RamS 
itīva cāśrupratipūrṇalocanā samāpya ca svastyayanaṃ yathāvidhi 
pradakṣiṇaṃ caiva cakāra rāghavaṃ punaḥ punaś cāpi nipīḍya sasvaje  RamS 
tathā tu devyā sa kṛtapradakṣiṇo nipīḍya mātuś caraṇau punaḥ punaḥ 
jagāma sītānilayaṃ mahāyaśāḥ sa rāghavaḥ prajvalitaḥ svayā śriyā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
abhivādya tu kausalyāṃ rāmaḥ samprasthito vanam 
kṛtasvastyayano mātrā dharmiṣṭhe vartmani sthitaḥ  RamS 
virājayan rājasuto rājamārgaṃ narair vṛtam 
hṛdayāny āmamantheva janasya guṇavattayā  RamS 
vaidehī cāpi tat sarvaṃ na śuśrāva tapasvinī 
tad eva hṛdi tasyāś ca yauvarājyābhiṣecanam  RamS 
devakāryaṃ sma sā kṛtvā kṛtajñā hṛṣṭacetanā 
abhijñā rājadharmāṇāṃ rājaputraṃ pratīkṣate  RamS 
praviveśātha rāmas tu svaveśma suvibhūṣitam 
prahṛṣṭajanasampūrṇaṃ hriyā kiṃcid avāṅmukhaḥ  RamS 
atha sītā samutpatya vepamānā ca taṃ patim 
apaśyac chokasaṃtaptaṃ cintāvyākulitendriyam  RamS 
vivarṇavadanaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ prasvinnam amarṣaṇam 
āha duḥkhābhisaṃtaptā kim idānīm idaṃ prabho  RamS 
adya bārhaspataḥ śrīmān yuktaḥ puṣyo na rāghava 
procyate brāhmaṇaiḥ prājñaiḥ kena tvam asi durmanāḥ  RamS 
na te śataśalākena jalaphenanibhena ca 
āvṛtaṃ vadanaṃ valgu chattreṇābhivirājate  RamS 
vyajanābhyāṃ ca mukhyābhyāṃ śatapattranibhekṣaṇam 
candrahaṃsaprakāśābhyāṃ vījyate na tavānanam  RamS 
vāgmino bandinaś cāpi prahṛṣṭās tvāṃ nararṣabha 
stuvanto nādya dṛśyante maṅgalaiḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ  RamS 
na te kṣaudraṃ ca dadhi ca brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ 
mūrdhni mūrdhāvasiktasya dadhati sma vidhānataḥ  RamS 
na tvāṃ prakṛtayaḥ sarvā śreṇīmukhyāś ca bhūṣitāḥ 
anuvrajitum icchanti paurajānapadās tathā  RamS 
caturbhir vegasampannair hayaiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ 
mukhyaḥ puṣyaratho yuktaḥ kiṃ na gacchati te 'grataḥ  RamS 
na hastī cāgrataḥ śrīmāṃs tava lakṣaṇapūjitaḥ 
prayāṇe lakṣyate vīra kṛṣṇameghagiriprabhaḥ  RamS 
na ca kāñcanacitraṃ te paśyāmi priyadarśana 
bhadrāsanaṃ puraskṛtya yāntaṃ vīrapuraḥsaram  RamS 
abhiṣeko yadā sajjaḥ kim idānīm idaṃ tava 
apūrvo mukhavarṇaś ca na praharṣaś ca lakṣyate  RamS 
itīva vilapantīṃ tāṃ provāca raghunandanaḥ 
sīte tatrabhavāṃs tātaḥ pravrājayati māṃ vanam  RamS 
kule mahati sambhūte dharmajñe dharmacāriṇi 
śṛṇu jānaki yenedaṃ krameṇābhyāgataṃ mama  RamS 
rājñā satyapratijñena pitrā daśarathena me 
kaikeyyai prītamanasā purā dattau mahāvarau  RamS 
tayādya mama sajje 'sminn abhiṣeke nṛpodyate 
pracoditaḥ sa samayo dharmeṇa pratinirjitaḥ  RamS 
caturdaśa hi varṣāṇi vastavyaṃ daṇḍake mayā 
pitrā me bharataś cāpi yauvarājye niyojitaḥ 
so 'haṃ tvām āgato draṣṭuṃ prasthito vijanaṃ vanam  RamS 
bharatasya samīpe te nāhaṃ kathyaḥ kadācana 
ṛddhiyuktā hi puruṣā na sahante parastavam 
tasmān na te guṇāḥ kathyā bharatasyāgrato mama  RamS 
nāpi tvaṃ tena bhartavyā viśeṣeṇa kadācana 
anukūlatayā śakyaṃ samīpe tasya vartitum  RamS 
ahaṃ cāpi pratijñāṃ tāṃ guroḥ samanupālayan 
vanam adyaiva yāsyāmi sthirā bhava manasvini  RamS 
yāte ca mayi kalyāṇi vanaṃ muniniṣevitam 
vratopavāsaratayā bhavitavyaṃ tvayānaghe  RamS 
kālyam utthāya devānāṃ kṛtvā pūjāṃ yathāvidhi 
vanditavyo daśarathaḥ pitā mama nareśvaraḥ  RamS 
mātā ca mama kausalyā vṛddhā saṃtāpakarśitā 
dharmam evāgrataḥ kṛtvā tvattaḥ sammānam arhati  RamS 
vanditavyāś ca te nityaṃ yāḥ śeṣā mama mātaraḥ 
snehapraṇayasambhogaiḥ samā hi mama mātaraḥ  RamS 
bhrātṛputrasamau cāpi draṣṭavyau ca viśeṣataḥ 
tvayā lakṣmaṇaśatrughnau prāṇaiḥ priyatarau mama  RamS 
vipriyaṃ na ca kartavyaṃ bharatasya kadācana 
sa hi rājā prabhuś caiva deśasya ca kulasya ca  RamS 
ārādhitā hi śīlena prayatnaiś copasevitāḥ 
rājānaḥ samprasīdanti prakupyanti viparyaye  RamS 
aurasān api putrān hi tyajanty ahitakāriṇaḥ 
samarthān sampragṛhṇanti janān api narādhipāḥ  RamS 
ahaṃ gamiṣyāmi mahāvanaṃ priye tvayā hi vastavyam ihaiva bhāmini 
yathā vyalīkaṃ kuruṣe na kasyacit tathā tvayā kāryam idaṃ vaco mama  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
evam uktā tu vaidehī priyārhā priyavādinī 
praṇayād eva saṃkruddhā bhartāram idam abravīt  RamS 
āryaputra pitā mātā bhrātā putras tathā snuṣā 
svāni puṇyāni bhuñjānāḥ svaṃ svaṃ bhāgyam upāsate  RamS 
bhartur bhāgyaṃ tu bhāryaikā prāpnoti puruṣarṣabha 
ataś caivāham ādiṣṭā vane vastavyam ity api  RamS 
na pitā nātmajo nātmā na mātā na sakhījanaḥ 
iha pretya ca nārīṇāṃ patir eko gatiḥ sadā  RamS 
yadi tvaṃ prasthito durgaṃ vanam adyaiva rāghava 
agratas te gamiṣyāmi mṛdnantī kuśakaṇṭakān  RamS 
īrṣyāroṣau bahiṣkṛtya bhuktaśeṣam ivodakam 
naya māṃ vīra viśrabdhaḥ pāpaṃ mayi na vidyate  RamS 
prāsādāgrair vimānair vā vaihāyasagatena vā 
sarvāvasthāgatā bhartuḥ pādacchāyā viśiṣyate  RamS 
anuśiṣṭāsmi mātrā ca pitrā ca vividhāśrayam 
nāsmi samprati vaktavyā vartitavyaṃ yathā mayā  RamS 
sukhaṃ vane nivatsyāmi yathaiva bhavane pituḥ 
acintayantī trīṃl lokāṃś cintayantī pativratam  RamS 
śuśrūṣamāṇā te nityaṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇī 
saha raṃsye tvayā vīra vaneṣu madhugandhiṣu  RamS 
tvaṃ hi kartuṃ vane śakto rāma samparipālanam 
anyasyāpi janasyeha kiṃ punar mama mānada  RamS 
phalamūlāśanā nityaṃ bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ 
na te duḥkhaṃ kariṣyāmi nivasantī saha tvayā  RamS 
icchāmi saritaḥ śailān palvalāni vanāni ca 
draṣṭuṃ sarvatra nirbhītā tvayā nāthena dhīmatā  RamS 
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇāḥ padminīḥ sādhupuṣpitāḥ 
iccheyaṃ sukhinī draṣṭuṃ tvayā vīreṇa saṃgatā  RamS 
saha tvayā viśālākṣa raṃsye paramanandinī 
evaṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ vāhaṃ tvayā saha  RamS 
svarge 'pi ca vinā vāso bhavitā yadi rāghava 
tvayā mama naravyāghra nāhaṃ tam api rocaye  RamS 
ahaṃ gamiṣyāmi vanaṃ sudurgamaṃ mṛgāyutaṃ vānaravāraṇair yutam 
vane nivatsyāmi yathā pitur gṛhe tavaiva pādāv upagṛhya saṃmatā  RamS 
ananyabhāvām anuraktacetasaṃ tvayā viyuktāṃ maraṇāya niścitām 
nayasva māṃ sādhu kuruṣva yācanāṃ na te mayāto gurutā bhaviṣyati  RamS 
tathā bruvāṇām api dharmavatsalo na ca sma sītāṃ nṛvaro ninīṣati 
uvāca caināṃ bahu saṃnivartane vane nivāsasya ca duḥkhitāṃ prati  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
sa evaṃ bruvatīṃ sītāṃ dharmajño dharmavatsalaḥ 
nivartanārthe dharmātmā vākyam etad uvāca ha  RamS 
sīte mahākulīnāsi dharme ca niratā sadā 
ihācara svadharmaṃ tvaṃ mā yathā manasaḥ sukham  RamS 
sīte yathā tvāṃ vakṣyāmi tathā kāryaṃ tvayābale 
vane doṣā hi bahavo vadatas tān nibodha me  RamS 
sīte vimucyatām eṣā vanavāsakṛtā matiḥ 
bahudoṣaṃ hi kāntāraṃ vanam ity abhidhīyate  RamS 
hitabuddhyā khalu vaco mayaitad abhidhīyate 
sadā sukhaṃ na jānāmi duḥkham eva sadā vanam  RamS 
girinirjharasambhūtā girikandaravāsinām 
siṃhānāṃ ninadā duḥkhāḥ śrotuṃ duḥkham ato vanam  RamS 
supyate parṇaśayyāsu svayaṃ bhagnāsu bhūtale 
rātriṣu śramakhinnena tasmād duḥkhataraṃ vanam  RamS 
upavāsaś ca kartavyo yathāprāṇena maithili 
jaṭābhāraś ca kartavyo valkalāmbaradhāriṇā  RamS 
atīva vātas timiraṃ bubhukṣā cātra nityaśaḥ 
bhayāni ca mahānty atra tato duḥkhataraṃ vanam  RamS 
sarīsṛpāś ca bahavo bahurūpāś ca bhāmini 
caranti pṛthivīṃ darpād ato duḥkhataraṃ vanam  RamS 
nadīnilayanāḥ sarpā nadīkuṭilagāminaḥ 
tiṣṭhanty āvṛtya panthānam ato duḥkhataraṃ vanam  RamS 
pataṃgā vṛścikāḥ kīṭā daṃśāś ca maśakaiḥ saha 
bādhante nityam abale sarvaṃ duḥkham ato vanam  RamS 
drumāḥ kaṇṭakinaś caiva kuśakāśāś ca bhāmini 
vane vyākulaśākhāgrās tena duḥkhataraṃ vanam  RamS 
tad alaṃ te vanaṃ gatvā kṣamaṃ na hi vanaṃ tava 
vimṛśann iha paśyāmi bahudoṣataraṃ vanam  RamS 
vanaṃ tu netuṃ na kṛtā matis tadā babhūva rāmeṇa yadā mahātmanā 
na tasya sītā vacanaṃ cakāra tat tato 'bravīd rāmam idaṃ suduḥkhitā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
etat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā sītā rāmasya duḥkhitā 
prasaktāśrumukhī mandam idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
ye tvayā kīrtitā doṣā vane vastavyatāṃ prati 
guṇān ity eva tān viddhi tava snehapuraskṛtān  RamS 
tvayā ca saha gantavyaṃ mayā gurujanājñayā 
tvadviyogena me rāma tyaktavyam iha jīvitam  RamS 
na ca māṃ tvatsamīpasthām api śaknoti rāghava 
surāṇām īśvaraḥ śakraḥ pradharṣayitum ojasā  RamS 
patihīnā tu yā nārī na sā śakṣyati jīvitum 
kāmam evaṃvidhaṃ rāma tvayā mama vidarśitam  RamS 
atha cāpi mahāprājña brāhmaṇānāṃ mayā śrutam 
purā pitṛgṛhe satyaṃ vastavyaṃ kila me vane  RamS 
lakṣaṇibhyo dvijātibhyaḥ śrutvāhaṃ vacanaṃ gṛhe 
vanavāsakṛtotsāhā nityam eva mahābala  RamS 
ādeśo vanavāsasya prāptavyaḥ sa mayā kila 
sā tvayā saha tatrāhaṃ yāsyāmi priya nānyathā  RamS 
kṛtādeśā bhaviṣyāmi gamiṣyāmi saha tvayā 
kālaś cāyaṃ samutpannaḥ satyavāg bhavatu dvijaḥ  RamS 
vanavāse hi jānāmi duḥkhāni bahudhā kila 
prāpyante niyataṃ vīra puruṣair akṛtātmabhiḥ  RamS 
kanyayā ca pitur gehe vanavāsaḥ śruto mayā 
bhikṣiṇyāḥ sādhuvṛttāyā mama mātur ihāgrataḥ  RamS 
prasāditaś ca vai pūrvaṃ tvaṃ vai bahuvidhaṃ prabho 
gamanaṃ vanavāsasya kāṅkṣitaṃ hi saha tvayā  RamS 
kṛtakṣaṇāhaṃ bhadraṃ te gamanaṃ prati rāghava 
vanavāsasya śūrasya caryā hi mama rocate  RamS 
śuddhātman premabhāvād dhi bhaviṣyāmi vikalmaṣā 
bhartāram anugacchantī bhartā hi mama daivatam  RamS 
pretyabhāve 'pi kalyāṇaḥ saṃgamo me saha tvayā 
śrutir hi śrūyate puṇyā brāhmaṇānāṃ yaśasvinām  RamS 
iha loke ca pitṛbhir yā strī yasya mahāmate 
adbhir dattā svadharmeṇa pretyabhāve 'pi tasya sā  RamS 
evam asmāt svakāṃ nārīṃ suvṛttāṃ hi pativratām 
nābhirocayase netuṃ tvaṃ māṃ keneha hetunā  RamS 
bhaktāṃ pativratāṃ dīnāṃ māṃ samāṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ 
netum arhasi kākutstha samānasukhaduḥkhinīm  RamS 
yadi māṃ duḥkhitām evaṃ vanaṃ netuṃ na cecchasi
