na caiva devī virarāma kūjitāt priyeti putreti ca rāghaveti ca  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
vanaṃ gate dharmapare rāme ramayatāṃ vare 
kausalyā rudatī svārtā bhartāram idam abravīt  RamS 
yadyapi triṣu lokeṣu prathitaṃ te mahad yaśaḥ 
sānukrośo vadānyaś ca priyavādī ca rāghavaḥ  RamS 
kathaṃ naravaraśreṣṭha putrau tau saha sītayā 
duḥkhitau sukhasaṃvṛddhau vane duḥkhaṃ sahiṣyataḥ  RamS 
sā nūnaṃ taruṇī śyāmā sukumārī sukhocitā 
katham uṣṇaṃ ca śītaṃ ca maithilī prasahiṣyate  RamS 
bhuktvāśanaṃ viśālākṣī sūpadaṃśānvitaṃ śubham 
vanyaṃ naivāram āhāraṃ kathaṃ sītopabhokṣyate  RamS 
gītavāditranirghoṣaṃ śrutvā śubham aninditā 
kathaṃ kravyādasiṃhānāṃ śabdaṃ śroṣyaty aśobhanam  RamS 
mahendradhvajasaṃkāśaḥ kva nu śete mahābhujaḥ 
bhujaṃ parighasaṃkāśam upadhāya mahābalaḥ  RamS 
padmavarṇaṃ sukeśāntaṃ padmaniḥśvāsam uttamam 
kadā drakṣyāmi rāmasya vadanaṃ puṣkarekṣaṇam  RamS 
vajrasāramayaṃ nūnaṃ hṛdayaṃ me na saṃśayaḥ 
apaśyantyā na taṃ yad vai phalatīdaṃ sahasradhā  RamS 
yadi pañcadaśe varṣe rāghavaḥ punar eṣyati 
jahyād rājyaṃ ca kośaṃ ca bharatenopabhokṣyate  RamS 
evaṃ kanīyasā bhrātrā bhuktaṃ rājyaṃ viśāṃ pate 
bhrātā jyeṣṭho variṣṭhaś ca kimarthaṃ nāvamaṃsyate  RamS 
na pareṇāhṛtaṃ bhakṣyaṃ vyāghraḥ khāditum icchati 
evam eva naravyāghraḥ paralīḍhaṃ na maṃsyate  RamS 
havir ājyaṃ puroḍāśāḥ kuśā yūpāś ca khādirāḥ 
naitāni yātayāmāni kurvanti punar adhvare  RamS 
tathā hy āttam idaṃ rājyaṃ hṛtasārāṃ surām iva 
nābhimantum alaṃ rāmo naṣṭasomam ivādhvaram  RamS 
naivaṃvidham asatkāraṃ rāghavo marṣayiṣyati 
balavān iva śārdūlo vāladher abhimarśanam  RamS 
sa tādṛśaḥ siṃhabalo vṛṣabhākṣo nararṣabhaḥ 
svayam eva hataḥ pitrā jalajenātmajo yathā  RamS 
dvijātidharmaḥ śāstradṛṣṭaḥ sanātanaḥ 
yadi te dharmanirate tvayā putre vivāsite  RamS 
gatir ekā patir nāryā dvitīyā gatir ātmajaḥ 
tṛtīyā jñātayo rājaṃś caturthī neha vidyate  RamS 
tatra tvaṃ caiva me nāsti rāmaś ca vanam āśritaḥ 
na vanaṃ gantum icchāmi sarvathā hi hatā tvayā  RamS 
hataṃ tvayā rājyam idaṃ sarāṣṭraṃ hatas tathātmā saha mantribhiś ca 
hatā saputrāsmi hatāś ca paurāḥ sutaś ca bhāryā ca tava prahṛṣṭau  RamS 
imāṃ giraṃ dāruṇaśabdasaṃśritāṃ niśamya rājāpi mumoha duḥkhitaḥ 
tataḥ sa śokaṃ praviveśa pārthivaḥ svaduṣkṛtaṃ cāpi punas tadāsmarat  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
evaṃ tu kruddhayā rājā rāmamātrā saśokayā 
śrāvitaḥ paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ cintayāmāsa duḥkhitaḥ  RamS 
tasya cintayamānasya pratyabhāt karma duṣkṛtam 
yad anena kṛtaṃ pūrvam ajñānāc chabdavedhinā  RamS 
amanās tena śokena rāmaśokena ca prabhuḥ 
dahyamānas tu śokābhyāṃ kausalyām āha bhūpatiḥ  RamS 
prasādaye tvāṃ kausalye racito 'yaṃ mayāñjaliḥ 
vatsalā cānṛśaṃsā ca tvaṃ hi nityaṃ pareṣv api  RamS 
bhartā tu khalu nārīṇāṃ guṇavān nirguṇo 'pi vā 
dharmaṃ vimṛśamānānāṃ pratyakṣaṃ devi daivatam  RamS 
sā tvaṃ dharmaparā nityaṃ dṛṣṭalokaparāvarā 
nārhase vipriyaṃ vaktuṃ duḥkhitāpi suduḥkhitam  RamS 
tad vākyaṃ karuṇaṃ rājñaḥ śrutvā dīnasya bhāṣitam 
kausalyā vyasṛjad bāṣpaṃ praṇālīva navodakam  RamS 
sa mūrdhni baddhvā rudatī rājñaḥ padmam ivāñjalim 
sambhramād abravīt trastā tvaramāṇākṣaraṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
prasīda śirasā yāce bhūmau nipatitāsmi te 
yācitāsmi hatā deva hantavyāhaṃ na hi tvayā  RamS 
naiṣā hi sā strī bhavati ślāghanīyena dhīmatā 
ubhayor lokayor vīra patyā yā saṃprasādyate  RamS 
jānāmi dharmaṃ dharmajña tvāṃ jāne satyavādinam 
putraśokārtayā tat tu mayā kim api bhāṣitam  RamS 
śoko nāśayate dhairyaṃ śoko nāśayate śrutam 
śoko nāśayate sarvaṃ nāsti śokasamo ripuḥ  RamS 
śayam āpatitaḥ soḍhuṃ praharo ripuhastataḥ 
soḍhum āpatitaḥ śokaḥ susūkṣmo 'pi na śakyate  RamS 
vanavāsāya rāmasya pañcarātro 'dya gaṇyate 
yaḥ śokahataharṣāyāḥ pañcavarṣopamo mama  RamS 
taṃ hi cintayamānāyāḥ śoko 'yaṃ hṛdi vardhate 
adīnām iva vegena samudrasalilaṃ mahat  RamS 
evaṃ hi kathayantyās tu kausalyāyāḥ śubhaṃ vacaḥ 
mandaraśmir abhūt suryo rajanī cābhyavartata  RamS 
atha prahlādito vākyair devyā kausalyayā nṛpaḥ 
śokena ca samākrānto nidrāyā vaśam eyivān  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
pratibuddho muhūrtena śokopahatacetanaḥ 
atha rājā daśarathaḥ sa cintām abhyapadyata  RamS 
rāmalakṣmaṇayoś caiva vivāsād vāsavopamam 
āviveśopasargas taṃ tamaḥ sūryam ivāsuram  RamS 
sa rājā rajanīṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ rāme pravrajite vanam 
ardharātre daśarathaḥ saṃsmaran duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam 
kausalyāṃ putraśokārtām idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
yad ācarati kalyāṇi śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham 
tad eva labhate bhadre kartā karmajam ātmanaḥ  RamS 
gurulāghavam arthānām ārambhe karmaṇāṃ phalam 
doṣaṃ vā yo na jānāti sa bāla iti hocyate  RamS 
kaścid āmravaṇaṃ chittvā palāśāṃś ca niṣiñcati 
puṣpaṃ dṛṣṭvā phale gṛdhnuḥ sa śocati phalāgame  RamS 
so 'ham āmravaṇaṃ chittvā palāśāṃś ca nyaṣecayam 
rāmaṃ phalāgame tyaktvā paścāc chocāmi durmatiḥ  RamS 
labdhaśabdena kausalye kumāreṇa dhanuṣmatā 
kumāraḥ śabdavedhīti mayā pāpam idaṃ kṛtam 
tad idaṃ me 'nusaṃprāptaṃ devi duḥkhaṃ svayaṃ kṛtam  RamS 
sammohād iha bālena yathā syād bhakṣitaṃ viṣam 
evaṃ mamāpy avijñātaṃ śabdavedhyamayaṃ phalam  RamS 
devy anūḍhā tvam abhavo yuvarājo bhavāmy aham 
tataḥ prāvṛḍ anuprāptā madakāmavivardhinī  RamS 
upāsya hi rasān bhaumāṃs taptvā ca jagad aṃśubhiḥ 
paretācaritāṃ bhīmāṃ ravir āviśate diśam  RamS 
uṣṇam antardadhe sadyaḥ snigdhā dadṛśire ghanāḥ 
tato jahṛṣire sarve bhekasāraṅgabarhiṇaḥ  RamS 
patitenāmbhasā channaḥ patamānena cāsakṛt 
ābabhau mattasāraṅgas toyarāśir ivācalaḥ  RamS 
tasminn atisukhe kāle dhanuṣmān iṣumān rathī 
vyāyāmakṛtasaṃkalpaḥ sarayūm anvagāṃ nadīm  RamS 
nipāne mahiṣaṃ rātrau gajaṃ vābhyāgataṃ nadīm 
anyaṃ vā śvāpadaṃ kaṃcij jighāṃsur ajitendriyaḥ  RamS 
athāndhakāre tv aśrauṣaṃ jale kumbhasya pūryataḥ 
acakṣur viṣaye ghoṣaṃ vāraṇasyeva nardataḥ  RamS 
tato 'haṃ śaram uddhṛtya dīptam āśīviṣopamam 
amuñcaṃ niśitaṃ bāṇam aham āśīviṣopamam  RamS 
tatra vāg uṣasi vyaktā prādurāsīd vanaukasaḥ 
hā heti patatas toye vāg abhūt tatra mānuṣī 
katham asmadvidhe śastraṃ nipatet tu tapasvini  RamS 
praviviktāṃ nadīṃ rātrāv udāhāro 'ham āgataḥ 
iṣuṇābhihataḥ kena kasya vā kiṃ kṛtaṃ mayā  RamS 
ṛṣer hi nyastadaṇḍasya vane vanyena jīvataḥ 
kathaṃ nu śastreṇa vadho madvidhasya vidhīyate  RamS 
jaṭābhāradharasyaiva valkalājinavāsasaḥ 
ko vadhena mamārthī syāt kiṃ vāsyāpakṛtaṃ mayā  RamS 
evaṃ niṣphalam ārabdhaṃ kevalānarthasaṃhitam 
na kaścit sādhu manyeta yathaiva gurutalpagam  RamS 
nemaṃ tathānuśocāmi jīvitakṣayam ātmanaḥ 
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ cobhāv anuśocāmi madvidhe  RamS 
tad etan mithunaṃ vṛddhaṃ cirakālabhṛtaṃ mayā 
mayi pañcatvam āpanne kāṃ vṛttiṃ vartayiṣyati  RamS 
vṛddhau ca mātāpitarāv ahaṃ caikeṣuṇā hataḥ 
kena sma nihatāḥ sarve subālenākṛtātmanā  RamS 
tāṃ giraṃ karuṇāṃ śrutvā mama dharmānukāṅkṣiṇaḥ 
karābhyāṃ saśaraṃ cāpaṃ vyathitasyāpatad bhuvi  RamS 
taṃ deśam aham āgamya dīnasattvaḥ sudurmanāḥ 
apaśyam iṣuṇā tīre sarayvās tāpasaṃ hatam  RamS 
sa mām udvīkṣya netrābhyāṃ trastam asvasthacetasam 
ity uvāca vacaḥ krūraṃ didhakṣann iva tejasā  RamS 
kiṃ tavāpakṛtaṃ rājan vane nivasatā mayā 
jihīrṣur ambho gurvarthaṃ yad ahaṃ tāḍitas tvayā  RamS 
ekena khalu bāṇena marmaṇy abhihate mayi 
dvāv andhau nihatau vṛddhau mātā janayitā ca me  RamS 
tau nūnaṃ durbalāv andhau matpratīkṣau pipāsitau 
ciram āśākṛtāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ kaṣṭāṃ saṃdhārayiṣyataḥ  RamS 
na nūnaṃ tapaso vāsti phalayogaḥ śrutasya vā 
pitā yan māṃ na jānāti śayānaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi  RamS 
jānann api ca kiṃ kuryād aśaktir aparikramaḥ 
bhidyamānam ivāśaktas trātum anyo nago nagam  RamS 
pitus tvam eva me gatvā śīghram ācakṣva rāghava 
na tvām anudahet kruddho vanaṃ vahnir ivaidhitaḥ  RamS 
iyam ekapadī rājan yato me pitur āśramaḥ 
taṃ prasādaya gatvā tvaṃ na tvāṃ sa kupitaḥ śapet  RamS 
viśalyaṃ kuru māṃ rājan marma me niśitaḥ śaraḥ 
ruṇaddhi mṛdu sotsedhaṃ tīram amburayo yathā  RamS 
na dvijātir ahaṃ rājan mā bhūt te manaso vyathā 
śūdrāyām asmi vaiśyena jāto janapadādhipa  RamS 
itīva vadataḥ kṛcchrād bāṇābhihatamarmaṇaḥ 
tasya tv ānamyamānasya taṃ bāṇam aham uddharam  RamS 
jalārdragātraṃ tu vilapya kṛcchrān marmavraṇaṃ saṃtatam ucchvasantam 
tataḥ sarayvāṃ tam ahaṃ śayānaṃ samīkṣya bhadre subhṛśaṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tad ajñānān mahat pāpaṃ kṛtvā saṃkulitendriyaḥ 
ekas tv acintayaṃ buddhyā kathaṃ nu sukṛtaṃ bhavet  RamS 
tatas taṃ ghaṭam ādāya pūrṇaṃ paramavāriṇā 
āśramaṃ tam ahaṃ prāpya yathākhyātapathaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
tatrāhaṃ durbalāv andhau vṛddhāv apariṇāyakau 
apaśyaṃ tasya pitarau lūnapakṣāv iva dvijau  RamS 
tannimittābhir āsīnau kathābhir aparikramau 
tām āśāṃ matkṛte hīnāv udāsīnāv anāthavat  RamS 
padaśabdaṃ tu me śrutvā munir vākyam abhāṣata 
kiṃ cirāyasi me putra pānīyaṃ kṣipram ānaya  RamS 
yannimittam idaṃ tāta salile krīḍitaṃ tvayā 
utkaṇṭhitā te māteyaṃ praviśa kṣipram āśramam  RamS 
yad vyalīkaṃ kṛtaṃ putra mātrā te yadi vā mayā 
na tan manasi kartavyaṃ tvayā tāta tapasvinā  RamS 
tvaṃ gatis tv agatīnāṃ ca cakṣus tvaṃ hīnacakṣuṣām 
samāsaktās tvayi prāṇāḥ kiṃcin nau nābhibhāṣase  RamS 
munim avyaktayā vācā tam ahaṃ sajjamānayā 
hīnavyañjanayā prekṣya bhīto bhīta ivābruvam  RamS 
manasaḥ karma ceṣṭābhir abhisaṃstabhya vāgbalam 
ācacakṣe tv ahaṃ tasmai putravyasanajaṃ bhayam  RamS 
kṣatriyo 'haṃ daśaratho nāhaṃ putro mahātmanaḥ 
sajjanāvamataṃ duḥkham idaṃ prāptaṃ svakarmajam  RamS 
bhagavaṃś cāpahasto 'haṃ sarayūtīram āgataḥ 
jighāṃsuḥ śvāpadaṃ kiṃcin nipāne vāgataṃ gajam  RamS 
tatra śruto mayā śabdo jale kumbhasya pūryataḥ 
dvipo 'yam iti matvā hi bāṇenābhihato mayā  RamS 
gatvā nadyās tatas tīram apaśyam iṣuṇā hṛdi 
vinirbhinnaṃ gataprāṇaṃ śayānaṃ bhuvi tāpasam  RamS 
bhagavañ śabdam ālakṣya mayā gajajighāṃsunā 
visṛṣṭo 'mbhasi nārācas tena te nihataḥ sutaḥ  RamS 
sa coddhṛtena bāṇena tatraiva svargam āsthitaḥ 
bhagavantāv ubhau śocann andhāv iti vilapya ca  RamS 
ajñānād bhavataḥ putraḥ sahasābhihato mayā 
śeṣam evaṃgate yat syāt tat prasīdatu me muniḥ  RamS 
sa tac chrutvā vacaḥ krūraṃ niḥśvasañ śokakarśitaḥ 
mām uvāca mahātejāḥ kṛtāñjalim upasthitam  RamS 
yady etad aśubhaṃ karma na sma me kathayeḥ svayam 
phalen mūrdhā sma te rājan sadyaḥ śatasahasradhā  RamS 
kṣatriyeṇa vadho rājan vānaprasthe viśeṣataḥ 
jñānapūrvaṃ kṛtaḥ sthānāc cyāvayed api vajriṇam  RamS 
ajñānāddhi kṛtaṃ yasmād idaṃ tenaiva jīvasi 
api hy adya kulaṃ na syād rāghavāṇāṃ kuto bhavān  RamS 
naya nau nṛpa taṃ deśam iti māṃ cābhyabhāṣata 
adya taṃ draṣṭum icchāvaḥ putraṃ paścimadarśanam  RamS 
rudhireṇāvasitāṅgaṃ prakīrṇājinavāsasam 
śayānaṃ bhuvi niḥsaṃjñaṃ dharmarājavaśaṃ gatam  RamS 
athāham ekas taṃ deśaṃ nītvā tau bhṛśaduḥkhitau 
asparśayam ahaṃ putraṃ taṃ muniṃ saha bhāryayā  RamS 
tau putram ātmanaḥ spṛṣṭvā tam āsādya tapasvinau 
nipetatuḥ śarīre 'sya pitā cāsyedam abravīt  RamS 
na nv ahaṃ te priyaḥ putra mātaraṃ paśya dhārmika 
kiṃ nu nāliṅgase putra sukumāra vaco vada  RamS 
kasya vāpararātre 'haṃ śroṣyāmi hṛdayaṃgamam 
adhīyānasya madhuraṃ śāstraṃ vānyad viśeṣataḥ  RamS 
ko māṃ saṃdhyām upāsyaiva snātvā hutahutāśanaḥ 
ślāghayiṣyaty upāsīnaḥ putraśokabhayārditam  RamS 
kandamūlaphalaṃ hṛtvā ko māṃ priyam ivātithim 
bhojayiṣyaty akarmaṇyam apragraham anāyakam  RamS 
imām andhāṃ ca vṛddhāṃ ca mātaraṃ te tapasvinīm 
kathaṃ putra bhariṣyāmi kṛpaṇāṃ putragardhinīm  RamS 
tiṣṭha mā mā gamaḥ putra yamasya sadanaṃ prati 
śvo mayā saha gantāsi jananyā ca samedhitaḥ  RamS 
ubhāv api ca śokārtāv anāthau kṛpaṇau vane 
kṣipram eva gamiṣyāvas tvayā hīnau yamakṣayam  RamS 
tato vaivasvataṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ pravakṣyāmi bhāratīm 
kṣamatāṃ dharmarājo me bibhṛyāt pitarāv ayam  RamS 
apāpo 'si yathā putra nihataḥ pāpakarmaṇā 
tena satyena gacchāśu ye lokāḥ śastrayodhinām  RamS 
yānti śūrā gatiṃ yāṃ ca saṃgrāmeṣv anivartinaḥ 
hatās tv abhimukhāḥ putra gatiṃ tāṃ paramāṃ vraja  RamS 
yāṃ gatiṃ sagaraḥ śaibyo dilīpo janamejayaḥ 
nahuṣo dhundhumāraś ca prāptās tāṃ gaccha putraka  RamS 
yā gatiḥ sarvasādhūnāṃ svādhyāyāt tapasā ca yā 
bhūmidasyāhitāgneś ca ekapatnīvratasya ca  RamS 
gosahasrapradātḥṇāṃ yā yā gurubhṛtām api 
dehanyāsakṛtāṃ yā ca tāṃ gatiṃ gaccha putraka 
na hi tv asmin kule jāto gacchaty akuśalāṃ gatim  RamS 
evaṃ sa kṛpaṇaṃ tatra paryadevayatāsakṛt 
tato 'smai kartum udakaṃ pravṛttaḥ saha bhāryayā  RamS 
sa tu divyena rūpeṇa muniputraḥ svakarmabhiḥ 
āśvāsya ca muhūrtaṃ tu pitarau vākyam abravīt  RamS 
sthānam asmi mahat prāpto bhavatoḥ paricāraṇāt 
bhavantāv api ca kṣipraṃ mama mūlam upaiṣyataḥ  RamS 
evam uktvā tu divyena vimānena vapuṣmatā 
āruroha divaṃ kṣipraṃ muniputro jitendriyaḥ  RamS 
sa kṛtvā tūdakaṃ tūrṇaṃ tāpasaḥ saha bhāryayā 
mām uvāca mahātejāḥ kṛtāñjalim upasthitam  RamS 
adyaiva jahi māṃ rājan maraṇe nāsti me vyathā 
yac chareṇaikaputraṃ māṃ tvam akārṣīr aputrakam  RamS 
tvayā tu yad avijñānān nihato me sutaḥ śuciḥ 
tena tvām abhiśapsyāmi suduḥkham atidāruṇam  RamS 
putravyasanajaṃ duḥkhaṃ yad etan mama sāmpratam 
evaṃ tvaṃ putraśokena rājan kālaṃ kariṣyasi  RamS 
tasmān mām āgataṃ bhadre tasyodārasya tadvacaḥ 
yad ahaṃ putraśokena saṃtyakṣyāmy adya jīvitam  RamS 
yadi māṃ saṃspṛśed rāmaḥ sakṛd adyālabheta vā 
na tan me sadṛśaṃ devi yan mayā rāghave kṛtam  RamS 
cakṣuṣā tvāṃ na paśyāmi smṛtir mama vilupyate 
dūtā vaivasvatasyaite kausalye tvarayanti mām  RamS 
atas tu kiṃ duḥkhataraṃ yad ahaṃ jīvitakṣaye 
na hi paśyāmi dharmajñaṃ rāmaṃ satyaparākramam  RamS 
na te manuṣyā devās te ye cāruśubhakuṇḍalam 
mukhaṃ drakṣyanti rāmasya varṣe pañcadaśe punaḥ  RamS 
padmapattrekṣaṇaṃ subhru sudaṃṣṭraṃ cārunāsikam 
dhanyā drakṣyanti rāmasya tārādhipanibhaṃ mukham  RamS 
sadṛśaṃ śāradasyendoḥ phullasya kamalasya ca 
sugandhi mama nāthasya dhanyā drakṣyanti tanmukham  RamS 
nivṛttavanavāsaṃ tam ayodhyāṃ punar āgatam 
drakṣyanti sukhino rāmaṃ śukraṃ mārgagataṃ yathā  RamS 
ayam ātmabhavaḥ śoko mām anātham acetanam 
saṃsādayati vegena yathā kūlaṃ nadīrayaḥ  RamS 
hā rāghava mahābāho hā mamāyāsanāśana 
rājā daśarathaḥ śocañ jīvitāntam upāgamat  RamS 
tathā tu dīnaṃ kathayan narādhipaḥ priyasya putrasya vivāsanāturaḥ 
gate 'rdharātre bhṛśaduḥkhapīḍitas tadā jahau prāṇam udāradarśanaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
atha rātryāṃ vyatītāyāṃ prātar evāpare 'hani 
bandinaḥ paryupātiṣṭhaṃs tat pārthivaniveśanam  RamS 
tataḥ śucisamācārāḥ paryupasthānakovidāḥ 
strīvarṣavarabhūyiṣṭhā upatasthur yathāpuram  RamS 
haricandanasaṃpṛktam udakaṃ kāñcanair ghaṭaiḥ 
āninyuḥ snānaśikṣājñā yathākālaṃ yathāvidhi  RamS 
maṅgalālambhanīyāni prāśanīyān upaskarān 
upaninyus tathāpy anyāḥ kumārībahulāḥ striyaḥ  RamS 
atha yāḥ kosalendrasya śayanaṃ pratyanantarāḥ 
tāḥ striyas tu samāgamya bhartāraṃ pratyabodhayan  RamS 
tā vepathuparītāś ca rājñaḥ prāṇeṣu śaṅkitāḥ 
pratisrotas tṛṇāgrāṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ saṃcakampire  RamS 
atha saṃvepamānānāṃ strīṇāṃ dṛṣṭvā ca pārthivam 
yat tad āśaṅkitaṃ pāpaṃ tasya jajñe viniścayaḥ  RamS 
tataḥ pracukruśur dīnāḥ sasvaraṃ tā varāṅganāḥ 
kareṇava ivāraṇye sthānapracyutayūthapāḥ  RamS 
tāsām ākrandaśabdena sahasodgatacetane 
kausalyā ca sumitrā ca tyaktanidre babhūvatuḥ  RamS 
kausalyā ca sumitrā ca dṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā ca pārthivam 
hā nātheti parikruśya petatur dharaṇītale  RamS 
sā kosalendraduhitā veṣṭamānā mahītale 
na babhrāja rajodhvastā tāreva gaganacyutā  RamS 
tat samuttrastasaṃbhrāntaṃ paryutsukajanākulam 
sarvatas tumulākrandaṃ paritāpārtabāndhavam  RamS 
sadyo nipatitānandaṃ dīnaviklavadarśanam 
babhūva naradevasya sadma diṣṭāntam īyuṣaḥ  RamS 
atītam ājñāya tu pārthivarṣabhaṃ yaśasvinaṃ saṃparivārya patnayaḥ 
bhṛśaṃ rudantyaḥ karuṇaṃ suduḥkhitāḥ pragṛhya bāhū vyalapann anāthavat  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tam agnim iva saṃśāntam ambuhīnam ivārṇavam 
hataprabham ivādityaṃ svargasthaṃ prekṣya bhūmipam  RamS 
kausalyā bāṣpapūrṇākṣī vividhaṃ śokakarśitā 
upagṛhya śiro rājñaḥ kaikeyīṃ pratyabhāṣata  RamS 
sakāmā bhava kaikeyi bhuṅkṣva rājyam akaṇṭakam 
tyaktvā rājānam ekāgrā nṛśaṃse duṣṭacāriṇi  RamS 
vihāya māṃ gato rāmo bhartā ca svargato mama 
vipathe sārthahīneva nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe  RamS 
bhartāraṃ taṃ parityajya kā strī daivatam ātmanaḥ 
icchej jīvitum anyatra kaikeyyās tyaktadharmaṇaḥ  RamS 
na lubdho budhyate doṣān kiṃ pākam iva bhakṣayan 
kubjānimittaṃ kaikeyyā rāghavāṇāṃ kulaṃ hatam  RamS 
aniyoge niyuktena rājñā rāmaṃ vivāsitam 
sabhāryaṃ janakaḥ śrutvā paritapsyaty ahaṃ yathā  RamS 
rāmaḥ kamalapattrākṣo jīvanāśam ito gataḥ 
videharājasya sutā tathā sītā tapasvinī 
duḥkhasyānucitā duḥkhaṃ vane paryudvijiṣyati  RamS 
nadatāṃ bhīmaghoṣāṇāṃ niśāsu mṛgapakṣiṇām 
niśamya nūnaṃ saṃtrastā rāghavaṃ saṃśrayiṣyati  RamS 
vṛddhaś caivālpaputraś ca vaidehīm anucintayan 
so 'pi śokasamāviṣṭo nanu tyakṣyati jīvitam  RamS 
tāṃ tataḥ sampariṣvajya vilapantīṃ tapasvinīm 
vyapaninyuḥ suduḥkhārtāṃ kausalyāṃ vyāvahārikāḥ  RamS 
tailadroṇyām athāmātyāḥ saṃveśya jagatīpatim 
rājñaḥ sarvāṇy athādiṣṭāś cakruḥ karmāṇy anantaram  RamS 
na tu saṃkālanaṃ rājño vinā putreṇa mantriṇaḥ 
sarvajñāḥ kartum īṣus te tato rakṣanti bhūmipam  RamS 
tailadroṇyāṃ tu sacivaiḥ śāyitaṃ taṃ narādhipam 
hā mṛto 'yam iti jñātvā striyas tāḥ paryadevayan  RamS 
bāhūn udyamya kṛpaṇā netraprasravaṇair mukhaiḥ 
rudantyaḥ śokasaṃtaptāḥ kṛpaṇaṃ paryadevayan  RamS 
niśā nakṣatrahīneva strīva bhartṛvivarjitā 
purī nārājatāyodhyā hīnā rājñā mahātmanā  RamS 
bāṣpaparyākulajanā hāhābhūtakulāṅganā 
śūnyacatvaraveśmāntā na babhrāja yathāpuram  RamS 
gataprabhā dyaur iva bhāskaraṃ vinā vyapetanakṣatragaṇeva śarvarī 
purī babhāse rahitā mahātmanā na cāsrakaṇṭhākulamārgacatvarā  RamS 
narāś ca nāryaś ca sametya saṃghaśo vigarhamāṇā bharatasya mātaram 
tadā nagaryāṃ naradevasaṃkṣaye babhūvur ārtā na ca śarma lebhire  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
vyatītāyāṃ tu śarvaryām ādityasyodaye tataḥ 
sametya rājakartāraḥ sabhām īyur dvijātayaḥ  RamS 
mārkaṇḍeyo 'tha maudgalyo vāmadevaś ca kāśyapaḥ 
kātyāyano gautamaś ca jābāliś ca mahāyaśāḥ  RamS 
ete dvijāḥ sahāmātyaiḥ pṛthag vācam udīrayan 
vasiṣṭham evābhimukhāḥ śreṣṭhaṃ rājapurohitam  RamS 
atītā śarvarī duḥkhaṃ yā no varṣaśatopamā 
asmin pañcatvam āpanne putraśokena pārthive  RamS 
svargataś ca mahārājo rāmaś cāraṇyam āśritaḥ 
lakṣmaṇaś cāpi tejasvī rāmeṇaiva gataḥ saha  RamS 
ubhau bharataśatrughnau kekayeṣu paraṃtapau 
pure rājagṛhe ramye mātāmahaniveśane  RamS 
ikṣvākūṇām ihādyaiva kaścid rājā vidhīyatām 
arājakaṃ hi no rāṣṭraṃ na vināśam avāpnuyāt  RamS 
nārājake janapade vidyunmālī mahāsvanaḥ 
abhivarṣati parjanyo mahīṃ divyena vāriṇā  RamS 
nārājake janapade bījamuṣṭiḥ prakīryate 
nārājake pituḥ putro bhāryā vā vartate vaśe  RamS 
arājake dhanaṃ nāsti nāsti bhāryāpy arājake 
idam atyāhitaṃ cānyat kutaḥ satyam arājake  RamS 
nārājake janapade kārayanti sabhāṃ narāḥ 
udyānāni ca ramyāṇi hṛṣṭāḥ puṇyagṛhāṇi ca  RamS 
nārājake janapade yajñaśīlā dvijātayaḥ 
sattrāṇy anvāsate dāntā brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśitavratāḥ  RamS 
nārājake janapade prabhūtanaṭanartakāḥ 
utsavāś ca samājāś ca vardhante rāṣṭravardhanāḥ  RamS 
nārājake janapade siddhārthā vyavahāriṇaḥ 
kathābhir anurajyante kathāśīlāḥ kathāpriyaiḥ  RamS 
nārājake janapade vāhanaiḥ śīghragāmibhiḥ 
narā niryānty araṇyāni nārībhiḥ saha kāminaḥ  RamS 
nārājake janapade dhanavantaḥ surakṣitāḥ 
śerate vivṛtadvārāḥ kṛṣigorakṣajīvinaḥ  RamS 
nārājake janapade vaṇijo dūragāminaḥ 
gacchanti kṣemam adhvānaṃ bahupuṇyasamācitāḥ  RamS 
nārājake janapade caraty ekacaro vaśī 
bhāvayann ātmanātmānaṃ yatra sāyaṃgṛho muniḥ  RamS 
nārājake janapade yogakṣemaṃ pravartate 
na cāpy arājake senā śatrūn viṣahate yudhi  RamS 
yathā hy anudakā nadyo yathā vāpy atṛṇaṃ vanam 
agopālā yathā gāvas tathā rāṣṭram arājakam  RamS 
nārājake janapade svakaṃ bhavati kasyacit 
matsyā iva narā nityaṃ bhakṣayanti parasparam  RamS 
ye hi saṃbhinnamaryādā nāstikāś chinnasaṃśayāḥ 
te 'pi bhāvāya kalpante rājadaṇḍanipīḍitāḥ  RamS 
aho tama ivedaṃ syān na prajñāyeta kiṃcana 
rājā cen na bhavel loke vibhajan sādhvasādhunī  RamS 
jīvaty api mahārāje tavaiva vacanaṃ vayam 
nātikramāmahe sarve velāṃ prāpyeva sāgaraḥ  RamS 
sa naḥ samīkṣya dvijavaryavṛttaṃ nṛpaṃ vinā rājyam araṇyabhūtam 
kumāram ikṣvākusutaṃ vadānyaṃ tvam eva rājānam ihābhiṣiñca  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyuvāca ha 
mitrāmātyagaṇān sarvān brāhmaṇāṃs tān idaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
yad asau mātulakule pure rājagṛhe sukhī 
bharato vasati bhrātrā śatrughnena samanvitaḥ  RamS 
tac chīghraṃ javanā dūtā gacchantu tvaritair hayaiḥ 
ānetuṃ bhrātarau vīrau kiṃ samīkṣāmahe vayam  RamS 
gacchantv iti tataḥ sarve vasiṣṭhaṃ vākyam abruvan 
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vasiṣṭho vākyam abravīt  RamS 
ehi siddhārtha vijaya jayantāśokanandana 
śrūyatām itikartavyaṃ sarvān eva bravīmi vaḥ  RamS 
puraṃ rājagṛhaṃ gatvā śīghraṃ śīghrajavair hayaiḥ 
tyaktaśokair idaṃ vācyaḥ śāsanād bharato mama  RamS 
purohitas tvāṃ kuśalaṃ prāha sarve ca mantriṇaḥ 
tvaramāṇaś ca niryāhi kṛtyam ātyayikaṃ tvayā  RamS 
mā cāsmai proṣitaṃ rāmaṃ mā cāsmai pitaraṃ mṛtam 
bhavantaḥ śaṃsiṣur gatvā rāghavāṇām imaṃ kṣayam  RamS 
kauśeyāni ca vastrāṇi bhūṣaṇāni varāṇi ca 
kṣipram ādāya rājñaś ca bharatasya ca gacchata 
vasiṣṭhenābhyanujñātā dūtāḥ saṃtvaritā yayuḥ  RamS 
te hastinapure gaṅgāṃ tīrtvā pratyaṅmukhā yayuḥ 
pāñcāladeśam āsādya madhyena kurujāṅgalam  RamS 
te prasannodakāṃ divyāṃ nānāvihagasevitām 
upātijagmur vegena śaradaṇḍāṃ janākulām  RamS 
nikūlavṛkṣam āsādya divyaṃ satyopayācanam 
abhigamyābhivādyaṃ taṃ kuliṅgāṃ prāviśan purīm  RamS 
abhikālaṃ tataḥ prāpya tejo'bhibhavanāc cyutāḥ 
yayur madhyena vāhlīkān sudāmānaṃ ca parvatam 
viṣṇoḥ padaṃ prekṣamāṇā vipāśāṃ cāpi śālmalīm  RamS 
te śrāntavāhanā dūtā vikṛṣṭena satā pathā 
girivrajaṃ puravaraṃ śīghram āsedur añjasā  RamS 
bhartuḥ priyārthaṃ kularakṣaṇārthaṃ bhartuś ca vaṃśasya parigrahārtham 
aheḍamānās tvarayā sma dūtā rātryāṃ tu te tat puram eva yātāḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
yām eva rātriṃ te dūtāḥ praviśanti sma tāṃ purīm 
bharatenāpi tāṃ rātriṃ svapno dṛṣṭo 'yam apriyaḥ  RamS 
vyuṣṭām eva tu tāṃ rātriṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ svapnam apriyam 
putro rājādhirājasya subhṛśaṃ paryatapyata  RamS 
tapyamānaṃ samājñāya vayasyāḥ priyavādinaḥ 
āyāsaṃ hi vineṣyantaḥ sabhāyāṃ cakrire kathāḥ  RamS 
vādayanti tathā śāntiṃ lāsayanty api cāpare 
nāṭakāny apare prāhur hāsyāni vividhāni ca  RamS 
sa tair mahātmā bharataḥ sakhibhiḥ priyavādibhiḥ 
goṣṭhīhāsyāni kurvadbhir na prāhṛṣyata rāghavaḥ  RamS 
tam abravīt priyasakho bharataṃ sakhibhir vṛtam 
suhṛdbhiḥ paryupāsīnaḥ kiṃ sakhe nānumodase  RamS 
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ suhṛdaṃ bharataḥ pratyuvāca ha 
śṛṇu tvaṃ yannimittaṃ me dainyam etad upāgatam  RamS 
svapne pitaram adrākṣaṃ malinaṃ muktamūrdhajam 
patantam adriśikharāt kaluṣe gomayahrade  RamS 
plavamānaś ca me dṛṣṭaḥ sa tasmin gomayahrade 
pibann añjalinā tailaṃ hasann iva muhur muhuḥ  RamS 
tatas tilodanaṃ bhuktvā punaḥ punar adhaḥśirāḥ 
tailenābhyaktasarvāṅgas tailam evāvagāhata  RamS 
svapne 'pi sāgaraṃ śuṣkaṃ candraṃ ca patitaṃ bhuvi 
sahasā cāpi saṃśāntaṃ jvalitaṃ jātavedasam  RamS 
avadīrṇāṃ ca pṛthivīṃ śuṣkāṃś ca vividhān drumān 
ahaṃ paśyāmi vidhvastān sadhūmāṃś caiva parvatān  RamS 
pīṭhe kārṣṇāyase cainaṃ niṣaṇṇaṃ kṛṣṇavāsasam 
prahasanti sma rājānaṃ pramadāḥ kṛṣṇapiṅgalāḥ  RamS 
tvaramāṇaś ca dharmātmā raktamālyānulepanaḥ 
rathena kharayuktena prayāto dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  RamS 
evam etan mayā dṛṣṭam imāṃ rātriṃ bhayāvahām 
ahaṃ rāmo 'tha vā rājā lakṣmaṇo vā mariṣyati  RamS 
naro yānena yaḥ svapne kharayuktena yāti hi 
acirāt tasya dhūmāgraṃ citāyāṃ sampradṛśyate 
etannimittaṃ dīno 'haṃ tan na vaḥ pratipūjaye  RamS 
śuṣyatīva ca me kaṇṭho na svastham iva me manaḥ 
jugupsann iva cātmānaṃ na ca paśyāmi kāraṇam  RamS 
imāṃ hi duḥsvapnagatiṃ niśāmya tām anekarūpām avitarkitāṃ purā 
bhayaṃ mahat taddhṛdayān na yāti me vicintya rājānam acintyadarśanam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
bharate bruvati svapnaṃ dūtās te klāntavāhanāḥ 
praviśyāsahyaparikhaṃ ramyaṃ rājagṛhaṃ puram  RamS 
samāgamya tu rājñā ca rājaputreṇa cārcitāḥ 
rājñaḥ pādau gṛhītvā tu tam ūcur bharataṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
purohitas tvā kuśalaṃ prāha sarve ca mantriṇaḥ 
tvaramāṇaś ca niryāhi kṛtyam ātyayikaṃ tvayā  RamS 
atra viṃśatikoṭyas tu nṛpater mātulasya te 
daśakoṭyas tu sampūrṇās tathaiva ca nṛpātmaja  RamS 
pratigṛhya ca tat sarvaṃ svanuraktaḥ suhṛjjane 
dūtān uvāca bharataḥ kāmaiḥ sampratipūjya tān  RamS 
kaccit sukuśalī rājā pitā daśaratho mama 
kaccic cārogatā rāme lakṣmaṇe vā mahātmani  RamS 
āryā ca dharmaniratā dharmajñā dharmadarśinī 
arogā cāpi kausalyā mātā rāmasya dhīmataḥ  RamS 
kaccit sumitrā dharmajñā jananī lakṣmaṇasya yā 
śatrughnasya ca vīrasya sārogā cāpi madhyamā  RamS 
ātmakāmā sadā caṇḍī krodhanā prājñamāninī 
arogā cāpi kaikeyī mātā me kim uvāca ha  RamS 
evam uktās tu te dūtā bharatena mahātmanā 
ūcuḥ sampraśritaṃ vākyam idaṃ taṃ bharataṃ tadā 
kuśalās te naravyāghra yeṣāṃ kuśalam icchasi  RamS 
bharataś cāpi tān dūtān evam ukto 'bhyabhāṣata 
āpṛcche 'haṃ mahārājaṃ dūtāḥ saṃtvarayanti mām  RamS 
evam uktvā tu tān dūtān bharataḥ pārthivātmajaḥ 
dūtaiḥ saṃcodito vākyaṃ mātāmaham uvāca ha  RamS 
rājan pitur gamiṣyāmi sakāśaṃ dūtacoditaḥ 
punar apy aham eṣyāmi yadā me tvaṃ smariṣyasi  RamS 
bharatenaivam uktas tu nṛpo mātāmahas tadā 
tam uvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ śirasy āghrāya rāghavam  RamS 
gaccha tātānujāne tvāṃ kaikeyī suprajās tvayā 
mātaraṃ kuśalaṃ brūyāḥ pitaraṃ ca paraṃtapa  RamS 
purohitaṃ ca kuśalaṃ ye cānye dvijasattamāḥ 
tau ca tāta maheṣvāsau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau  RamS 
tasmai hastyuttamāṃś citrān kambalān ajināni ca 
abhisatkṛtya kaikeyo bharatāya dhanaṃ dadau  RamS 
rukmaniṣkasahasre dve ṣoḍaśāśvaśatāni ca 
satkṛtya kaikeyī putraṃ kekayo dhanam ādiśat  RamS 
tathāmātyān abhipretān viśvāsyāṃś ca guṇānvitān 
dadāv aśvapatiḥ śīghraṃ bharatāyānuyāyinaḥ  RamS 
airāvatān aindraśirān nāgān vai priyadarśanān 
kharāñ śīghrān susaṃyuktān mātulo 'smai dhanaṃ dadau  RamS 
antaḥpure 'tisaṃvṛddhān vyāghravīryabalānvitān 
daṃṣṭrāyudhān mahākāyāñ śunaś copāyanaṃ dadau  RamS 
sa mātāmaham āpṛcchya mātulaṃ ca yudhājitam 
ratham āruhya bharataḥ śatrughnasahito yayau  RamS 
rathān maṇḍalacakrāṃś ca yojayitvā paraḥśatam 
uṣṭrago'śvakharair bhṛtyā bharataṃ yāntam anvayuḥ  RamS 
balena gupto bharato mahātmā sahāryakasyātmasamair amātyaiḥ 
ādāya śatrughnam apetaśatrur gṛhād yayau siddha ivendralokāt  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
sa prāṅmukho rājagṛhād abhiniryāya vīryavān 
hrādinīṃ dūrapārāṃ ca pratyaksrotastaraṃgiṇīm 
śatadrūm atarac chrīmān nadīm ikṣvākunandanaḥ  RamS 
elādhāne nadīṃ tīrtvā prāpya cāparaparpaṭān 
śilām ākurvatīṃ tīrtvā āgneyaṃ śalyakartanam  RamS 
satyasaṃdhaḥ śuciḥ śrīmān prekṣamāṇaḥ śilāvahām 
atyayāt sa mahāśailān vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ prati  RamS 
veginīṃ ca kuliṅgākhyāṃ hrādinīṃ parvatāvṛtām 
yamunāṃ prāpya saṃtīrṇo balam āśvāsayat tadā  RamS 
śītīkṛtya tu gātrāṇi klāntān āśvāsya vājinaḥ 
tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca prāyād ādāya codakam  RamS 
rājaputro mahāraṇyam anabhīkṣṇopasevitam 
bhadro bhadreṇa yānena mārutaḥ kham ivātyayāt  RamS 
toraṇaṃ dakṣiṇārdhena jambūprastham upāgamat 
varūthaṃ ca yayau ramyaṃ grāmaṃ daśarathātmajaḥ  RamS 
tatra ramye vane vāsaṃ kṛtvāsau prāṅmukho yayau 
udyānam ujjihānāyāḥ priyakā yatra pādapāḥ  RamS 
sālāṃs tu priyakān prāpya śīghrān āsthāya vājinaḥ 
anujñāpyātha bharato vāhinīṃ tvarito yayau  RamS 
vāsaṃ kṛtvā sarvatīrthe tīrtvā cottānikāṃ nadīm 
anyā nadīś ca vividhāḥ pārvatīyais turaṃgamaiḥ  RamS 
hastipṛṣṭhakam āsādya kuṭikām atyavartata 
tatāra ca naravyāghro lauhitye sa kapīvatīm 
ekasāle sthāṇumatīṃ vinate gomatīṃ nadīm  RamS 
kaliṅganagare cāpi prāpya sālavanaṃ tadā 
bharataḥ kṣipram āgacchat supariśrāntavāhanaḥ  RamS 
vanaṃ ca samatītyāśu śarvaryām aruṇodaye 
ayodhyāṃ manunā rājñā nirmitāṃ sa dadarśa ha  RamS 
tāṃ purīṃ puruṣavyāghraḥ saptarātroṣiṭaḥ pathi 
ayodhyām agrato dṛṣṭvā rathe sārathim abravīt  RamS 
eṣā nātipratītā me puṇyodyānā yaśasvinī 
ayodhyā dṛśyate dūrāt sārathe pāṇḍumṛttikā  RamS 
yajvabhir guṇasampannair brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ 
bhūyiṣṭham ṛddhair ākīrṇā rājarṣivarapālitā  RamS 
ayodhyāyāṃ purā śabdaḥ śrūyate tumulo mahān 
samantān naranārīṇāṃ tam adya na śṛṇomy aham  RamS 
udyānāni hi sāyāhne krīḍitvoparatair naraiḥ 
samantād vipradhāvadbhiḥ prakāśante mamānyadā  RamS 
tāny adyānurudantīva parityaktāni kāmibhiḥ 
araṇyabhūteva purī sārathe pratibhāti me  RamS 
na hy atra yānair dṛśyante na gajair na ca vājibhiḥ 
niryānto vābhiyānto vā naramukhyā yathāpuram  RamS 
aniṣṭāni ca pāpāni paśyāmi vividhāni ca 
nimittāny amanojñāni tena sīdati me manaḥ  RamS 
dvāreṇa vaijayantena prāviśac chrāntavāhanaḥ 
dvāḥsthair utthāya vijayaṃ pṛṣṭas taiḥ sahito yayau  RamS 
sa tv anekāgrahṛdayo dvāḥsthaṃ pratyarcya taṃ janam 
sūtam aśvapateḥ klāntam abravīt tatra rāghavaḥ  RamS 
śrutā no yādṛśāḥ pūrvaṃ nṛpatīnāṃ vināśane 
ākārās tān ahaṃ sarvān iha paśyāmi sārathe  RamS 
malinaṃ cāśrupūrṇākṣaṃ dīnaṃ dhyānaparaṃ kṛśam 
sastrīpuṃsaṃ ca paśyāmi janam utkaṇṭhitaṃ pure  RamS 
ity evam uktvā bharataḥ sūtaṃ taṃ dīnamānasaḥ 
tāny aniṣṭāny ayodhyāyāṃ prekṣya rājagṛhaṃ yayau 
tāṃ śūnyaśṛṅgāṭakaveśmarathyāṃ rajo'ruṇadvārakapāṭayantrām  RamS 
dṛṣṭvā purīm indrapurīprakāśāṃ duḥkhena sampūrṇataro babhūva 
bahūni paśyan manaso 'priyāṇi yāny anyadā nāsya pure babhūvuḥ 
avākśirā dīnamanā na hṛṣṭaḥ pitur mahātmā praviveśa veśma  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
apaśyaṃs tu tatas tatra pitaraṃ pitur ālaye 
jagāma bharato draṣṭuṃ mātaraṃ mātur ālaye  RamS 
anuprāptaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā kaikeyī proṣitaṃ sutam 
utpapāta tadā hṛṣṭā tyaktvā sauvarṇamānasam  RamS 
sa praviśyaiva dharmātmā svagṛhaṃ śrīvivarjitam 
bharataḥ prekṣya jagrāha jananyāś caraṇau śubhau  RamS 
taṃ mūrdhni samupāghrāya pariṣvajya yaśasvinam 
aṅke bharatam āropya praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame  RamS 
adya te katicid rātryaś cyutasyāryakaveśmanaḥ 
api nādhvaśramaḥ śīghraṃ rathenāpatatas tava  RamS 
āryakas te sukuśalī yudhājin mātulas tava 
pravāsāc ca sukhaṃ putra sarvaṃ me vaktum arhasi  RamS 
evaṃ pṛṣṭas tu kaikeyyā priyaṃ pārthivanandanaḥ 
ācaṣṭa bharataḥ sarvaṃ mātre rājīvalocanaḥ  RamS 
adya me saptamī rātriś cyutasyāryakaveśmanaḥ 
ambāyāḥ kuśalī tāto yudhājin mātulaś ca me  RamS 
yan me dhanaṃ ca ratnaṃ ca dadau rājā paraṃtapaḥ 
pariśrāntaṃ pathy abhavat tato 'haṃ pūrvam āgataḥ  RamS 
rājavākyaharair dūtais tvaryamāṇo 'ham āgataḥ 
yad ahaṃ praṣṭum icchāmi tad ambā vaktum arhati  RamS 
śūnyo 'yaṃ śayanīyas te paryaṅko hemabhūṣitaḥ 
na cāyam ikṣvākujanaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ pratibhāti me  RamS 
rājā bhavati bhūyiṣṭham ihāmbāyā niveśane 
tam ahaṃ nādya paśyāmi draṣṭum icchann ihāgataḥ  RamS 
pitur grahīṣye caraṇau taṃ mamākhyāhi pṛcchataḥ 
āhosvid amba jyeṣṭhāyāḥ kausalyāyā niveśane  RamS 
taṃ pratyuvāca kaikeyī priyavad ghoram apriyam 
ajānantaṃ prajānantī rājyalobhena mohitā 
yā gatiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ te pitā gataḥ  RamS 
tac chrutvā bharato vākyaṃ dharmābhijanavāñ śuciḥ 
papāta sahasā bhūmau pitṛśokabalārditaḥ  RamS 
tataḥ śokena saṃvītaḥ pitur maraṇaduḥkhitaḥ 
vilalāpa mahātejā bhrāntākulitacetanaḥ  RamS 
etat suruciraṃ bhāti pitur me śayanaṃ purā 
tad idaṃ na vibhāty adya vihīnaṃ tena dhīmatā  RamS 
tam ārtaṃ devasaṃkāśaṃ samīkṣya patitaṃ bhuvi 
utthāpayitvā śokārtaṃ vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  RamS 
uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha kiṃ śeṣe rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ 
tvadvidhā na hi śocanti santaḥ sadasi saṃmatāḥ  RamS 
sa ruditvā ciraṃ kālaṃ bhūmau viparivṛtya ca 
jananīṃ pratyuvācedaṃ śokair bahubhir āvṛtaḥ  RamS 
abhiṣekṣyati rāmaṃ tu rājā yajñaṃ nu yakṣyati 
ity ahaṃ kṛtasaṃkalpo hṛṣṭo yātrām ayāsiṣam  RamS 
tad idaṃ hy anyathā bhūtaṃ vyavadīrṇaṃ mano mama 
pitaraṃ yo na paśyāmi nityaṃ priyahite ratam  RamS 
amba kenātyagād rājā vyādhinā mayy anāgate 
dhanyā rāmādayaḥ sarve yaiḥ pitā saṃskṛtaḥ svayam  RamS 
na nūnaṃ māṃ mahārājaḥ prāptaṃ jānāti kīrtimān 
upajighreddhi māṃ mūrdhni tātaḥ saṃnamya satvaram  RamS 
kva sa pāṇiḥ sukhasparśas tātasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ 
yena māṃ rajasā dhvastam abhīkṣṇaṃ parimārjati  RamS 
yo me bhrātā pitā bandhur yasya dāso 'smi dhīmataḥ 
tasya māṃ śīghram ākhyāhi rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ  RamS 
pitā hi bhavati jyeṣṭho dharmam āryasya jānataḥ 
tasya pādau grahīṣyāmi sa hīdānīṃ gatir mama  RamS 
ārye kim abravīd rājā pitā me satyavikramaḥ 
paścimaṃ sādhusaṃdeśam icchāmi śrotum ātmanaḥ  RamS 
iti pṛṣṭā yathātattvaṃ kaikeyī vākyam abravīt 
rāmeti rājā vilapan hā sīte lakṣmaṇeti ca 
sa mahātmā paraṃ lokaṃ gato gatimatāṃ varaḥ  RamS 
imāṃ tu paścimāṃ vācaṃ vyājahāra pitā tava 
kāladharmaparikṣiptaḥ pāśair iva mahāgajaḥ  RamS 
siddhārthās tu narā rāmam āgataṃ sītayā saha 
lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābāhuṃ drakṣyanti punar āgatam  RamS 
tac chrutvā viṣasādaiva dvitīyāpriyaśaṃsanāt 
viṣaṇṇavadano bhūtvā bhūyaḥ papraccha mātaram  RamS 
kva cedānīṃ sa dharmātmā kausalyānandavardhanaḥ 
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā sītayā ca samaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
tathā pṛṣṭā yathātattvam ākhyātum upacakrame 
mātāsya yugapad vākyaṃ vipriyaṃ priyaśaṅkayā  RamS 
sa hi rājasutaḥ putra cīravāsā mahāvanam 
daṇḍakān saha vaidehyā lakṣmaṇānucaro gataḥ  RamS 
tac chrutvā bharatas trasto bhrātuś cāritraśaṅkayā 
svasya vaṃśasya māhātmyāt praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame  RamS 
kaccin na brāhmaṇadhanaṃ hṛtaṃ rāmeṇa kasyacit 
kaccin nāḍhyo daridro vā tenāpāpo vihiṃsitaḥ  RamS 
kaccin na paradārān vā rājaputro 'bhimanyate 
kasmāt sa daṇḍakāraṇye bhrūṇaheva vivāsitaḥ  RamS 
athāsya capalā mātā tat svakarma yathātatham 
tenaiva strīsvabhāvena vyāhartum upacakrame  RamS 
na brāhmaṇadhanaṃ kiṃciddhṛtaṃ rāmeṇa kasyacit 
kaścin nāḍhyo daridro vā tenāpāpo vihiṃsitaḥ 
na rāmaḥ paradārāṃś ca cakṣurbhyām api paśyati  RamS 
mayā tu putra śrutvaiva rāmasyaivābhiṣecanam 
yācitas te pitā rājyaṃ rāmasya ca vivāsanam  RamS 
sa svavṛttiṃ samāsthāya pitā te tat tathākarot 
rāmaś ca sahasaumitriḥ preṣitaḥ saha sītayā  RamS 
tam apaśyan priyaṃ putraṃ mahīpālo mahāyaśāḥ 
putraśokaparidyūnaḥ pañcatvam upapedivān  RamS 
tvayā tv idānīṃ dharmajña rājatvam avalambyatām 
tvatkṛte hi mayā sarvam idam evaṃvidhaṃ kṛtam  RamS 
tat putra śīghraṃ vidhinā vidhijñair vasiṣṭhamukhyaiḥ sahito dvijendraiḥ 
saṃkālya rājānam adīnasattvam ātmānam urvyām abhiṣecayasva  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
śrutvā tu pitaraṃ vṛttaṃ bhrātarau ca vivāsitau 
bharato duḥkhasaṃtapta idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
kiṃ nu kāryaṃ hatasyeha mama rājyena śocataḥ 
vihīnasyātha pitrā ca bhrātrā pitṛsamena ca  RamS 
duḥkhe me duḥkham akaror vraṇe kṣāram ivādadhāḥ 
rājānaṃ pretabhāvasthaṃ kṛtvā rāmaṃ ca tāpasam  RamS 
kulasya tvam abhāvāya kālarātrir ivāgatā 
aṅgāram upagūhya sma pitā me nāvabuddhavān  RamS 
kausalyā ca sumitrā ca putraśokābhipīḍite 
duṣkaraṃ yadi jīvetāṃ prāpya tvāṃ jananīṃ mama  RamS 
nanu tv āryo 'pi dharmātmā tvayi vṛttim anuttamām 
vartate guruvṛttijño yathā mātari vartate  RamS 
tathā jyeṣṭhā hi me mātā kausalyā dīrghadarśinī 
tvayi dharmaṃ samāsthāya bhaginyām iva vartate  RamS 
tasyāḥ putraṃ kṛtātmānaṃ cīravalkalavāsasam 
prasthāpya vanavāsāya kathaṃ pāpe na śocasi  RamS 
apāpadarśinaṃ śūraṃ kṛtātmānaṃ yaśasvinam 
pravrājya cīravasanaṃ kiṃ nu paśyasi kāraṇam  RamS 
lubdhāyā vidito manye na te 'haṃ rāghavaṃ prati 
tathā hy anartho rājyārthaṃ tvayā nīto mahān ayam  RamS 
ahaṃ hi puruṣavyāghrāv apaśyan rāmalakṣmaṇau 
kena śaktiprabhāvena rājyaṃ rakṣitum utsahe  RamS 
taṃ hi nityaṃ mahārājo balavantaṃ mahābalaḥ 
apāśrito 'bhūd dharmātmā merur meruvanaṃ yathā  RamS 
so 'haṃ katham imaṃ bhāraṃ mahādhuryasamudyatam 
damyo dhuram ivāsādya saheyaṃ kena caujasā  RamS 
atha vā me bhavec chaktir yogair buddhibalena vā 
sakāmāṃ na kariṣyāmi tvām ahaṃ putragardhinīm 
nivartayiṣyāmi vanād bhrātaraṃ svajanapriyam  RamS 
ity evam uktvā bharato mahātmā priyetarair vākyagaṇais tudaṃs tām 
śokāturaś cāpi nanāda bhūyaḥ siṃho yathā parvatagahvarasthaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tāṃ tathā garhayitvā tu mātaraṃ bharatas tadā 
roṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ punar evābravīd vacaḥ  RamS 
rājyād bhraṃśasva kaikeyi nṛśaṃse duṣṭacāriṇi 
parityaktā ca dharmeṇa mā mṛtaṃ rudatī bhava  RamS 
kiṃ nu te 'dūṣayad rājā rāmo vā bhṛśadhārmikaḥ 
yayor mṛtyur vivāsaś ca tvatkṛte tulyam āgatau  RamS 
bhrūṇahatyām asi prāptā kulasyāsya vināśanāt 
kaikeyi narakaṃ gaccha mā ca bhartuḥ salokatām  RamS 
yat tvayā hīdṛśaṃ pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ ghoreṇa karmaṇā 
sarvalokapriyaṃ hitvā mamāpy āpāditaṃ bhayam  RamS 
tvatkṛte me pitā vṛtto rāmaś cāraṇyam āśritaḥ 
ayaśo jīvaloke ca tvayāhaṃ pratipāditaḥ  RamS 
mātṛrūpe mamāmitre nṛśaṃse rājyakāmuke 
na te 'ham abhibhāṣyo 'smi durvṛtte patighātini  RamS 
kausalyā ca sumitrā ca yāś cānyā mama mātaraḥ 
duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭās tvāṃ prāpya kuladūṣiṇīm  RamS 
na tvam aśvapateḥ kanyā dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ 
rākṣasī tatra jātāsi kulapradhvaṃsinī pituḥ  RamS 
yat tvayā dhārmiko rāmo nityaṃ satyaparāyaṇaḥ 
vanaṃ prasthāpito duḥkhāt pitā ca tridivaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
yatpradhānāsi tat pāpaṃ mayi pitrā vinākṛte 
bhrātṛbhyāṃ ca parityakte sarvalokasya cāpriye  RamS 
kausalyāṃ dharmasaṃyuktāṃ viyuktāṃ pāpaniścaye 
kṛtvā kaṃ prāpsyase tv adya lokaṃ nirayagāminī  RamS 
kiṃ nāvabudhyase krūre niyataṃ bandhusaṃśrayam 
jyeṣṭhaṃ pitṛsamaṃ rāmaṃ kausalyāyā ātmasambhavam  RamS 
aṅgapratyaṅgajaḥ putro hṛdayāc cāpi jāyate 
tasmāt priyataro mātuḥ priyatvān na tu bāndhavaḥ  RamS 
anyadā kila dharmajñā surabhiḥ surasaṃmatā 
vahamānau dadarśorvyāṃ putrau vigatacetasau  RamS 
tāv ardhadivase śrāntau dṛṣṭvā putrau mahītale 
ruroda putraśokena bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇā  RamS 
adhastād vrajatas tasyāḥ surarājño mahātmanaḥ 
bindavaḥ patitā gātre sūkṣmāḥ surabhigandhinaḥ  RamS 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā śokasaṃtaptāṃ vajrapāṇir yaśasvinīm 
indraḥ prāñjalir udvignaḥ surarājo 'bravīd vacaḥ  RamS 
bhayaṃ kaccin na cāsmāsu kutaścid vidyate mahat 
kutonimittaḥ śokas te brūhi sarvahitaiṣiṇi  RamS 
evam uktā tu surabhiḥ surarājena dhīmatā 
pratyuvāca tato dhīrā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradā  RamS 
śāntaṃ pāpaṃ na vaḥ kiṃcit kutaścid amarādhipa 
ahaṃ tu magnau śocāmi svaputrau viṣame sthitau  RamS 
etau dṛṣṭvā kṛṣau dīnau sūryaraśmipratāpinau 
ardyamānau balīvardau karṣakeṇa surādhipa  RamS 
mama kāyāt prasūtau hi duḥkhitau bhārapīḍitau 
yau dṛṣṭvā paritapye 'haṃ nāsti putrasamaḥ priyaḥ  RamS 
yasyāḥ putrasahasrāṇi sāpi śocati kāmadhuk 
kiṃ punar yā vinā rāmaṃ kausalyā vartayiṣyati  RamS 
ekaputrā ca sādhvī ca vivatseyaṃ tvayā kṛtā 
tasmāt tvaṃ satataṃ duḥkhaṃ pretya ceha ca lapsyase  RamS 
ahaṃ hy apacitiṃ bhrātuḥ pituś ca sakalām imām 
vardhanaṃ yaśasaś cāpi kariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ  RamS 
ānāyayitvā tanayaṃ kausalyāyā mahādyutim 
svayam eva pravekṣyāmi vanaṃ muniniṣevitam  RamS 
iti nāga ivāraṇye tomarāṅkuśacoditaḥ 
papāta bhuvi saṃkruddho niḥśvasann iva pannagaḥ  RamS 
saṃraktanetraḥ śithilāmbaras tadā vidhūtasarvābharaṇaḥ paraṃtapaḥ 
babhūva bhūmau patito nṛpātmajaḥ śacīpateḥ ketur ivotsavakṣaye  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tathaiva krośatas tasya bharatasya mahātmanaḥ 
kausalyā śabdam ājñāya sumitrām idam abravīt  RamS 
āgataḥ krūrakāryāyāḥ kaikeyyā bharataḥ sutaḥ 
tam ahaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi bharataṃ dīrghadarśinam  RamS 
evam uktvā sumitrāṃ sā vivarṇā malināmbarā 
pratasthe bharato yatra vepamānā vicetanā  RamS 
sa tu rāmānujaś cāpi śatrughnasahitas tadā 
pratasthe bharato yatra kausalyāyā niveśanam  RamS 
tataḥ śatrughnabharatau kausalyāṃ prekṣya duḥkhitau 
paryaṣvajetāṃ duḥkhārtāṃ patitāṃ naṣṭacetanām  RamS 
bharataṃ pratyuvācedaṃ kausalyā bhṛśaduḥkhitā 
idaṃ te rājyakāmasya rājyaṃ prāptam akaṇṭakam 
samprāptaṃ bata kaikeyyā śīghraṃ krūreṇa karmaṇā  RamS 
prasthāpya cīravasanaṃ putraṃ me vanavāsinam 
kaikeyī kaṃ guṇaṃ tatra paśyati krūradarśinī  RamS 
kṣipraṃ mām api kaikeyī prasthāpayitum arhati 
hiraṇyanābho yatrāste suto me sumahāyaśāḥ  RamS 
atha vā svayam evāhaṃ sumitrānucarā sukham 
agnihotraṃ puraskṛtya prasthāsye yatra rāghavaḥ  RamS 
kāmaṃ vā svayam evādya tatra māṃ netum arhasi 
yatrāsau puruṣavyāghras tapyate me tapaḥ sutaḥ  RamS 
idaṃ hi tava vistīrṇaṃ dhanadhānyasamācitam 
hastyaśvarathasampūrṇaṃ rājyaṃ niryātitaṃ tayā  RamS 
evaṃ vilapamānāṃ tāṃ bharataḥ prāñjalis tadā 
kausalyāṃ pratyuvācedaṃ śokair bahubhir āvṛtām  RamS 
ārye kasmād ajānantaṃ garhase mām akilbiṣam 
vipulāṃ ca mama prītiṃ sthirāṃ jānāsi rāghave  RamS 
kṛtā śāstrānugā buddhir mā bhūt tasya kadācana 
satyasaṃdhaḥ satāṃ śreṣṭho yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
praiṣyaṃ pāpīyasāṃ yātu sūryaṃ ca prati mehatu 
hantu pādena gāṃ suptāṃ yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
kārayitvā mahat karma bhartā bhṛtyam anarthakam 
adharmo yo 'sya so 'syās tu yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
paripālayamānasya rājño bhūtāni putravat 
tatas tu druhyatāṃ pāpaṃ yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
baliṣaḍbhāgam uddhṛtya nṛpasyārakṣataḥ prajāḥ 
adharmo yo 'sya so 'syāstu yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
saṃśrutya ca tapasvibhyaḥ sattre vai yajñadakṣiṇām 
tāṃ vipralapatāṃ pāpaṃ yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
hastyaśvarathasambādhe yuddhe śastrasamākule 
mā sma kārṣīt satāṃ dharmaṃ yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
upadiṣṭaṃ susūkṣmārthaṃ śāstraṃ yatnena dhīmatā 
sa nāśayatu duṣṭātmā yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
pāyasaṃ kṛsaraṃ chāgaṃ vṛthā so 'śnātu nirghṛṇaḥ 
gurūṃś cāpy avajānātu yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
putrair dāraiś ca bhṛtyaiś ca svagṛhe parivāritaḥ 
sa eko mṛṣṭam aśnātu yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
rājastrībālavṛddhānāṃ vadhe yat pāpam ucyate 
bhṛtyatyāge ca yat pāpaṃ tat pāpaṃ pratipadyatām  RamS 
ubhe saṃdhye śayānasya yat pāpaṃ parikalpyate 
tac ca pāpaṃ bhavet tasya yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
yad agnidāyake pāpaṃ yat pāpaṃ gurutalpage 
mitradrohe ca yat pāpaṃ tat pāpaṃ pratipadyatām  RamS 
devatānāṃ pitḥṇāṃ ca mātāpitros tathaiva ca 
mā sma kārṣīt sa śuśrūṣāṃ yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
satāṃ lokāt satāṃ kīrtyāḥ sajjuṣṭāt karmaṇas tathā 
bhraśyatu kṣipram adyaiva yasyāryo 'numate gataḥ  RamS 
vihīnāṃ patiputrābhyāṃ kausalyāṃ pārthivātmajaḥ 
evam āśvāsayann eva duḥkhārto nipapāta ha  RamS 
tathā tu śapathaiḥ kaṣṭaiḥ śapamānam acetanam 
bharataṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ kausalyā vākyam abravīt  RamS 
mama duḥkham idaṃ putra bhūyaḥ samupajāyate 
śapathaiḥ śapamāno hi prāṇān uparuṇatsi me  RamS 
diṣṭyā na calito dharmād ātmā te sahalakṣmaṇaḥ 
vatsa satyapratijño me satāṃ lokān avāpsyasi  RamS 
evaṃ vilapamānasya duḥkhārtasya mahātmanaḥ 
mohāc ca śokasaṃrodhād babhūva lulitaṃ manaḥ  RamS 
lālapyamānasya vicetanasya pranaṣṭabuddheḥ patitasya bhūmau 
muhur muhur niḥśvasataś ca dīrghaṃ sā tasya śokena jagāma rātriḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tam evaṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ bharataṃ kekayīsutam 
uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho vasiṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhavāg ṛṣiḥ  RamS 
alaṃ śokena bhadraṃ te rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ 
prāptakālaṃ narapateḥ kuru saṃyānam uttaram  RamS 
vasiṣṭhasya vacaḥ śrutvā bharato dhāraṇāṃ gataḥ 
pretakāryāṇi sarvāṇi kārayāmāsa dharmavit  RamS 
uddhṛtaṃ tailasaṃkledāt sa tu bhūmau niveśitam 
āpītavarṇavadanaṃ prasuptam iva bhūmipam  RamS 
niveśya śayane cāgrye nānāratnapariṣkṛte 
tato daśarathaṃ putro vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ  RamS 
kiṃ te vyavasitaṃ rājan proṣite mayy anāgate 
vivāsya rāmaṃ dharmajñaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābalam  RamS 
kva yāsyasi mahārāja hitvemaṃ duḥkhitaṃ janam 
hīnaṃ puruṣasiṃhena rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā  RamS 
yogakṣemaṃ tu te rājan ko 'smin kalpayitā pure 
tvayi prayāte svas tāta rāme ca vanam āśrite  RamS 
vidhavā pṛthivī rājaṃs tvayā hīnā na rājate 
hīnacandreva rajanī nagarī pratibhāti mām  RamS 
evaṃ vilapamānaṃ taṃ bharataṃ dīnamānasam 
abravīd vacanaṃ bhūyo vasiṣṭhas tu mahān ṛṣiḥ  RamS 
pretakāryāṇi yāny asya kartavyāni viśāṃpateḥ 
tāny avyagraṃ mahābāho kriyantām avicāritam  RamS 
tatheti bharato vākyaṃ vasiṣṭhasyābhipūjya tat 
ṛtvikpurohitācāryāṃs tvarayāmāsa sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
ye tv agrato narendrasya agnyagārād bahiṣkṛtāḥ 
ṛtvigbhir yājakaiś caiva te hriyante yathāvidhi  RamS 
śibikāyām athāropya rājānaṃ gatacetanam 
bāṣpakaṇṭhā vimanasas tam ūhuḥ paricārakāḥ  RamS 
hiraṇyaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ ca vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca 
prakiranto janā mārgaṃ nṛpater agrato yayuḥ  RamS 
candanāguruniryāsān saralaṃ padmakaṃ tathā 
devadārūṇi cāhṛtya citāṃ cakrus tathāpare  RamS 
gandhān uccāvacāṃś cānyāṃs tatra dattvātha bhūmipam 
tataḥ saṃveśayāmāsuś citāmadhye tam ṛtvijaḥ  RamS 
tathā hutāśanaṃ hutvā jepus tasya tadartvijaḥ 
jaguś ca te yathāśāstraṃ tatra sāmāni sāmagāḥ  RamS 
śibikābhiś ca yānaiś ca yathārhaṃ tasya yoṣitaḥ 
nagarān niryayus tatra vṛddhaiḥ parivṛtās tadā  RamS 
prasavyaṃ cāpi taṃ cakrur ṛtvijo 'gnicitaṃ nṛpam 
striyaś ca śokasaṃtaptāḥ kausalyāpramukhās tadā  RamS 
krauñcīnām iva nārīṇāṃ ninādas tatra śuśruve 
ārtānāṃ karuṇaṃ kāle krośantīnāṃ sahasraśaḥ  RamS 
tato rudantyo vivaśā vilapya ca punaḥ punaḥ 
yānebhyaḥ sarayūtīram avaterur varāṅganāḥ  RamS 
kṛtodakaṃ te bharatena sārdhaṃ nṛpāṅganā mantripurohitāś ca 
puraṃ praviśyāśruparītanetrā bhūmau daśāhaṃ vyanayanta duḥkham  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tato daśāhe 'tigate kṛtaśauco nṛpātmajaḥ 
dvādaśe 'hani samprāpte śrāddhakarmāṇy akārayat  RamS 
brāhmaṇebhyo dadau ratnaṃ dhanam annaṃ ca puṣkalam 
bāstikaṃ bahuśuklaṃ ca gāś cāpi śataśas tathā  RamS 
dāsīdāsaṃ ca yānaṃ ca veśmāni sumahānti ca 
brāhmaṇebhyo dadau putro rājñas tasyaurdhvadaihikam  RamS 
tataḥ prabhātasamaye divase 'tha trayodaśe 
vilalāpa mahābāhur bharataḥ śokamūrchitaḥ  RamS 
śabdāpihitakaṇṭhaś ca śodhanārtham upāgataḥ 
citāmūle pitur vākyam idam āha suduḥkhitaḥ  RamS 
tāta yasmin nisṛṣṭo 'haṃ tvayā bhrātari rāghave 
tasmin vanaṃ pravrajite śūnye tyakto 'smy ahaṃ tvayā  RamS 
yathāgatir anāthāyāḥ putraḥ pravrājito vanam 
tām ambāṃ tāta kausalyāṃ tyaktvā tvaṃ kva gato nṛpa  RamS 
dṛṣṭvā bhasmāruṇaṃ tac ca dagdhāsthisthānamaṇḍalam 
pituḥ śarīranirvāṇaṃ niṣṭanan viṣasāda ha  RamS 
sa tu dṛṣṭvā rudan dīnaḥ papāta dharaṇītale 
utthāpyamānaḥ śakrasya yantradhvaja iva cyutaḥ  RamS 
abhipetus tataḥ sarve tasyāmātyāḥ śucivratam 
antakāle nipatitaṃ yayātim ṛṣayo yathā  RamS 
śatrughnaś cāpi bharataṃ dṛṣṭvā śokapariplutam 
visaṃjño nyapatad bhūmau bhūmipālam anusmaran  RamS 
unmatta iva niścetā vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ 
smṛtvā pitur guṇāṅgāni tāni tāni tadā tadā  RamS 
mantharāprabhavas tīvraḥ kaikeyīgrāhasaṃkulaḥ 
varadānamayo 'kṣobhyo 'majjayac chokasāgaraḥ  RamS 
sukumāraṃ ca bālaṃ ca satataṃ lālitaṃ tvayā 
kva tāta bharataṃ hitvā vilapantaṃ gato bhavān  RamS 
nanu bhojyeṣu pāneṣu vastreṣv ābharaṇeṣu ca 
pravārayasi naḥ sarvāṃs tan naḥ ko 'dya kariṣyati  RamS 
avadāraṇakāle tu pṛthivī nāvadīryate 
vihīnā yā tvayā rājñā dharmajñena mahātmanā  RamS 
pitari svargam āpanne rāme cāraṇyam āśrite 
kiṃ me jīvitasāmarthyaṃ pravekṣyāmi hutāśanam  RamS 
hīno bhrātrā ca pitrā ca śūnyām ikṣvākupālitām 
ayodhyāṃ na pravekṣyāmi pravekṣyāmi tapovanam  RamS 
tayor vilapitaṃ śrutvā vyasanaṃ cānvavekṣya tat 
bhṛśam ārtatarā bhūyaḥ sarva evānugāminaḥ  RamS 
tato viṣaṇṇau śrāntau ca śatrughnabharatāv ubhau 
dharaṇyāṃ saṃvyaceṣṭetāṃ bhagnaśṛṅgāv ivarṣabhau  RamS 
tataḥ prakṛtimān vaidyaḥ pitur eṣāṃ purohitaḥ 
vasiṣṭho bharataṃ vākyam utthāpya tam uvāca ha  RamS 
trīṇi dvaṃdvāni bhūteṣu pravṛttāny aviśeṣataḥ 
teṣu cāparihāryeṣu naivaṃ bhavitum arhati  RamS 
sumantraś cāpi śatrughnam utthāpyābhiprasādya ca 
śrāvayāmāsa tattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtabhavābhavau  RamS 
utthitau tau naravyāghrau prakāśete yaśasvinau 
varṣātapapariklinnau pṛthag indradhvajāv iva  RamS 
aśrūṇi parimṛdnantau raktākṣau dīnabhāṣiṇau 
amātyās tvarayanti sma tanayau cāparāḥ kriyāḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
atra yātrāṃ samīhantaṃ śatrughno lakṣmaṇānujaḥ 
bharataṃ śokasaṃtaptam idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
gatir yaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ duḥkhe kiṃ punar ātmanaḥ 
sa rāmaḥ sattvasampannaḥ striyā pravrājito vanam  RamS 
balavān vīryasampanno lakṣmaṇo nāma yo 'py asau 
kiṃ na mocayate rāmaṃ kṛtvāpi pitṛnigraham  RamS 
pūrvam eva tu nigrāhyaḥ samavekṣya nayānayau 
utpathaṃ yaḥ samārūḍho nāryā rājā vaśaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
iti sambhāṣamāṇe tu śatrughne lakṣmaṇānuje 
prāgdvāre 'bhūt tadā kubjā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā  RamS 
liptā candanasāreṇa rājavastrāṇi bibhratī 
mekhalādāmabhiś citrai rajjubaddheva vānarī  RamS 
tāṃ samīkṣya tadā dvāḥstho bhṛśaṃ pāpasya kāriṇīm 
gṛhītvākaruṇāṃ kubjāṃ śatrughnāya nyavedayat  RamS 
yasyāḥ kṛte vane rāmo nyastadehaś ca vaḥ pitā 
seyaṃ pāpā nṛśaṃsā ca tasyāḥ kuru yathāmati  RamS 
śatrughnaś ca tad ājñāya vacanaṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ 
antaḥpuracarān sarvān ity uvāca dhṛtavrataḥ  RamS 
tīvram utpāditaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhrātḥṇāṃ me tathā pituḥ 
yayā seyaṃ nṛśaṃsasya karmaṇaḥ phalam aśnutām  RamS 
evam uktā ca tenāśu sakhījanasamāvṛtā 
gṛhītā balavat kubjā sā tadgṛham anādayat  RamS 
tataḥ subhṛśasaṃtaptas tasyāḥ sarvaḥ sakhījanaḥ 
kruddham ājñāya śatrughnaṃ vyapalāyata sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
amantrayata kṛtsnaś ca tasyāḥ sarvasakhījanaḥ 
yathāyaṃ samupakrānto niḥśeṣaṃ naḥ kariṣyati  RamS 
sānukrośāṃ vadānyāṃ ca dharmajñāṃ ca yaśasvinīm 
kausalyāṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmaḥ sā hi no 'stu dhruvā gatiḥ  RamS 
sa ca roṣeṇa tāmrākṣaḥ śatrughnaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ 
vicakarṣa tadā kubjāṃ krośantīṃ pṛthivītale  RamS 
tasyā hy ākṛṣyamāṇāyā mantharāyās tatas tataḥ 
citraṃ bahuvidhaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ pṛthivyāṃ tad vyaśīryata  RamS 
tena bhāṇḍena saṃkīrṇaṃ śrīmadrājaniveśanam 
aśobhata tadā bhūyaḥ śāradaṃ gaganaṃ yathā  RamS 
sa balī balavat krodhād gṛhītvā puruṣarṣabhaḥ 
kaikeyīm abhinirbhartsya babhāṣe paruṣaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
tair vākyaiḥ paruṣair duḥkhaiḥ kaikeyī bhṛśaduḥkhitā 
śatrughnabhayasaṃtrastā putraṃ śaraṇam āgatā  RamS 
tāṃ prekṣya bharataḥ kruddhaṃ śatrughnam idam abravīt 
avadhyāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ pramadāḥ kṣamyatām iti  RamS 
hanyām aham imāṃ pāpāṃ kaikeyīṃ duṣṭacāriṇīm 
yadi māṃ dhārmiko rāmo nāsūyen mātṛghātakam  RamS 
imām api hatāṃ kubjāṃ yadi jānāti rāghavaḥ 
tvāṃ ca māṃ caiva dharmātmā nābhibhāṣiṣyate dhruvam  RamS 
bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā śatrughno lakṣmaṇānujaḥ 
nyavartata tato roṣāt tāṃ mumoca ca mantharām  RamS 
sā pādamūle kaikeyyā mantharā nipapāta ha 
niḥśvasantī suduḥkhārtā kṛpaṇaṃ vilalāpa ca  RamS 
śatrughnavikṣepavimūḍhasaṃjñāṃ samīkṣya kubjāṃ bharatasya mātā 
śanaiḥ samāśvāsayad ārtarūpāṃ krauñcīṃ vilagnām iva vīkṣamāṇām  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tataḥ prabhātasamaye divase 'tha caturdaśe 
sametya rājakartāro bharataṃ vākyam abruvan  RamS 
gato daśarathaḥ svargaṃ yo no gurutaro guruḥ 
rāmaṃ pravrājya vai jyeṣṭhaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābalam  RamS 
tvam adya bhava no rājā rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ 
saṃgatyā nāparādhnoti rājyam etad anāyakam  RamS 
ābhiṣecanikaṃ sarvam idam ādāya rāghava 
pratīkṣate tvāṃ svajanaḥ śreṇayaś ca nṛpātmaja  RamS 
rājyaṃ gṛhāṇa bharata pitṛpaitāmahaṃ mahat 
abhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ pāhi cāsmān nararṣabha  RamS 
ābhiṣecanikaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ kṛtvā sarvaṃ pradakṣiṇam 
bharatas taṃ janaṃ sarvaṃ pratyuvāca dhṛtavrataḥ  RamS 
jyeṣṭhasya rājatā nityam ucitā hi kulasya naḥ 
naivaṃ bhavanto māṃ vaktum arhanti kuśalā janāḥ  RamS 
rāmaḥ pūrvo hi no bhrātā bhaviṣyati mahīpatiḥ 
ahaṃ tv araṇye vatsyāmi varṣāṇi nava pañca ca  RamS 
yujyatāṃ mahatī senā caturaṅgamahābalā 
ānayiṣyāmy ahaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ bhrātaraṃ rāghavaṃ vanāt  RamS 
ābhiṣecanikaṃ caiva sarvam etad upaskṛtam 
puraskṛtya gamiṣyāmi rāmahetor vanaṃ prati  RamS 
tatraiva taṃ naravyāghram abhiṣicya puraskṛtam 
āneṣyāmi tu vai rāmaṃ havyavāham ivādhvarāt  RamS 
na sakāmāṃ kariṣyāmi svām imāṃ mātṛgandhinīm 
vane vatsyāmy ahaṃ durge rāmo rājā bhaviṣyati  RamS 
kriyatāṃ śilpibhiḥ panthāḥ samāni viṣamāṇi ca 
rakṣiṇaś cānusaṃyāntu pathi durgavicārakāḥ  RamS 
evaṃ sambhāṣamāṇaṃ taṃ rāmahetor nṛpātmajam 
pratyuvāca janaḥ sarvaḥ śrīmadvākyam anuttamam  RamS 
evaṃ te bhāṣamāṇasya padmā śrīr upatiṣṭhatām 
yas tvaṃ jyeṣṭhe nṛpasute pṛthivīṃ dātum icchasi  RamS 
anuttamaṃ tad vacanaṃ nṛpātmaja prabhāṣitaṃ saṃśravaṇe niśamya ca 
praharṣajās taṃ prati bāṣpabindavo nipetur āryānananetrasambhavāḥ  RamS 
ūcus te vacanam idaṃ niśamya hṛṣṭāḥ sāmātyāḥ sapariṣado viyātaśokāḥ 
panthānaṃ naravarabhaktimāñ janaś ca vyādiṣṭas tava vacanāc ca śilpivargaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
atha bhūmipradeśajñāḥ sūtrakarmaviśāradāḥ 
svakarmābhiratāḥ śūrāḥ khanakā yantrakās tathā  RamS 
karmāntikāḥ sthapatayaḥ puruṣā yantrakovidāḥ 
tathā vardhakayaś caiva mārgiṇo vṛkṣatakṣakāḥ  RamS 
kūpakārāḥ sudhākārā vaṃśakarmakṛtas tathā 
samarthā ye ca draṣṭāraḥ puratas te pratasthire  RamS 
sa tu harṣāt tam uddeśaṃ janaugho vipulaḥ prayān 
aśobhata mahāvegaḥ sāgarasyeva parvaṇi  RamS 
te svavāraṃ samāsthāya vartmakarmāṇi kovidāḥ 
karaṇair vividhopetaiḥ purastāt sampratasthire  RamS 
latāvallīś ca gulmāṃś ca sthāṇūn aśmana eva ca 
janās te cakrire mārgaṃ chindanto vividhān drumān  RamS 
avṛkṣeṣu ca deśeṣu kecid vṛkṣān aropayan 
kecit kuṭhāraiṣ ṭaṅkaiś ca dātraiś chindan kvacit kvacit  RamS 
apare vīraṇastambān balino balavattarāḥ 
vidhamanti sma durgāṇi sthalāni ca tatas tataḥ  RamS 
apare 'pūrayan kūpān pāṃsubhiḥ śvabhram āyatam 
nimnabhāgāṃs tathā kecit samāṃś cakruḥ samantataḥ  RamS 
babandhur bandhanīyāṃś ca kṣodyān saṃcukṣudus tadā 
bibhidur bhedanīyāṃś ca tāṃs tān deśān narās tadā  RamS 
acireṇaiva kālena parivāhān bahūdakān 
cakrur bahuvidhākārān sāgarapratimān bahūn 
udapānān bahuvidhān vedikāparimaṇḍitān  RamS 
sa sudhākuṭṭimatalaḥ prapuṣpitamahīruhaḥ 
mattodghuṣṭadvijagaṇaḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtaḥ  RamS 
candanodakasaṃsikto nānākusumabhūṣitaḥ 
bahv aśobhata senāyāḥ panthāḥ svargapathopamaḥ  RamS 
ājñāpyātha yathājñapti yuktās te 'dhikṛtā narāḥ 
ramaṇīyeṣu deśeṣu bahusvāduphaleṣu ca  RamS 
yo niveśas tv abhipreto bharatasya mahātmanaḥ 
bhūyas taṃ śobhayāmāsur bhūṣābhir bhūṣaṇopamam  RamS 
nakṣatreṣu praśasteṣu muhūrteṣu ca tadvidaḥ 
niveśaṃ sthāpayāmāsur bharatasya mahātmanaḥ  RamS 
bahupāṃsucayāś cāpi parikhāparivāritāḥ 
tatrendrakīlapratimāḥ pratolīvaraśobhitāḥ  RamS 
prāsādamālāsaṃyuktāḥ saudhaprākārasaṃvṛtāḥ 
patākāśobhitāḥ sarve sunirmitamahāpathāḥ  RamS 
visarpadbhir ivākāśe viṭaṅkāgravimānakaiḥ 
samucchritair niveśās te babhuḥ śakrapuropamāḥ  RamS 
jāhnavīṃ tu samāsādya vividhadrumakānanām 
śītalāmalapānīyāṃ mahāmīnasamākulām  RamS 
sacandratārāgaṇamaṇḍitaṃ yathā nabhaḥ kṣapāyām amalaṃ virājate 
narendramārgaḥ sa tathā vyarājata krameṇa ramyaḥ śubhaśilpinirmitaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tato nāndīmukhīṃ rātriṃ bharataṃ sūtamāgadhāḥ 
tuṣṭuvur vāgviśeṣajñāḥ stavair maṅgalasaṃhitaiḥ  RamS 
suvarṇakoṇābhihataḥ prāṇadad yāmadundubhiḥ 
dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca śataśo vādyāṃś coccāvacasvarān  RamS 
sa tūryaghoṣaḥ sumahān divam āpūrayann iva 
bharataṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ bhūyaḥ śokair arandhrayat  RamS 
tataḥ prabuddho bharatas taṃ ghoṣaṃ saṃnivartya ca 
nāhaṃ rājeti cāpy uktvā śatrughnam idam abravīt  RamS 
paśya śatrughna kaikeyyā lokasyāpakṛtaṃ mahat 
visṛjya mayi duḥkhāni rājā daśaratho gataḥ  RamS 
tasyaiṣā dharmarājasya dharmamūlā mahātmanaḥ 
paribhramati rājaśrīr naur ivākarṇikā jale  RamS 
ity evaṃ bharataṃ prekṣya vilapantaṃ vicetanam 
kṛpaṇaṃ ruruduḥ sarvāḥ sasvaraṃ yoṣitas tadā  RamS 
tathā tasmin vilapati vasiṣṭho rājadharmavit 
sabhām ikṣvākunāthasya praviveśa mahāyaśāḥ  RamS 
śātakumbhamayīṃ ramyāṃ maṇiratnasamākulām 
sudharmām iva dharmātmā sagaṇaḥ pratyapadyata  RamS 
sa kāñcanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ parārdhyāstaraṇāvṛtam 
adhyāsta sarvavedajño dūtān anuśaśāsa ca  RamS 
brāhmaṇān kṣatriyān yodhān amātyān gaṇavallabhān 
kṣipram ānayatāvyagrāḥ kṛtyam ātyayikaṃ hi naḥ  RamS 
tato halahalāśabdo mahān samudapadyata 
rathair aśvair gajaiś cāpi janānām upagacchatām  RamS 
tato bharatam āyāntaṃ śatakratum ivāmarāḥ 
pratyanandan prakṛtayo yathā daśarathaṃ tathā  RamS 
hrada iva timināgasaṃvṛtaḥ stimitajalo maṇiśaṅkhaśarkaraḥ 
daśarathasutaśobhitā sabhā sadaśaratheva babhau yathā purā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tām āryagaṇasampūrṇāṃ bharataḥ pragrahāṃ sabhām 
dadarśa buddhisampannaḥ pūrṇacandrāṃ niśām iva  RamS 
āsanāni yathānyāyam āryāṇāṃ viśatāṃ tadā 
adṛśyata ghanāpāye pūrṇacandreva śarvarī  RamS 
rājñas tu prakṛtīḥ sarvāḥ samagrāḥ prekṣya dharmavit 
idaṃ purohito vākyaṃ bharataṃ mṛdu cābravīt  RamS 
tāta rājā daśarathaḥ svargato dharmam ācaran 
dhanadhānyavatīṃ sphītāṃ pradāya pṛthivīṃ tava  RamS 
rāmas tathā satyadhṛtiḥ satāṃ dharmam anusmaran 
nājahāt pitur ādeśaṃ śaśī jyotsnām ivoditaḥ  RamS 
pitrā bhrātrā ca te dattaṃ rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam 
tad bhuṅkṣva muditāmātyaḥ kṣipram evābhiṣecaya  RamS 
udīcyāś ca pratīcyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca kevalāḥ 
koṭyāparāntāḥ sāmudrā ratnāny abhiharantu te  RamS 
tac chrutvā bharato vākyaṃ śokenābhipariplutaḥ 
jagāma manasā rāmaṃ dharmajño dharmakāṅkṣayā  RamS 
sa bāṣpakalayā vācā kalahaṃsasvaro yuvā 
vilalāpa sabhāmadhye jagarhe ca purohitam  RamS 
caritabrahmacaryasya vidyā snātasya dhīmataḥ 
dharme prayatamānasya ko rājyaṃ madvidho haret  RamS 
kathaṃ daśarathāj jāto bhaved rājyāpahārakaḥ 
rājyaṃ cāhaṃ ca rāmasya dharmaṃ vaktum ihārhasi  RamS 
jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaś ca dharmātmā dilīpanahuṣopamaḥ 
labdhum arhati kākutstho rājyaṃ daśaratho yathā  RamS 
anāryajuṣṭam asvargyaṃ kuryāṃ pāpam ahaṃ yadi 
ikṣvākūṇām ahaṃ loke bhaveyaṃ kulapāṃsanaḥ  RamS 
yaddhi mātrā kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ nāhaṃ tad abhirocaye 
ihastho vanadurgasthaṃ namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ  RamS 
rāmam evānugacchāmi sa rājā dvipadāṃ varaḥ 
trayāṇām api lokānāṃ rāghavo rājyam arhati  RamS 
tad vākyaṃ dharmasaṃyuktaṃ śrutvā sarve sabhāsadaḥ 
harṣān mumucur aśrūṇi rāme nihitacetasaḥ  RamS 
yadi tv āryaṃ na śakṣyāmi vinivartayituṃ vanāt 
vane tatraiva vatsyāmi yathāryo lakṣmaṇas tathā  RamS 
sarvopāyaṃ tu vartiṣye vinivartayituṃ balāt 
samakṣam āryamiśrāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ guṇavartinām  RamS 
evam uktvā tu dharmātmā bharato bhrātṛvatsalaḥ 
samīpastham uvācedaṃ sumantraṃ mantrakovidam  RamS 
tūrṇam utthāya gaccha tvaṃ sumantra mama śāsanāt 
yātrām ājñāpaya kṣipraṃ balaṃ caiva samānaya  RamS 
evam uktaḥ sumantras tu bharatena mahātmanā 
prahṛṣṭaḥ so 'diśat sarvaṃ yathā saṃdiṣṭam iṣṭavat  RamS 
tāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ prakṛtayo balādhyakṣā balasya ca 
śrutvā yātrāṃ samājñaptāṃ rāghavasya nivartane  RamS 
tato yodhāṅganāḥ sarvā bhartḥn sarvān gṛhe gṛhe 
yātrāgamanam ājñāya tvarayanti sma harṣitāḥ  RamS 
te hayair gorathaiḥ śīghraiḥ syandanaiś ca manojavaiḥ 
saha yodhair balādhyakṣā balaṃ sarvam acodayan  RamS 
sajjaṃ tu tad balaṃ dṛṣṭvā bharato gurusaṃnidhau 
rathaṃ me tvarayasveti sumantraṃ pārśvato 'bravīt  RamS 
bharatasya tu tasyājñāṃ pratigṛhya praharṣitaḥ 
rathaṃ gṛhītvā prayayau yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ  RamS 
sa rāghavaḥ satyadhṛtiḥ pratāpavān bruvan suyuktaṃ dṛḍhasatyavikramaḥ 
guruṃ mahāraṇyagataṃ yaśasvinaṃ prasādayiṣyan bharato 'bravīt tadā  RamS 
tūrṇaṃ samutthāya sumantra gaccha balasya yogāya balapradhānān 
ānetum icchāmi hi taṃ vanasthaṃ prasādya rāmaṃ jagato hitāya  RamS 
sa sūtaputro bharatena samyag ājñāpitaḥ saṃparipūrṇakāmaḥ 
śaśāsa sarvān prakṛtipradhānān balasya mukhyāṃś ca suhṛjjanaṃ ca  RamS 
tataḥ samutthāya kule kule te rājanyavaiśyā vṛṣalāś ca viprāḥ 
ayūyujann uṣṭrarathān kharāṃś ca nāgān hayāṃś caiva kulaprasūtān  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tataḥ samutthitaḥ kālyam āsthāya syandanottamam 
prayayau bharataḥ śīghraṃ rāmadarśanakāṅkṣayā  RamS 
agrataḥ prayayus tasya sarve mantripurodhasaḥ 
adhiruhya hayair yuktān rathān sūryarathopamān  RamS 
navanāgasahasrāṇi kalpitāni yathāvidhi 
anvayur bharataṃ yāntam ikṣvākukulanandanam  RamS 
ṣaṣṭhī rathasahasrāṇi dhanvino vividhāyudhāḥ 
anvayur bharataṃ yāntaṃ rājaputraṃ yaśasvinam  RamS 
śataṃ sahasrāṇy aśvānāṃ samārūḍhāni rāghavam 
anvayur bharataṃ yāntaṃ rājaputraṃ yaśasvinam  RamS 
kaikeyī ca sumitrā ca kausalyā ca yaśasvinī 
rāmānayanasaṃhṛṣṭā yayur yānena bhāsvatā  RamS 
prayātāś cāryasaṃghātā rāmaṃ draṣṭuṃ salakṣmaṇam 
tasyaiva ca kathāś citrāḥ kurvāṇā hṛṣṭamānasāḥ  RamS 
meghaśyāmaṃ mahābāhuṃ sthirasattvaṃ dṛḍhavratam 
kadā drakṣyāmahe rāmaṃ jagataḥ śokanāśanam  RamS 
dṛṣṭa eva hi naḥ śokam apaneṣyati rāghavaḥ 
tamaḥ sarvasya lokasya samudyann iva bhāskaraḥ  RamS 
ity evaṃ kathayantas te samprahṛṣṭāḥ kathāḥ śubhāḥ 
pariṣvajānāś cānyonyaṃ yayur nāgarikās tadā  RamS 
ye ca tatrāpare sarve saṃmatā ye ca naigamāḥ 
rāmaṃ prati yayur hṛṣṭāḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayas tadā  RamS 
maṇikārāś ca ye kecit kumbhakārāś ca śobhanāḥ 
sūtrakarmakṛtaś caiva ye ca śastropajīvinaḥ  RamS 
māyūrakāḥ krākacikā rocakā vedhakās tathā 
dantakārāḥ sudhākārās tathā gandhopajīvinaḥ  RamS 
suvarṇakārāḥ prakhyātās tathā kambaladhāvakāḥ 
snāpakācchādakā vaidyā dhūpakāḥ śauṇḍikās tathā  RamS 
rajakās tunnavāyāś ca grāmaghoṣamahattarāḥ 
śailūṣāś ca saha strībhir yānti kaivartakās tathā  RamS 
samāhitā vedavido brāhmaṇā vṛttasaṃmatāḥ 
gorathair bharataṃ yāntam anujagmuḥ sahasraśaḥ  RamS 
suveṣāḥ śuddhavasanās tāmramṛṣṭānulepanāḥ 
sarve te vividhair yānaiḥ śanair bharatam anvayuḥ  RamS 
prahṛṣṭamuditā senā sānvayāt kaikayīsutam 
vyavātiṣṭhata sā senā bharatasyānuyāyinī  RamS 
nirīkṣyānugatāṃ senāṃ tāṃ ca gaṅgāṃ śivodakām 
bharataḥ sacivān sarvān abravīd vākyakovidaḥ  RamS 
niveśayata me sainyam abhiprāyeṇa sarvaśaḥ 
viśrāntāḥ pratariṣyāmaḥ śva idānīṃ mahānadīm  RamS 
dātuṃ ca tāvad icchāmi svar gatasya mahīpateḥ 
aurdhvadehanimittārtham avatīryodakaṃ nadīm  RamS 
tasyaivaṃ bruvato 'mātyās tathety uktvā samāhitāḥ 
nyaveśayaṃs tāṃś chandena svena svena pṛthakpṛthak  RamS 
niveśya gaṅgām anu tāṃ mahānadīṃ camūṃ vidhānaiḥ paribarhaśobhinīm 
uvāsa rāmasya tadā mahātmano vicintayāno bharato nivartanam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tato niviṣṭāṃ dhvajinīṃ gaṅgām anvāśritāṃ nadīm 
niṣādarājo dṛṣṭvaiva jñātīn saṃtvarito 'bravīt  RamS 
mahatīyam ataḥ senā sāgarābhā pradṛśyate 
nāsyāntam avagacchāmi manasāpi vicintayan  RamS 
sa eṣa hi mahākāyaḥ kovidāradhvajo rathe 
bandhayiṣyati vā dāśān atha vāsmān vadhiṣyati  RamS 
atha dāśarathiṃ rāmaṃ pitrā rājyād vivāsitam 
bharataḥ kaikeyīputro hantuṃ samadhigacchati  RamS 
bhartā caiva sakhā caiva rāmo dāśarathir mama 
tasyārthakāmāḥ saṃnaddhā gaṅgānūpe 'tra tiṣṭhata  RamS 
tiṣṭhantu sarvadāśāś ca gaṅgām anvāśritā nadīm 
balayuktā nadīrakṣā māṃsamūlaphalāśanāḥ  RamS 
nāvāṃ śatānāṃ pañcānāṃ kaivartānāṃ śataṃ śatam 
saṃnaddhānāṃ tathā yūnāṃ tiṣṭhantv ity abhyacodayat  RamS 
yadā tuṣṭas tu bharato rāmasyeha bhaviṣyati 
seyaṃ svastimayī senā gaṅgām adya tariṣyati  RamS 
ity uktvopāyanaṃ gṛhya matsyamāṃsamadhūni ca 
abhicakrāma bharataṃ niṣādādhipatir guhaḥ  RamS 
tam āyāntaṃ tu samprekṣya sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān 
bharatāyācacakṣe 'tha vinayajño vinītavat  RamS 
eṣa jñātisahasreṇa sthapatiḥ parivāritaḥ 
kuśalo daṇḍakāraṇye vṛddho bhrātuś ca te sakhā  RamS 
tasmāt paśyatu kākutstha tvāṃ niṣādādhipo guhaḥ 
asaṃśayaṃ vijānīte yatra tau rāmalakṣmaṇau  RamS 
etat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā sumantrād bharataḥ śubham 
uvāca vacanaṃ śīghraṃ guhaḥ paśyatu mām iti  RamS 
labdhvābhyanujñāṃ saṃhṛṣṭo jñātibhiḥ parivāritaḥ 
āgamya bharataṃ prahvo guho vacanam abravīt  RamS 
niṣkuṭaś caiva deśo 'yaṃ vañcitāś cāpi te vayam 
nivedayāmas te sarve svake dāśakule vasa  RamS 
asti mūlaṃ phalaṃ caiva niṣādaiḥ samupāhṛtam 
ārdraṃ ca māṃsaṃ śuṣkaṃ ca vanyaṃ coccāvacaṃ mahat  RamS 
āśaṃse svāśitā senā vatsyatīmāṃ vibhāvarīm 
arcito vividhaiḥ kāmaiḥ śvaḥ sasainyo gamiṣyasi  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
evam uktas tu bharato niṣādādhipatiṃ guham 
pratyuvāca mahāprājño vākyaṃ hetvarthasaṃhitam  RamS 
ūrjitaḥ khalu te kāmaḥ kṛto mama guroḥ sakhe 
yo me tvam īdṛśīṃ senām eko 'bhyarcitum icchasi  RamS 
ity uktvā tu mahātejā guhaṃ vacanam uttamam 
abravīd bharataḥ śrīmān niṣādādhipatiṃ punaḥ  RamS 
katareṇa gamiṣyāmi bharadvājāśramaṃ guha 
gahano 'yaṃ bhṛśaṃ deśo gaṅgānūpo duratyayaḥ  RamS 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rājaputrasya dhīmataḥ 
abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ guho gahanagocaraḥ  RamS 
dāśās tv anugamiṣyanti dhanvinaḥ susamāhitāḥ 
ahaṃ cānugamiṣyāmi rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ  RamS 
kaccin na duṣṭo vrajasi rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ 
iyaṃ te mahatī senā śaṅkāṃ janayatīva me  RamS 
tam evam abhibhāṣantam ākāśa iva nirmalaḥ 
bharataḥ ślakṣṇayā vācā guhaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
mā bhūt sa kālo yat kaṣṭaṃ na māṃ śaṅkitum arhasi 
rāghavaḥ sa hi me bhrātā jyeṣṭhaḥ pitṛsamo mama  RamS 
taṃ nivartayituṃ yāmi kākutsthaṃ vanavāsinam 
buddhir anyā na te kāryā guha satyaṃ bravīmi te  RamS 
sa tu saṃhṛṣṭavadanaḥ śrutvā bharatabhāṣitam 
punar evābravīd vākyaṃ bharataṃ prati harṣitaḥ  RamS 
dhanyas tvaṃ na tvayā tulyaṃ paśyāmi jagatītale 
ayatnād āgataṃ rājyaṃ yas tvaṃ tyaktum ihecchasi  RamS 
śāśvatī khalu te kīrtir lokān anucariṣyati 
yas tvaṃ kṛcchragataṃ rāmaṃ pratyānayitum icchasi  RamS 
evaṃ sambhāṣamāṇasya guhasya bharataṃ tadā 
babhau naṣṭaprabhaḥ sūryo rajanī cābhyavartata  RamS 
saṃniveśya sa tāṃ senāṃ guhena paritoṣitaḥ 
śatrughnena saha śrīmāñ śayanaṃ punar āgamat  RamS 
rāmacintāmayaḥ śoko bharatasya mahātmanaḥ 
upasthito hy anarhasya dharmaprekṣasya tādṛśaḥ  RamS 
antardāhena dahanaḥ saṃtāpayati rāghavam 
vanadāhābhisaṃtaptaṃ gūḍho 'gnir iva pādapam  RamS 
prasrutaḥ sarvagātrebhyaḥ svedaḥ śokāgnisambhavaḥ 
yathā sūryāṃśusaṃtapto himavān prasruto himam  RamS 
dhyānanirdaraśailena viniḥśvasitadhātunā 
dainyapādapasaṃghena śokāyāsādhiśṛṅgiṇā  RamS 
pramohānantasattvena saṃtāpauṣadhiveṇunā 
ākrānto duḥkhaśailena mahatā kaikayīsutaḥ  RamS 
guhena sārdhaṃ bharataḥ samāgato mahānubhāvaḥ sajanaḥ samāhitaḥ 
sudurmanās taṃ bharataṃ tadā punar guhaḥ samāśvāsayad agrajaṃ prati  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
ācacakṣe 'tha sadbhāvaṃ lakṣmaṇasya mahātmanaḥ 
bharatāyāprameyāya guho gahanagocaraḥ  RamS 
taṃ jāgrataṃ guṇair yuktaṃ varacāpeṣudhāriṇam 
bhrātṛguptyartham atyantam ahaṃ lakṣmaṇam abruvam  RamS 
iyaṃ tāta sukhā śayyā tvadartham upakalpitā 
pratyāśvasihi śeṣvāsyāṃ sukhaṃ rāghavanandana  RamS 
ucito 'yaṃ janaḥ sarvo duḥkhānāṃ tvaṃ sukhocitaḥ 
dharmātmaṃs tasya guptyarthaṃ jāgariṣyāmahe vayam  RamS 
na hi rāmāt priyataro mamāsti bhuvi kaścana 
motsuko bhūr bravīmy etad apy asatyaṃ tavāgrataḥ  RamS 
asya prasādād āśaṃse loke 'smin sumahad yaśaḥ 
dharmāvāptiṃ ca vipulām arthāvāptiṃ ca kevalām  RamS 
so 'haṃ priyasakhaṃ rāmaṃ śayānaṃ saha sītayā 
rakṣiṣyāmi dhanuṣpāṇiḥ sarvaiḥ svair jñātibhiḥ saha  RamS 
na hi me 'viditaṃ kiṃcid vane 'smiṃś carataḥ sadā 
caturaṅgaṃ hy api balaṃ prasahema vayaṃ yudhi  RamS 
evam asmābhir uktena lakṣmaṇena mahātmanā 
anunītā vayaṃ sarve dharmam evānupaśyatā  RamS 
kathaṃ dāśarathau bhūmau śayāne saha sītayā 
śakyā nidrā mayā labdhuṃ jīvitaṃ vā sukhāni vā  RamS 
yo na devāsuraiḥ sarvaiḥ śakyaḥ prasahituṃ yudhi 
taṃ paśya guha saṃviṣṭaṃ tṛṇeṣu saha sītayā  RamS 
mahatā tapasā labdho vividhaiś ca pariśramaiḥ 
eko daśarathasyaiṣa putraḥ sadṛśalakṣaṇaḥ  RamS 
asmin pravrājite rājā na ciraṃ vartayiṣyati 
vidhavā medinī nūnaṃ kṣipram eva bhaviṣyati  RamS 
vinadya sumahānādaṃ śrameṇoparatāḥ striyaḥ 
nirghoṣoparataṃ nūnam adya rājaniveśanam  RamS 
kausalyā caiva rājā ca tathaiva jananī mama 
nāśaṃse yadi te sarve jīveyuḥ śarvarīm imām  RamS 
jīved api hi me mātā śatrughnasyānvavekṣayā 
duḥkhitā yā tu kausalyā vīrasūr vinaśiṣyati  RamS 
atikrāntam atikrāntam anavāpya manoratham 
rājye rāmam anikṣipya pitā me vinaśiṣyati  RamS 
siddhārthāḥ pitaraṃ vṛttaṃ tasmin kāle hy upasthite 
pretakāryeṣu sarveṣu saṃskariṣyanti bhūmipam  RamS 
ramyacatvarasaṃsthānāṃ suvibhaktamahāpathām 
harmyaprāsādasampannāṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitām  RamS 
gajāśvarathasambādhāṃ tūryanādavināditām 
sarvakalyāṇasampūrṇāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulām  RamS 
ārāmodyānasampūrṇāṃ samājotsavaśālinīm 
sukhitā vicariṣyanti rājadhānīṃ pitur mama  RamS 
api satyapratijñena sārdhaṃ kuśalinā vayam 
nivṛtte samaye hy asmin sukhitāḥ praviśemahi  RamS 
paridevayamānasya tasyaivaṃ sumahātmanaḥ 
tiṣṭhato rājaputrasya śarvarī sātyavartata  RamS 
prabhāte vimale sūrye kārayitvā jaṭā ubhau 
asmin bhāgīrathītīre sukhaṃ saṃtāritau mayā  RamS 
jaṭādharau tau drumacīravāsasau mahābalau kuñjarayūthapopamau 
vareṣucāpāsidharau paraṃtapau vyavekṣamāṇau saha sītayā gatau  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
guhasya vacanaṃ śrutvā bharato bhṛśam apriyam 
dhyānaṃ jagāma tatraiva yatra tac chrutam apriyam  RamS 
sukumāro mahāsattvaḥ siṃhaskandho mahābhujaḥ 
puṇḍarīkaviśālākṣas taruṇaḥ priyadarśanaḥ  RamS 
pratyāśvasya muhūrtaṃ tu kālaṃ paramadurmanāḥ 
papāta sahasā totrair hṛdi viddha iva dvipaḥ  RamS 
tadavasthaṃ tu bharataṃ śatrughno 'nantarasthitaḥ 
pariṣvajya rurodoccair visaṃjñaḥ śokakarśitaḥ  RamS 
tataḥ sarvāḥ samāpetur mātaro bharatasya tāḥ 
upavāsakṛśā dīnā bhartṛvyasanakarśitāḥ  RamS 
tāś ca taṃ patitaṃ bhūmau rudantyaḥ paryavārayan 
kausalyā tv anusṛtyainaṃ durmanāḥ pariṣasvaje  RamS 
vatsalā svaṃ yathā vatsam upagūhya tapasvinī 
paripapraccha bharataṃ rudantī śokalālasā  RamS 
putra vyādhir na te kaccic charīraṃ paribādhate 
adya rājakulasyāsya tvadadhīnaṃ hi jīvitam  RamS 
tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā putra jīvāmi rāme sabhrātṛke gate 
vṛtte daśarathe rājñi nātha ekas tvam adya naḥ  RamS 
kaccin na lakṣmaṇe putra śrutaṃ te kiṃcid apriyam 
putra vā hy ekaputrāyāḥ sahabhārye vanaṃ gate  RamS 
sa muhūrtaṃ samāśvasya rudann eva mahāyaśāḥ 
kausalyāṃ parisāntvyedaṃ guhaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
bhrātā me kvāvasad rātriṃ kva sītā kva ca lakṣmaṇaḥ 
asvapac chayane kasmin kiṃ bhuktvā guha śaṃsa me  RamS 
so 'bravīd bharataṃ pṛṣṭo niṣādādhipatir guhaḥ 
yadvidhaṃ pratipede ca rāme priyahite 'tithau  RamS 
annam uccāvacaṃ bhakṣāḥ phalāni vividhāni ca 
rāmāyābhyavahārārthaṃ bahu copahṛtaṃ mayā  RamS 
tat sarvaṃ pratyanujñāsīd rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ 
na hi tat pratyagṛhṇāt sa kṣatradharmam anusmaran  RamS 
na hy asmābhiḥ pratigrāhyaṃ sakhe deyaṃ tu sarvadā 
iti tena vayaṃ rājann anunītā mahātmanā  RamS 
lakṣmaṇena samānītaṃ pītvā vāri mahāyaśāḥ 
aupavāsyaṃ tadākārṣīd rāghavaḥ saha sītayā  RamS 
tatas tu jalaśeṣeṇa lakṣmaṇo 'py akarot tadā 
vāgyatās te trayaḥ saṃdhyām upāsata samāhitāḥ  RamS 
saumitris tu tataḥ paścād akarot svāstaraṃ śubham 
svayam ānīya barhīṃṣi kṣipraṃ rāghavakāraṇāt  RamS 
tasmin samāviśad rāmaḥ svāstare saha sītayā 
prakṣālya ca tayoḥ pādāv apacakrāma lakṣmaṇaḥ  RamS 
etat tad iṅgudīmūlam idam eva ca tat tṛṇam 
yasmin rāmaś ca sītā ca rātriṃ tāṃ śayitāv ubhau  RamS 
niyamya pṛṣṭhe tu talāṅgulitravāñ śaraiḥ supūrṇāv iṣudhī paraṃtapaḥ 
mahad dhanuḥ sajyam upohya lakṣmaṇo niśām atiṣṭhat parito 'sya kevalam  RamS 
tatas tv ahaṃ cottamabāṇacāpadhṛk sthito 'bhavaṃ tatra sa yatra lakṣmaṇaḥ 
atandribhir jñātibhir āttakārmukair mahendrakalpaṃ paripālayaṃs tadā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tac chrutvā nipuṇaṃ sarvaṃ bharataḥ saha mantribhiḥ 
iṅgudīmūlam āgamya rāmaśayyām avekṣya tām  RamS 
abravīj jananīḥ sarvā iha tena mahātmanā 
śarvarī śayitā bhūmāv idam asya vimarditam  RamS 
mahābhāgakulīnena mahābhāgena dhīmatā 
jāto daśarathenorvyāṃ na rāmaḥ svaptum arhati  RamS 
ajinottarasaṃstīrṇe varāstaraṇasaṃcaye 
śayitvā puruṣavyāghraḥ kathaṃ śete mahītale  RamS 
prāsādāgravimāneṣu valabhīṣu ca sarvadā 
haimarājatabhaumeṣu varāstaraṇaśāliṣu  RamS 
puṣpasaṃcayacitreṣu candanāgarugandhiṣu 
pāṇḍurābhraprakāśeṣu śukasaṃgharuteṣu ca  RamS 
gītavāditranirghoṣair varābharaṇaniḥsvanaiḥ 
mṛdaṅgavaraśabdaiś ca satataṃ pratibodhitaḥ  RamS 
bandibhir vanditaḥ kāle bahubhiḥ sūtamāgadhaiḥ 
gāthābhir anurūpābhiḥ stutibhiś ca paraṃtapaḥ  RamS 
aśraddheyam idaṃ loke na satyaṃ pratibhāti mā 
muhyate khalu me bhāvaḥ svapno 'yam iti me matiḥ  RamS 
na nūnaṃ daivataṃ kiṃcit kālena balavattaram 
yatra dāśarathī rāmo bhūmāv evaṃ śayīta saḥ  RamS 
videharājasya sutā sītā ca priyadarśanā 
dayitā śayitā bhūmau snuṣā daśarathasya ca  RamS 
iyaṃ śayyā mama bhrātur idaṃ hi parivartitam 
sthaṇḍile kaṭhine sarvaṃ gātrair vimṛditaṃ tṛṇam  RamS 
manye sābharaṇā suptā sītāsmiñ śayane tadā 
tatra tatra hi dṛśyante saktāḥ kanakabindavaḥ  RamS 
uttarīyam ihāsaktaṃ suvyaktaṃ sītayā tadā 
tathā hy ete prakāśante saktāḥ kauśeyatantavaḥ  RamS 
manye bhartuḥ sukhā śayyā yena bālā tapasvinī 
sukumārī satī duḥkhaṃ na vijānāti maithilī  RamS 
sārvabhaumakule jātaḥ sarvalokasukhāvahaḥ 
sarvalokapriyas tyaktvā rājyaṃ priyam anuttamam  RamS 
katham indīvaraśyāmo raktākṣaḥ priyadarśanaḥ 
sukhabhāgī ca duḥkhārhaḥ śayito bhuvi rāghavaḥ  RamS 
siddhārthā khalu vaidehī patiṃ yānugatā vanam 
vayaṃ saṃśayitāḥ sarve hīnās tena mahātmanā  RamS 
akarṇadhārā pṛthivī śūnyeva pratibhāti mā 
gate daśarathe svarge rāme cāraṇyam āśrite  RamS 
na ca prārthayate kaścin manasāpi vasuṃdharām 
vane 'pi vasatas tasya bāhuvīryābhirakṣitām  RamS 
śūnyasaṃvaraṇārakṣām ayantritahayadvipām 
apāvṛtapuradvārāṃ rājadhānīm arakṣitām  RamS 
aprahṛṣṭabalāṃ nyūnāṃ viṣamasthām anāvṛtām 
śatravo nābhimanyante bhakṣān viṣakṛtān iva  RamS 
adya prabhṛti bhūmau tu śayiṣye 'haṃ tṛṇeṣu vā 
phalamūlāśano nityaṃ jaṭācīrāṇi dhārayan  RamS 
tasyārtham uttaraṃ kālaṃ nivatsyāmi sukhaṃ vane 
taṃ pratiśravam āmucya nāsya mithyā bhaviṣyati  RamS 
vasantaṃ bhrātur arthāya śatrughno mānuvatsyati 
lakṣmaṇena saha tv āryo 'yodhyāṃ pālayiṣyati  RamS 
abhiṣekṣyanti kākutstham ayodhyāyāṃ dvijātayaḥ 
api me devatāḥ kuryur imaṃ satyaṃ manoratham  RamS 
prasādyamānaḥ śirasā mayā svayaṃ bahuprakāraṃ yadi na prapatsyate 
tato 'nuvatsyāmi cirāya rāghavaṃ vane vasan nārhati mām upekṣitum  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
vyuṣya rātriṃ tu tatraiva gaṅgākūle sa rāghavaḥ 
bharataḥ kālyam utthāya śatrughnam idam abravīt  RamS 
śatrughottiṣṭha kiṃ śeṣe niṣādādhipatiṃ guham 
śīghram ānaya bhadraṃ te tārayiṣyati vāhinīm  RamS 
jāgarmi nāhaṃ svapimi tathaivāryaṃ vicintayan 
ity evam abravīd bhrātrā śatrughno 'pi pracoditaḥ  RamS 
iti saṃvadator evam anyonyaṃ narasiṃhayoḥ 
āgamya prāñjaliḥ kāle guho bharatam abravīt  RamS 
kaccit sukhaṃ nadītīre 'vātsīḥ kākutstha śarvarīm 
kaccic ca saha sainyasya tava sarvam anāmayam  RamS 
guhasya tat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā snehād udīritam 
rāmasyānuvaśo vākyaṃ bharato 'pīdam abravīt  RamS 
sukhā naḥ śarvarī rājan pūjitāś cāpi te vayam 
gaṅgāṃ tu naubhir bahvībhir dāśāḥ saṃtārayantu naḥ  RamS 
tato guhaḥ saṃtvaritaḥ śrutvā bharataśāsanam 
pratipraviśya nagaraṃ taṃ jñātijanam abravīt  RamS 
uttiṣṭhata prabudhyadhvaṃ bhadram astu hi vaḥ sadā 
nāvaḥ samanukarṣadhvaṃ tārayiṣyāma vāhinīm  RamS 
te tathoktāḥ samutthāya tvaritā rājaśāsanāt 
pañca nāvāṃ śatāny eva samāninyuḥ samantataḥ  RamS 
anyāḥ svastikavijñeyā mahāghaṇṭādharā varāḥ 
śobhamānāḥ patākinyo yuktavātāḥ susaṃhatāḥ  RamS 
tataḥ svastikavijñeyāṃ pāṇḍukambalasaṃvṛtām 
sanandighoṣāṃ kalyāṇīṃ guho nāvam upāharat  RamS 
tām āruroha bharataḥ śatrughnaś ca mahābalaḥ 
kausalyā ca sumitrā ca yāś cānyā rājayoṣitaḥ  RamS 
purohitaś ca tat pūrvaṃ gurave brāhmaṇāś ca ye 
anantaraṃ rājadārās tathaiva śakaṭāpaṇāḥ  RamS 
āvāsam ādīpayatāṃ tīrthaṃ cāpy avagāhatām 
bhāṇḍāni cādadānānāṃ ghoṣas tridivam aspṛśat  RamS 
patākinyas tu tā nāvaḥ svayaṃ dāśair adhiṣṭhitāḥ 
vahantyo janam ārūḍhaṃ tadā saṃpetur āśugāḥ  RamS 
nārīṇām abhipūrṇās tu kāścit kāścit tu vājinām 
kaścit tatra vahanti sma yānayugyaṃ mahādhanam  RamS 
tāḥ sma gatvā paraṃ tīram avaropya ca taṃ janam 
nivṛttāḥ kāṇḍacitrāṇi kriyante dāśabandhubhiḥ  RamS 
savaijayantās tu gajā gajārohaiḥ pracoditāḥ 
tarantaḥ sma prakāśante sadhvajā iva parvatāḥ  RamS 
nāvaś cāruruhus tv anye plavais terus tathāpare 
anye kumbhaghaṭais terur anye teruś ca bāhubhiḥ  RamS 
sā puṇyā dhvajinī gaṅgāṃ dāśaiḥ saṃtāritā svayam 
maitre muhūrte prayayau prayāgavanam uttamam  RamS 
āśvāsayitvā ca camūṃ mahātmā niveśayitvā ca yathopajoṣam 
draṣṭuṃ bharadvājam ṛṣipravaryam ṛtvigvṛtaḥ san bharataḥ pratasthe  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
bharadvājāśramaṃ dṛṣṭvā krośād eva nararṣabhaḥ 
balaṃ sarvam avasthāpya jagāma saha mantribhiḥ  RamS 
padbhyām eva hi dharmajño nyastaśastraparicchadaḥ 
vasāno vāsasī kṣaume purodhāya purohitam  RamS 
tataḥ saṃdarśane tasya bharadvājasya rāghavaḥ 
mantriṇas tān avasthāpya jagāmānu purohitam  RamS 
vasiṣṭham atha dṛṣṭvaiva bharadvājo mahātapāḥ 
saṃcacālāsanāt tūrṇaṃ śiṣyān arghyam iti bruvan  RamS 
samāgamya vasiṣṭhena bharatenābhivāditaḥ 
abudhyata mahātejāḥ sutaṃ daśarathasya tam  RamS 
tābhyām arghyaṃ ca pādyaṃ ca dattvā paścāt phalāni ca 
ānupūrvyāc ca dharmajñaḥ papraccha kuśalaṃ kule  RamS 
ayodhyāyāṃ bale kośe mitreṣv api ca mantriṣu 
jānan daśarathaṃ vṛttaṃ na rājānam udāharat  RamS 
vasiṣṭho bharataś cainaṃ papracchatur anāmayam 
śarīre 'gniṣu vṛkṣeṣu śiṣyeṣu mṛgapakṣiṣu  RamS 
tatheti ca pratijñāya bharadvājo mahātapāḥ 
bharataṃ pratyuvācedaṃ rāghavasnehabandhanāt  RamS 
kim ihāgamane kāryaṃ tava rājyaṃ praśāsataḥ 
etad ācakṣva me sarvaṃ na hi me śudhyate manaḥ  RamS 
suṣuve yamamitraghnaṃ kausalyānandavardhanam 
bhrātrā saha sabhāryo yaś ciraṃ pravrājito vanam  RamS 
niyuktaḥ strīniyuktena pitrā yo 'sau mahāyaśāḥ 
vanavāsī bhavetīha samāḥ kila caturdaśa  RamS 
kaccin na tasyāpāpasya pāpaṃ kartum ihecchasi 
akaṇṭakaṃ bhoktumanā rājyaṃ tasyānujasya ca  RamS 
evam ukto bharadvājaṃ bharataḥ pratyuvāca ha 
paryaśrunayano duḥkhād vācā saṃsajjamānayā  RamS 
hato 'smi yadi mām evaṃ bhagavān api manyate 
matto na doṣam āśaṅker naivaṃ mām anuśādhi hi  RamS 
na caitad iṣṭaṃ mātā me yad avocan madantare 
nāham etena tuṣṭaś ca na tad vacanam ādade  RamS 
ahaṃ tu taṃ naravyāghram upayātaḥ prasādakaḥ 
pratinetum ayodhyāṃ ca pādau tasyābhivanditum  RamS 
tvaṃ mām evaṃ gataṃ matvā prasādaṃ kartum arhasi 
śaṃsa me bhagavan rāmaḥ kva samprati mahīpatiḥ  RamS 
uvāca taṃ bharadvājaḥ prasādād bharataṃ vacaḥ 
tvayy etat puruṣavyāghra yuktaṃ rāghavavaṃśaje 
guruvṛttir damaś caiva sādhūnāṃ cānuyāyitā  RamS 
jāne caitan manaḥsthaṃ te dṛḍhīkaraṇam astv iti 
apṛcchaṃ tvāṃ tavātyarthaṃ kīrtiṃ samabhivardhayan  RamS 
asau vasati te bhrātā citrakūṭe mahāgirau 
śvas tu gantāsi taṃ deśaṃ vasādya saha mantribhiḥ 
etaṃ me kuru suprājña kāmaṃ kāmārthakovida  RamS 
tatas tathety evam udāradarśanaḥ pratītarūpo bharato 'bravīd vacaḥ 
cakāra buddhiṃ ca tadā mahāśrame niśānivāsāya narādhipātmajaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
kṛtabuddhiṃ nivāsāya tathaiva sa munis tadā 
bharataṃ kaikayīputram ātithyena nyamantrayat  RamS 
abravīd bharatas tv enaṃ nanv idaṃ bhavatā kṛtam 
pādyam arghyaṃ tathātithyaṃ vane yad upapadyate  RamS 
athovāca bharadvājo bharataṃ prahasann iva 
jāne tvāṃ prītisaṃyuktaṃ tuṣyes tvaṃ yena kenacit  RamS 
senāyās tu tavaitasyāḥ kartum icchāmi bhojanam 
mama prītir yathārūpā tvam arho manujarṣabha  RamS 
kimarthaṃ cāpi nikṣipya dūre balam ihāgataḥ 
kasmān nehopayāto 'si sabalaḥ puruṣarṣabha  RamS 
bharataḥ pratyuvācedaṃ prāñjalis taṃ tapodhanam 
sasainyo nopayāto 'smi bhagavan bhagavadbhayāt  RamS 
vājimukhyā manuṣyāś ca mattāś ca varavāraṇāḥ 
pracchādya mahatīṃ bhūmiṃ bhagavann anuyānti mām  RamS 
te vṛkṣān udakaṃ bhūmim āśrameṣūṭajāṃs tathā 
na hiṃsyur iti tenāham eka evāgatas tataḥ  RamS 
ānīyatām itaḥ senety ājñaptaḥ paramarṣiṇā 
tathā tu cakre bharataḥ senāyāḥ samupāgamam  RamS 
agniśālāṃ praviśyātha pītvāpaḥ parimṛjya ca 
ātithyasya kriyāhetor viśvakarmāṇam āhvayat  RamS 
āhvaye viśvakarmāṇam ahaṃ tvaṣṭāram eva ca 
ātithyaṃ kartum icchāmi tatra me saṃvidhīyatām  RamS 
prāksrotasaś ca yā nadyaḥ pratyaksrotasa eva ca 
pṛthivyām antarikṣe ca samāyāntv adya sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
anyāḥ sravantu maireyaṃ surām anyāḥ suniṣṭhitām 
aparāś codakaṃ śītam ikṣukāṇḍarasopamam  RamS 
āhvaye devagandharvān viśvāvasuhahāhuhūn 
tathaivāpsaraso devīr gandharvīś cāpi sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
ghṛtācīm atha viśvācīṃ miśrakeśīm alambusām 
śakraṃ yāś copatiṣṭhanti brahmāṇaṃ yāś ca bhāminīḥ 
sarvās tumburuṇā sārdham āhvaye saparicchadāḥ  RamS 
vanaṃ kuruṣu yad divyaṃ vāso bhūṣaṇapattravat 
divyanārīphalaṃ śaśvat tat kauberam ihaiva tu  RamS 
iha me bhagavān somo vidhattām annam uttamam 
bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca coṣyaṃ ca lehyaṃ ca vividhaṃ bahu  RamS 
vicitrāṇi ca mālyāni pādapapracyutāni ca 
surādīni ca peyāni māṃsāni vividhāni ca  RamS 
evaṃ samādhinā yuktas tejasāpratimena ca 
śikṣāsvarasamāyuktaṃ tapasā cābravīn muniḥ  RamS 
manasā dhyāyatas tasya prāṅmukhasya kṛtāñjaleḥ 
ājagmus tāni sarvāṇi daivatāni pṛthakpṛthak  RamS 
malayaṃ darduraṃ caiva tataḥ svedanudo 'nilaḥ 
upaspṛśya vavau yuktyā supriyātmā sukhaḥ śivaḥ  RamS 
tato 'bhyavartanta ghanā divyāḥ kusumavṛṣṭayaḥ 
devadundubhighoṣaś ca dikṣu sarvāsu śuśruve  RamS 
pravavuś cottamā vātā nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥ 
prajagur devagandharvā vīṇāḥ pramumucuḥ svarān  RamS 
sa śabdo dyāṃ ca bhūmiṃ ca prāṇināṃ śravaṇāni ca 
viveśoccāritaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ samo layaguṇānvitaḥ  RamS 
tasminn uparate śabde divye śrotrasukhe nṛṇām 
dadarśa bhārataṃ sainyaṃ vidhānaṃ viśvakarmaṇaḥ  RamS 
babhūva hi samā bhūmiḥ samantāt pañcayojanam 
śādvalair bahubhiś channā nīlavaiḍūryasaṃnibhaiḥ  RamS 
tasmin bilvāḥ kapitthāś ca panasā bījapūrakāḥ 
āmalakyo babhūvuś ca cūtāś ca phalabhūṣaṇāḥ  RamS 
uttarebhyaḥ kurubhyaś ca vanaṃ divyopabhogavat 
ājagāma nadī divyā tīrajair bahubhir vṛtā  RamS 
catuḥśālāni śubhrāṇi śālāś ca gajavājinām 
harmyaprāsādasaṃghātās toraṇāni śubhāni ca  RamS 
sitameghanibhaṃ cāpi rājaveśma sutoraṇam 
śuklamālyakṛtākāraṃ divyagandhasamukṣitam  RamS 
caturasram asaṃbādhaṃ śayanāsanayānavat 
divyaiḥ sarvarasair yuktaṃ divyabhojanavastravat  RamS 
upakalpitasarvānnaṃ dhautanirmalabhājanam 
kḷptasarvāsanaṃ śrīmat svāstīrṇaśayanottamam  RamS 
praviveśa mahābāhur anujñāto maharṣiṇā 
veśma tad ratnasampūrṇaṃ bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ  RamS 
anujagmuś ca taṃ sarve mantriṇaḥ sapurohitāḥ 
babhūvuś ca mudā yuktās taṃ dṛṣṭvā veśmasaṃvidhim  RamS 
tatra rājāsanaṃ divyaṃ vyajanaṃ chattram eva ca 
bharato mantribhiḥ sārdham abhyavartata rājavat  RamS 
āsanaṃ pūjayāmāsa rāmāyābhipraṇamya ca 
vālavyajanam ādāya nyaṣīdat sacivāsane  RamS 
ānupūrvyān niṣeduś ca sarve mantripurohitāḥ 
tataḥ senāpatiḥ paścāt praśāstā ca niṣedatuḥ  RamS 
tatas tatra muhūrtena nadyaḥ pāyasakardamāḥ 
upātiṣṭhanta bharataṃ bharadvājasya śāsanāt  RamS 
tāsām ubhayataḥ kūlaṃ pāṇḍumṛttikalepanāḥ 
ramyāś cāvasathā divyā brahmaṇas tu prasādajāḥ  RamS 
tenaiva ca muhūrtena divyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ 
āgur viṃśatisāhasrā brahmaṇā prahitāḥ striyaḥ  RamS 
suvarṇamaṇimuktena pravālena ca śobhitāḥ 
āgur viṃśatisāhasrāḥ kuberaprahitāḥ striyaḥ  RamS 
yābhir gṛhītaḥ puruṣaḥ sonmāda iva lakṣyate 
āgur viṃśatisāhasrā nandanād apsarogaṇāḥ  RamS 
nāradas tumburur gopaḥ parvataḥ sūryavarcasaḥ 
ete gandharvarājāno bharatasyāgrato jaguḥ  RamS 
alambusā miśrakeśī puṇḍarīkātha vāmanā 
upānṛtyaṃs tu bharataṃ bharadvājasya śāsanāt  RamS 
yāni mālyāni deveṣu yāni caitrarathe vane 
prayāge tāny adṛśyanta bharadvājasya śāsanāt  RamS
