bilvā mārdaṅgikā āsañ śamyāgrāhā vibhītakāḥ 
aśvatthā nartakāś cāsan bharadvājasya tejasā  RamS 
tataḥ saralatālāś ca tilakā naktamālakāḥ 
prahṛṣṭās tatra saṃpetuḥ kubjā bhūtvātha vāmanāḥ  RamS 
śiṃśapāmalakī jambūr yāś cānyāḥ kānane latāḥ 
pramadāvigrahaṃ kṛtvā bharadvājāśrame 'vasan  RamS 
surāṃ surāpāḥ pibata pāyasaṃ ca bubhukṣitāḥ 
māṃsāni ca sumedhyāni bhakṣyantāṃ yāvad icchatha  RamS 
utsādya snāpayanti sma nadītīreṣu valguṣu 
apy ekam ekaṃ puruṣaṃ pramadāḥ sapta cāṣṭa ca  RamS 
saṃvahantyaḥ samāpetur nāryo ruciralocanāḥ 
parimṛjya tathā nyāyaṃ pāyayanti varāṅganāḥ  RamS 
hayān gajān kharān uṣṭrāṃs tathaiva surabheḥ sutān 
ikṣūṃś ca madhujālāṃś ca bhojayanti sma vāhanān 
ikṣvākuvarayodhānāṃ codayanto mahābalāḥ  RamS 
nāśvabandho 'śvam ājānān na gajaṃ kuñjaragrahaḥ 
mattapramattamuditā camūḥ sā tatra saṃbabhau  RamS 
tarpitāḥ sarvakāmais te raktacandanarūṣitāḥ 
apsarogaṇasaṃyuktāḥ sainyā vācam udairayan  RamS 
naivāyodhyāṃ gamiṣyāmo na gamiṣyāma daṇḍakān 
kuśalaṃ bharatasyāstu rāmasyāstu tathā sukham  RamS 
iti pādātayodhāś ca hastyaśvārohabandhakāḥ 
anāthās taṃ vidhiṃ labdhvā vācam etām udairayan  RamS 
samprahṛṣṭā vinedus te narās tatra sahasraśaḥ 
bharatasyānuyātāraḥ svargo 'yam iti cābruvan  RamS 
tato bhuktavatāṃ teṣāṃ tad annam amṛtopamam 
divyān udvīkṣya bhakṣyāṃs tān abhavad bhakṣaṇe matiḥ  RamS 
preṣyāś ceṭyaś ca vadhvaś ca balasthāś cāpi sarvaśaḥ 
babhūvus te bhṛśaṃ tṛptāḥ sarve cāhatavāsasaḥ  RamS 
kuñjarāś ca kharoṣṭraś ca go'śvāś ca mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ 
babhūvuḥ subhṛtās tatra nānyo hy anyam akalpayat  RamS 
nāśuklavāsās tatrāsīt kṣudhito malino 'pi vā 
rajasā dhvastakeśo vā naraḥ kaścid adṛśyata  RamS 
ājaiś cāpi ca vārāhair niṣṭhānavarasaṃcayaiḥ 
phalaniryūhasaṃsiddhaiḥ sūpair gandharasānvitaiḥ  RamS 
puṣpadhvajavatīḥ pūrṇāḥ śuklasyānnasya cābhitaḥ 
dadṛśur vismitās tatra narā lauhīḥ sahasraśaḥ  RamS 
babhūvur vanapārśveṣu kūpāḥ pāyasakardamāḥ 
tāś ca kāmadughā gāvo drumāś cāsan madhuścyutaḥ  RamS 
vāpyo maireyapūrṇāś ca mṛṣṭamāṃsacayair vṛtāḥ 
prataptapiṭharaiś cāpi mārgamāyūrakaukkuṭaiḥ  RamS 
pātrīṇāṃ ca sahasrāṇi śātakumbhamayāni ca 
sthālyaḥ kumbhyaḥ karambhyaś ca dadhipūrṇāḥ susaṃskṛtāḥ 
yauvanasthasya gaurasya kapitthasya sugandhinaḥ  RamS 
hradāḥ pūrṇā rasālasya dadhnaḥ śvetasya cāpare 
babhūvuḥ pāyasasyānte śarkarāyāś ca saṃcayāḥ  RamS 
kalkāṃś cūrṇakaṣāyāṃś ca snānāni vividhāni ca 
dadṛśur bhājanasthāni tīrtheṣu saritāṃ narāḥ  RamS 
śuklān aṃśumataś cāpi dantadhāvanasaṃcayān 
śuklāṃś candanakalkāṃś ca samudgeṣv avatiṣṭhataḥ  RamS 
darpaṇān parimṛṣṭāṃś ca vāsasāṃ cāpi saṃcayān 
pādukopānahāṃ caiva yugmān yatra sahasraśaḥ  RamS 
āñjanīḥ kaṅkatān kūrcāṃś chattrāṇi ca dhanūṃṣi ca 
marmatrāṇāni citrāṇi śayanāny āsanāni ca  RamS 
pratipānahradān pūrṇān kharoṣṭragajavājinām 
avagāhya sutīrthāṃś ca hradān sotpalapuṣkarān  RamS 
nīlavaiḍūryavarṇāṃś ca mṛdūn yavasasaṃcayān 
nirvāpārthaṃ paśūnāṃ te dadṛśus tatra sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
vyasmayanta manuṣyās te svapnakalpaṃ tad adbhutam 
dṛṣṭvātithyaṃ kṛtaṃ tādṛg bharatasya maharṣiṇā  RamS 
ity evaṃ ramamāṇānāṃ devānām iva nandane 
bharadvājāśrame ramye sā rātrir vyatyavartata  RamS 
pratijagmuś ca tā nadyo gandharvāś ca yathāgatam 
bharadvājam anujñāpya tāś ca sarvā varāṅganāḥ  RamS 
tathaiva mattā madirotkaṭā narās tathaiva divyāgurucandanokṣitāḥ 
tathaiva divyā vividhāḥ sraguttamāḥ pṛthakprakīrṇā manujaiḥ pramarditāḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tatas tāṃ rajanīm uṣya bharataḥ saparicchadaḥ 
kṛtātithyo bharadvājaṃ kāmād abhijagāma ha  RamS 
tam ṛṣiḥ puruṣavyāghraṃ prekṣya prāñjalim āgatam 
hutāgnihotro bharataṃ bharadvājo 'bhyabhāṣata  RamS 
kaccid atra sukhā rātris tavāsmadviṣaye gatā 
samagras te janaḥ kaccid ātithye śaṃsa me 'nagha  RamS 
tam uvācāñjaliṃ kṛtvā bharato 'bhipraṇamya ca 
āśramād abhiniṣkrāntam ṛṣim uttamatejasam  RamS 
sukhoṣito 'smi bhagavan samagrabalavāhanaḥ 
tarpitaḥ sarvakāmaiś ca sāmātyo balavat tvayā  RamS 
apetaklamasaṃtāpāḥ subhikṣāḥ supratiśrayāḥ 
api preṣyān upādāya sarve sma susukhoṣitāḥ  RamS 
āmantraye 'haṃ bhagavan kāmaṃ tvām ṛṣisattama 
samīpaṃ prasthitaṃ bhrātur maitreṇekṣasva cakṣuṣā  RamS 
āśramaṃ tasya dharmajña dhārmikasya mahātmanaḥ 
ācakṣva katamo mārgaḥ kiyān iti ca śaṃsa me  RamS 
iti pṛṣṭas tu bharataṃ bhrātṛdarśanalālasam 
pratyuvāca mahātejā bharadvājo mahātapāḥ  RamS 
bharatārdhatṛtīyeṣu yojaneṣv ajane vane 
citrakūṭo giris tatra ramyanirdarakānanaḥ  RamS 
uttaraṃ pārśvam āsādya tasya mandākinī nadī 
puṣpitadrumasaṃchannā ramyapuṣpitakānanā  RamS 
anantaraṃ tat saritaś citrakūṭaś ca parvataḥ 
tayoḥ parṇakuṭī tāta tatra tau vasato dhruvam  RamS 
dakṣiṇenaiva mārgeṇa savyadakṣiṇam eva ca 
gajavājirathākīrṇāṃ vāhinīṃ vāhinīpate 
vāhayasva mahābhāga tato drakṣyasi rāghavam  RamS 
prayāṇam iti ca śrutvā rājarājasya yoṣitaḥ 
hitvā yānāni yānārhā brāhmaṇaṃ paryavārayan  RamS 
vepamānā kṛśā dīnā saha devyā sumitrayā 
kausalyā tatra jagrāha karābhyāṃ caraṇau muneḥ  RamS 
asamṛddhena kāmena sarvalokasya garhitā 
kaikeyī tasya jagrāha caraṇau savyapatrapā  RamS 
taṃ pradakṣiṇam āgamya bhagavantaṃ mahāmunim 
adūrād bharatasyaiva tasthau dīnamanās tadā  RamS 
tataḥ papraccha bharataṃ bharadvājo dṛḍhavrataḥ 
viśeṣaṃ jñātum icchāmi mātḥṇāṃ tava rāghava  RamS 
evam uktas tu bharato bharadvājena dhārmikaḥ 
uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā vākyaṃ vacanakovidaḥ  RamS 
yām imāṃ bhagavan dīnāṃ śokānaśanakarśitām 
pitur hi mahiṣīṃ devīṃ devatām iva paśyasi  RamS 
eṣā taṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ siṃhavikrāntagāminam 
kausalyā suṣuve rāmaṃ dhātāram aditir yathā  RamS 
asyā vāmabhujaṃ śliṣṭā yaiṣā tiṣṭhati durmanāḥ 
karṇikārasya śākheva śīrṇapuṣpā vanāntare  RamS 
etasyās tau sutau devyāḥ kumārau devavarṇinau 
ubhau lakṣmaṇaśatrughnau vīrau satyaparākramau  RamS 
yasyāḥ kṛte naravyāghrau jīvanāśam ito gatau 
rājā putravihīnaś ca svargaṃ daśaratho gataḥ  RamS 
aiśvaryakāmāṃ kaikeyīm anāryām āryarūpiṇīm 
mamaitāṃ mātaraṃ viddhi nṛśaṃsāṃ pāpaniścayām 
yatomūlaṃ hi paśyāmi vyasanaṃ mahad ātmanaḥ  RamS 
ity uktvā naraśārdūlo bāṣpagadgadayā girā 
sa niśaśvāsa tāmrākṣo nāgaḥ kruddha ivāsakṛt  RamS 
bharadvājo maharṣis taṃ bruvantaṃ bharataṃ tadā 
pratyuvāca mahābuddhir idaṃ vacanam arthavat  RamS 
na doṣeṇāvagantavyā kaikeyī bharata tvayā 
rāmapravrājanaṃ hy etat sukhodarkaṃ bhaviṣyati  RamS 
abhivādya tu saṃsiddhaḥ kṛtvā cainaṃ pradakṣiṇam 
āmantrya bharataḥ sainyaṃ yujyatām ity acodayat  RamS 
tato vājirathān yuktvā divyān hemapariṣkṛtān 
adhyārohat prayāṇārthī bahūn bahuvidho janaḥ  RamS 
gajakanyāgajāś caiva hemakakṣyāḥ patākinaḥ 
jīmūtā iva gharmānte saghoṣāḥ sampratasthire  RamS 
vividhāny api yānāni mahānti ca laghūni ca 
prayayuḥ sumahārhāṇi pādair eva padātayaḥ  RamS 
atha yānapravekais tu kausalyāpramukhāḥ striyaḥ 
rāmadarśanakāṅkṣiṇyaḥ prayayur muditās tadā  RamS 
sa cārkataruṇābhāsāṃ niyuktāṃ śibikāṃ śubhām 
āsthāya prayayau śrīmān bharataḥ saparicchadaḥ  RamS 
sā prayātā mahāsenā gajavājirathākulā 
dakṣiṇāṃ diśam āvṛtya mahāmegha ivotthitaḥ 
vanāni tu vyatikramya juṣṭāni mṛgapakṣibhiḥ  RamS 
sā samprahṛṣṭadvipavājiyodhā vitrāsayantī mṛgapakṣisaṃghān 
mahad vanaṃ tat pravigāhamānā rarāja senā bharatasya tatra  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tayā mahatyā yāyinyā dhvajinyā vanavāsinaḥ 
arditā yūthapā mattāḥ sayūthāḥ sampradudruvuḥ  RamS 
ṛkṣāḥ pṛṣatasaṃghāś ca ruravaś ca samantataḥ 
dṛśyante vanarājīṣu giriṣv api nadīṣu ca  RamS 
sa sampratasthe dharmātmā prīto daśarathātmajaḥ 
vṛto mahatyā nādinyā senayā caturaṅgayā  RamS 
sāgaraughanibhā senā bharatasya mahātmanaḥ 
mahīṃ saṃchādayāmāsa prāvṛṣi dyām ivāmbudaḥ  RamS 
turaṃgaughair avatatā vāraṇaiś ca mahājavaiḥ 
anālakṣyā ciraṃ kālaṃ tasmin kāle babhūva bhūḥ  RamS 
sa yātvā dūram adhvānaṃ supariśrāntavāhanaḥ 
uvāca bharataḥ śrīmān vasiṣṭhaṃ mantriṇāṃ varam  RamS 
yādṛśaṃ lakṣyate rūpaṃ yathā caiva śrutaṃ mayā 
vyaktaṃ prāptāḥ sma taṃ deśaṃ bharadvājo yam abravīt  RamS 
ayaṃ giriś citrakūṭas tathā mandākinī nadī 
etat prakāśate dūrān nīlameghanibhaṃ vanam  RamS 
gireḥ sānūni ramyāṇi citrakūṭasya samprati 
vāraṇair avamṛdyante māmakaiḥ parvatopamaiḥ  RamS 
muñcanti kusumāny ete nagāḥ parvatasānuṣu 
nīlā ivātapāpāye toyaṃ toyadharā ghanāḥ  RamS 
kiṃnarācaritoddeśaṃ paśya śatrughna parvatam 
hayaiḥ samantād ākīrṇaṃ makarair iva sāgaram  RamS 
ete mṛgagaṇā bhānti śīghravegāḥ pracoditāḥ 
vāyupraviddhāḥ śaradi megharājir ivāmbare  RamS 
kurvanti kusumāpīḍāñ śiraḥsu surabhīn amī 
meghaprakāśaiḥ phalakair dākṣiṇātyā yathā narāḥ  RamS 
niṣkūjam iva bhūtvedaṃ vanaṃ ghorapradarśanam 
ayodhyeva janākīrṇā samprati pratibhāti mā  RamS 
khurair udīrito reṇur divaṃ pracchādya tiṣṭhati 
taṃ vahaty anilaḥ śīghraṃ kurvann iva mama priyam  RamS 
syandanāṃs turagopetān sūtamukhyair adhiṣṭhitān 
etān saṃpatataḥ śīghraṃ paśya śatrughna kānane  RamS 
etān vitrāsitān paśya barhiṇaḥ priyadarśanān 
etam āviśataḥ śailam adhivāsaṃ patatriṇām  RamS 
atimātram ayaṃ deśo manojñaḥ pratibhāti mā 
tāpasānāṃ nivāso 'yaṃ vyaktaṃ svargapatho yathā  RamS 
mṛgā mṛgībhiḥ sahitā bahavaḥ pṛṣatā vane 
manojñarūpā lakṣyante kusumair iva citritāḥ  RamS 
sādhu sainyāḥ pratiṣṭhantāṃ vicinvantu ca kānanam 
yathā tau puruṣavyāghrau dṛśyete rāmalakṣmaṇau  RamS 
bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā puruṣāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ 
viviśus tad vanaṃ śūrā dhūmaṃ ca dadṛśus tataḥ  RamS 
te samālokya dhūmāgram ūcur bharatam āgatāḥ 
nāmanuṣye bhavaty agnir vyaktam atraiva rāghavau  RamS 
atha nātra naravyāghrau rājaputrau paraṃtapau 
anye rāmopamāḥ santi vyaktam atra tapasvinaḥ  RamS 
tac chrutvā bharatas teṣāṃ vacanaṃ sādhusaṃmatam 
sainyān uvāca sarvāṃs tān amitrabalamardanaḥ  RamS 
yattā bhavantas tiṣṭhantu neto gantavyam agrataḥ 
aham eva gamiṣyāmi sumantro gurur eva ca  RamS 
evam uktās tataḥ sarve tatra tasthuḥ samantataḥ 
bharato yatra dhūmāgraṃ tatra dṛṣṭiṃ samādadhāt  RamS 
vyavasthitā yā bharatena sā camūr nirīkṣamāṇāpi ca dhūmam agrataḥ 
babhūva hṛṣṭā nacireṇa jānatī priyasya rāmasya samāgamaṃ tadā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
dīrghakāloṣitas tasmin girau girivanapriyaḥ 
vaidehyāḥ priyamākāṅkṣan svaṃ ca cittaṃ vilobhayan  RamS 
atha dāśarathiś citraṃ citrakūṭam adarśayat 
bhāryām amarasaṃkāśaḥ śacīm iva puraṃdaraḥ  RamS 
na rājyād bhraṃśanaṃ bhadre na suhṛdbhir vinābhavaḥ 
mano me bādhate dṛṣṭvā ramaṇīyam imaṃ girim  RamS 
paśyemam acalaṃ bhadre nānādvijagaṇāyutam 
śikharaiḥ kham ivodviddhair dhātumadbhir vibhūṣitam  RamS 
kecid rajatasaṃkāśāḥ kecit kṣatajasaṃnibhāḥ 
pītamāñjiṣṭhavarṇāś ca kecin maṇivaraprabhāḥ  RamS 
puṣpārkaketakābhāś ca kecij jyotīrasaprabhāḥ 
virājante 'calendrasya deśā dhātuvibhūṣitāḥ  RamS 
nānāmṛgagaṇadvīpitarakṣvṛkṣagaṇair vṛtaḥ 
aduṣṭair bhāty ayaṃ śailo bahupakṣisamākulaḥ  RamS 
āmrajambvasanair lodhraiḥ priyālaiḥ panasair dhavaiḥ 
aṅkolair bhavyatiniśair bilvatindukaveṇubhiḥ  RamS 
kāśmaryariṣṭavaraṇair madhūkais tilakais tathā 
badaryāmalakair nīpair vetradhanvanabījakaiḥ  RamS 
puṣpavadbhiḥ phalopetaiś chāyāvadbhir manoramaiḥ 
evamādibhir ākīrṇaḥ śriyaṃ puṣyaty ayaṃ giriḥ  RamS 
śailaprastheṣu ramyeṣu paśyemān kāmaharṣaṇān 
kiṃnarān dvaṃdvaśo bhadre ramamāṇān manasvinaḥ  RamS 
śākhāvasaktān khaḍgāṃś ca pravarāṇy ambarāṇi ca 
paśya vidyādharastrīṇāṃ krīḍoddeśān manoramān  RamS 
jalaprapātair udbhedair nisyandaiś ca kvacit kvacit 
sravadbhir bhāty ayaṃ śailaḥ sravan mada iva dvipaḥ  RamS 
guhāsamīraṇo gandhān nānāpuṣpabhavān vahan 
ghrāṇatarpaṇam abhyetya kaṃ naraṃ na praharṣayet  RamS 
yadīha śarado 'nekās tvayā sārdham anindite 
lakṣmaṇena ca vatsyāmi na māṃ śokaḥ pradhakṣyati  RamS 
bahupuṣpaphale ramye nānādvijagaṇāyute 
vicitraśikhare hy asmin ratavān asmi bhāmini  RamS 
anena vanavāsena mayā prāptaṃ phaladvayam 
pituś cānṛṇatā dharme bharatasya priyaṃ tathā  RamS 
vaidehi ramase kaccic citrakūṭe mayā saha 
paśyantī vividhān bhāvān manovākkāyasaṃyatān  RamS 
idam evāmṛtaṃ prāhū rājñāṃ rājarṣayaḥ pare 
vanavāsaṃ bhavārthāya pretya me prapitāmahāḥ  RamS 
śilāḥ śailasya śobhante viśālāḥ śataśo 'bhitaḥ 
bahulā bahulair varṇair nīlapītasitāruṇaiḥ  RamS 
niśi bhānty acalendrasya hutāśanaśikhā iva 
oṣadhyaḥ svaprabhā lakṣmyā bhrājamānāḥ sahasraśaḥ  RamS 
kecit kṣayanibhā deśāḥ kecid udyānasaṃnibhāḥ 
kecid ekaśilā bhānti parvatasyāsya bhāmini  RamS 
bhittveva vasudhāṃ bhāti citrakūṭaḥ samutthitaḥ 
citrakūṭasya kūṭo 'sau dṛśyate sarvataḥ śivaḥ  RamS 
kuṣṭhapuṃnāgatagarabhūrjapatrottarachadān 
kāmināṃ svāstarān paśya kuśeśayadalāyutān  RamS 
mṛditāś cāpaviddhāś ca dṛśyante kamalasrajaḥ 
kāmibhir vanite paśya phalāni vividhāni ca  RamS 
vasvaukasārāṃ nalinīm atyetīvottarān kurūn 
parvataś citrakūṭo 'sau bahumūlaphalodakaḥ  RamS 
imaṃ tu kālaṃ vanite vijahrivāṃs tvayā ca sīte saha lakṣmaṇena ca 
ratiṃ prapatsye kuladharmavardhinīṃ satāṃ pathi svair niyamaiḥ paraiḥ sthitaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
atha śailād viniṣkramya maithilīṃ kosaleśvaraḥ 
adarśayac chubhajalāṃ ramyāṃ mandākinīṃ nadīm  RamS 
abravīc ca varārohāṃ cārucandranibhānanām 
videharājasya sutāṃ rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ  RamS 
vicitrapulināṃ ramyāṃ haṃsasārasasevitām 
kusumair upasaṃpannāṃ paśya mandākinīṃ nadīm  RamS 
nānāvidhais tīraruhair vṛtāṃ puṣpaphaladrumaiḥ 
rājantīṃ rājarājasya nalinīm iva sarvataḥ  RamS 
mṛgayūthanipītāni kaluṣāmbhāṃsi sāmpratam 
tīrthāni ramaṇīyāni ratiṃ saṃjanayanti me  RamS 
jaṭājinadharāḥ kāle valkalottaravāsasaḥ 
ṛṣayas tv avagāhante nadīṃ mandākinīṃ priye  RamS 
ādityam upatiṣṭhante niyamād ūrdhvabāhavaḥ 
ete 'pare viśālākṣi munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ  RamS 
mārutoddhūtaśikharaiḥ pranṛtta iva parvataḥ 
pādapaiḥ pattrapuṣpāṇi sṛjadbhir abhito nadīm  RamS 
kaccin maṇinikāśodāṃ kaccit pulinaśālinīm 
kaccit siddhajanākīrṇāṃ paśya mandākinīṃ nadīm  RamS 
nirdhūtān vāyunā paśya vitatān puṣpasaṃcayān 
poplūyamānān aparān paśya tvaṃ jalamadhyagān  RamS 
tāṃś cātivalguvacaso rathāṅgāhvayanā dvijāḥ 
adhirohanti kalyāṇi niṣkūjantaḥ śubhā giraḥ  RamS 
darśanaṃ citrakūṭasya mandākinyāś ca śobhane 
adhikaṃ puravāsāc ca manye ca tava darśanāt  RamS 
vidhūtakaluṣaiḥ siddhais tapodamaśamānvitaiḥ 
nityavikṣobhitajalāṃ vigāhasva mayā saha  RamS 
sakhīvac ca vigāhasva sīte mandākinīm imām 
kamalāny avamajjantī puṣkarāṇi ca bhāmini  RamS 
tvaṃ paurajanavad vyālān ayodhyām iva parvatam 
manyasva vanite nityaṃ sarayūvad imāṃ nadīm  RamS 
lakṣmaṇaś caiva dharmātmā mannideśe vyavasthitaḥ 
tvaṃ cānukūlā vaidehi prītiṃ janayatho mama  RamS 
upaspṛśaṃs triṣavaṇaṃ madhumūlaphalāśanaḥ 
nāyodhyāyai na rājyāya spṛhaye 'dya tvayā saha  RamS 
imāṃ hi ramyāṃ gajayūthalolitāṃ nipītatoyāṃ gajasiṃhavānaraiḥ 
supuṣpitaiḥ puṣpadharair alaṃkṛtāṃ na so 'sti yaḥ syān na gatakramaḥ sukhī  RamS 
itīva rāmo bahusaṃgataṃ vacaḥ priyāsahāyaḥ saritaṃ prati bruvan 
cacāra ramyaṃ nayanāñjanaprabhaṃ sa citrakūṭaṃ raghuvaṃśavardhanaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tathā tatrāsatas tasya bharatasyopayāyinaḥ 
sainyareṇuś ca śabdaś ca prādurāstāṃ nabhaḥspṛśau  RamS 
etasminn antare trastāḥ śabdena mahatā tataḥ 
arditā yūthapā mattāḥ sayūthā dudruvur diśaḥ  RamS 
sa taṃ sainyasamudbhūtaṃ śabdaṃ śuśrava rāghavaḥ 
tāṃś ca vipradrutān sarvān yūthapān anvavaikṣata  RamS 
tāṃś ca vidravato dṛṣṭvā taṃ ca śrutvā sa niḥsvanam 
uvāca rāmaḥ saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasam  RamS 
hanta lakṣmaṇa paśyeha sumitrā suprajās tvayā 
bhīmastanitagambhīras tumulaḥ śrūyate svanaḥ  RamS 
rājā vā rājamātro vā mṛgayām aṭate vane 
anyad vā śvāpadaṃ kiṃcit saumitre jñātum arhasi 
sarvam etad yathātattvam acirāj jñātum arhasi  RamS 
sa lakṣmaṇaḥ saṃtvaritaḥ sālam āruhya puṣpitam 
prekṣamāṇo diśaḥ sarvāḥ pūrvāṃ diśam avaikṣata  RamS 
udaṅmukhaḥ prekṣamāṇo dadarśa mahatīṃ camūm 
rathāśvagajasambādhāṃ yattair yuktāṃ padātibhiḥ  RamS 
tām aśvagajasampūrṇāṃ rathadhvajavibhūṣitām 
śaśaṃsa senāṃ rāmāya vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  RamS 
agniṃ saṃśamayatv āryaḥ sītā ca bhajatāṃ guhām 
sajyaṃ kuruṣva cāpaṃ ca śarāṃś ca kavacaṃ tathā  RamS 
taṃ rāmaḥ puruṣavyāghro lakṣmaṇaṃ pratyuvāca ha 
aṅgāvekṣasva saumitre kasyaitāṃ manyase camūm  RamS 
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇo vākyam abravīt 
didhakṣann iva tāṃ senāṃ ruṣitaḥ pāvako yathā  RamS 
sampannaṃ rājyam icchaṃs tu vyaktaṃ prāpyābhiṣecanam 
āvāṃ hantuṃ samabhyeti kaikeyyā bharataḥ sutaḥ  RamS 
eṣa vai sumahāñ śrīmān viṭapī saṃprakāśate 
virājaty udgataskandhaḥ kovidāradhvajo rathe  RamS 
bhajanty ete yathākāmam aśvān āruhya śīghragān 
ete bhrājanti saṃhṛṣṭā gajān āruhya sādinaḥ  RamS 
gṛhītadhanuṣau cāvāṃ giriṃ vīra śrayāvahe 
api nau vaśam āgacchet kovidāradhvajo raṇe  RamS 
api drakṣyāmi bharataṃ yatkṛte vyasanaṃ mahat 
tvayā rāghava samprāptaṃ sītayā ca mayā tathā  RamS 
yannimittaṃ bhavān rājyāc cyuto rāghava śāśvatāt 
samprāpto 'yam arir vīra bharato vadhya eva me  RamS 
bharatasya vadhe doṣaṃ nāhaṃ paśyāmi rāghava 
pūrvāpakāriṇāṃ tyāge na hy adharmo vidhīyate 
etasmin nihate kṛtsnām anuśādhi vasuṃdharām  RamS 
adya putraṃ hataṃ saṃkhye kaikeyī rājyakāmukā 
mayā paśyet suduḥkhārtā hastibhagnam iva drumam  RamS 
kaikeyīṃ ca vadhiṣyāmi sānubandhāṃ sabāndhavām 
kaluṣeṇādya mahatā medinī parimucyatām  RamS 
adyemaṃ saṃyataṃ krodham asatkāraṃ ca mānada 
mokṣyāmi śatrusainyeṣu kakṣeṣv iva hutāśanam  RamS 
adyaitac citrakūṭasya kānanaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ 
bhindañ śatruśarīrāṇi kariṣye śoṇitokṣitam  RamS 
śarair nirbhinnahṛdayān kuñjarāṃs turagāṃs tathā 
śvāpadāḥ parikarṣantu narāṃś ca nihatān mayā  RamS 
śarāṇāṃ dhanuṣaś cāham anṛṇo 'smi mahāvane 
sasainyaṃ bharataṃ hatvā bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
susaṃrabdhaṃ tu saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ krodhamūrchitam 
rāmas tu parisāntvyātha vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  RamS 
kim atra dhanuṣā kāryam asinā vā sacarmaṇā 
maheṣvāse mahāprājñe bharate svayam āgate  RamS 
prāptakālaṃ yad eṣo 'smān bharato draṣṭum icchati 
asmāsu manasāpy eṣa nāhitaṃ kiṃcid ācaret  RamS 
vipriyaṃ kṛtapūrvaṃ te bharatena kadā na kim 
īdṛśaṃ vā bhayaṃ te 'dya bharataṃ yo 'tra śaṅkase  RamS 
na hi te niṣṭhuraṃ vācyo bharato nāpriyaṃ vacaḥ 
ahaṃ hy apriyam uktaḥ syāṃ bharatasyāpriye kṛte  RamS 
kathaṃ nu putrāḥ pitaraṃ hanyuḥ kasyāṃcid āpadi 
bhrātā vā bhrātaraṃ hanyāt saumitre prāṇam ātmanaḥ  RamS 
yadi rājyasya hetos tvam imāṃ vācaṃ prabhāṣase 
vakṣyāmi bharataṃ dṛṣṭvā rājyam asmai pradīyatām  RamS 
ucyamāno hi bharato mayā lakṣmaṇa tattvataḥ 
rājyam asmai prayaccheti bāḍham ity eva vakṣyati  RamS 
tathokto dharmaśīlena bhrātrā tasya hite rataḥ 
lakṣmaṇaḥ praviveśeva svāni gātrāṇi lajjayā  RamS 
vrīḍitaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ pratyuvāca ha 
eṣa manye mahābāhur ihāsmān draṣṭum āgataḥ  RamS 
vanavāsam anudhyāya gṛhāya pratineṣyati 
imāṃ vāpy eṣa vaidehīm atyantasukhasevinīm  RamS 
etau tau saṃprakāśete gotravantau manoramau 
vāyuvegasamau vīra javanau turagottamau  RamS 
sa eṣa sumahākāyaḥ kampate vāhinīmukhe 
nāgaḥ śatruṃjayo nāma vṛddhas tātasya dhīmataḥ  RamS 
avatīrya tu sālāgrāt tasmāt sa samitiṃjayaḥ 
lakṣmaṇaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā tasthau rāmasya pārśvataḥ  RamS 
bharatenātha saṃdiṣṭā sammardo na bhaved iti 
samantāt tasya śailasya senāvāsam akalpayat  RamS 
adhyardham ikṣvākucamūr yojanaṃ parvatasya sā 
pārśve nyaviśad āvṛtya gajavājirathākulā  RamS 
sā citrakūṭe bharatena senā dharmaṃ puraskṛtya vidhūya darpam 
prasādanārthaṃ raghunandanasya virocate nītimatā praṇītā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
niveśya senāṃ tu vibhuḥ padbhyāṃ pādavatāṃ varaḥ 
abhigantuṃ sa kākutstham iyeṣa guruvartakam  RamS 
niviṣṭamātre sainye tu yathoddeśaṃ vinītavat 
bharato bhrātaraṃ vākyaṃ śatrughnam idam abravīt  RamS 
kṣipraṃ vanam idaṃ saumya narasaṃghaiḥ samantataḥ 
lubdhaiś ca sahitair ebhis tvam anveṣitum arhasi  RamS 
yāvan na rāmaṃ drakṣyāmi lakṣmaṇaṃ vā mahābalam 
vaidehīṃ vā mahābhāgāṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  RamS 
yāvan na candrasaṃkāśaṃ drakṣyāmi śubham ānanam 
bhrātuḥ padmapalāśākṣaṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  RamS 
yāvan na caraṇau bhrātuḥ pārthivavyañjanānvitau 
śirasā dhārayiṣyāmi na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  RamS 
yāvan na rājye rājyārhaḥ pitṛpaitāmahe sthitaḥ 
abhiṣekajalaklinno na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  RamS 
kṛtakṛtyā mahābhāgā vaidehī janakātmajā 
bhartāraṃ sāgarāntāyāḥ pṛthivyā yānugacchati  RamS 
subhagaś citrakūṭo 'sau girirājopamo giriḥ 
yasmin vasati kākutsthaḥ kubera iva nandane  RamS 
kṛtakāryam idaṃ durgaṃ vanaṃ vyālaniṣevitam 
yad adhyāste mahātejā rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ  RamS 
evam uktvā mahātejā bharataḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ 
padbhyām eva mahātejāḥ praviveśa mahad vanam  RamS 
sa tāni drumajālāni jātāni girisānuṣu 
puṣpitāgrāṇi madhyena jagāma vadatāṃ varaḥ  RamS 
sa gireś citrakūṭasya sālam āsādya puṣpitam 
rāmāśramagatasyāgner dadarśa dhvajam ucchritam  RamS 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bharataḥ śrīmān mumoda sahabāndhavaḥ 
atra rāma iti jñātvā gataḥ pāram ivāmbhasaḥ  RamS 
sa citrakūṭe tu girau niśāmya rāmāśramaṃ puṇyajanopapannam 
guhena sārdhaṃ tvarito jagāma punar niveśyaiva camūṃ mahātmā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
niviṣṭāyāṃ tu senāyām utsuko bharatas tadā 
jagāma bhrātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ śatrughnam anudarśayan  RamS 
ṛṣiṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ saṃdiśya mātḥn me śīghram ānaya 
iti tvaritam agre sa jagāma guruvatsalaḥ  RamS 
sumantras tv api śatrughnam adūrād anvapadyata 
rāmadarśanajas tarṣo bharatasyeva tasya ca  RamS 
gacchann evātha bharatas tāpasālayasaṃsthitām 
bhrātuḥ parṇakuṭīṃ śrīmān uṭajaṃ ca dadarśa ha  RamS 
śālāyās tv agratas tasyā dadarśa bharatas tadā 
kāṣṭhāni cāvabhagnāni puṣpāṇy avacitāni ca  RamS 
dadarśa ca vane tasmin mahataḥ saṃcayān kṛtān 
mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca karīṣaiḥ śītakāraṇāt  RamS 
gacchan eva mahābāhur dyutimān bharatas tadā 
śatrughnaṃ cābravīd dhṛṣṭas tān amātyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ  RamS 
manye prāptāḥ sma taṃ deśaṃ bharadvājo yam abravīt 
nātidūre hi manye 'haṃ nadīṃ mandākinīm itaḥ  RamS 
uccair baddhāni cīrāṇi lakṣmaṇena bhaved ayam 
abhijñānakṛtaḥ panthā vikāle gantum icchatā  RamS 
idaṃ codāttadantānāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvinām 
śailapārśve parikrāntam anyonyam abhigarjatām  RamS 
yam evādhātum icchanti tāpasāḥ satataṃ vane 
tasyāsau dṛśyate dhūmaḥ saṃkulaḥ kṛṣṇavartmanaḥ  RamS 
atrāhaṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ gurusatkārakāriṇam 
āryaṃ drakṣyāmi saṃhṛṣṭo maharṣim iva rāghavam  RamS 
atha gatvā muhūrtaṃ tu citrakūṭaṃ sa rāghavaḥ 
mandākinīm anuprāptas taṃ janaṃ cedam abravīt  RamS 
jagatyāṃ puruṣavyāghra āste vīrāsane rataḥ 
janendro nirjanaṃ prāpya dhin me janma sajīvitam  RamS 
matkṛte vyasanaṃ prāpto lokanātho mahādyutiḥ 
sarvān kāmān parityajya vane vasati rāghavaḥ  RamS 
iti lokasamākruṣṭaḥ pādeṣv adya prasādayan 
rāmasya nipatiṣyāmi sītāyāś ca punaḥ punaḥ  RamS 
evaṃ sa vilapaṃs tasmin vane daśarathātmajaḥ 
dadarśa mahatīṃ puṇyāṃ parṇaśālāṃ manoramām  RamS 
sālatālāśvakarṇānāṃ parṇair bahubhir āvṛtām 
viśālāṃ mṛdubhis tīrṇāṃ kuśair vedim ivādhvare  RamS 
śakrāyudhanikāśaiś ca kārmukair bhārasādhanaiḥ 
rukmapṛṣṭhair mahāsāraiḥ śobhitāṃ śatrubādhakaiḥ  RamS 
arkaraśmipratīkāśair ghorais tūṇīgataiḥ śaraiḥ 
śobhitāṃ dīptavadanaiḥ sarpair bhogavatīm iva  RamS 
mahārajatavāsobhyām asibhyāṃ ca virājitām 
rukmabinduvicitrābhyāṃ carmabhyāṃ cāpi śobhitām  RamS 
godhāṅgulitrair āsaktaiś citraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣitaiḥ 
arisaṃghair anādhṛṣyāṃ mṛgaiḥ siṃhaguhām iva  RamS 
prāgudaksravaṇāṃ vediṃ viśālāṃ dīptapāvakām 
dadarśa bharatas tatra puṇyāṃ rāmaniveśane  RamS 
nirīkṣya sa muhūrtaṃ tu dadarśa bharato gurum 
uṭaje rāmam āsīnaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍaladhāriṇam  RamS 
taṃ tu kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ cīravalkalavāsasam 
dadarśa rāmam āsīnam abhitaḥ pāvakopamam  RamS 
siṃhaskandhaṃ mahābāhuṃ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇam 
pṛthivyāḥ sagarāntāyā bhartāraṃ dharmacāriṇam  RamS 
upaviṣṭaṃ mahābāhuṃ brahmāṇam iva śāśvatam 
sthaṇḍile darbhasaṃstīrṇe sītayā lakṣmaṇena ca  RamS 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bharataḥ śrīmān duḥkhamohapariplutaḥ 
abhyadhāvata dharmātmā bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ  RamS 
dṛṣṭvā ca vilalāpārto bāṣpasaṃdigdhayā girā 
aśaknuvan dhārayituṃ dhairyād vacanam abravīt  RamS 
yaḥ saṃsadi prakṛtibhir bhaved yukta upāsitum 
vanyair mṛgair upāsīnaḥ so 'yam āste mamāgrajaḥ  RamS 
vāsobhir bahusāhasrair yo mahātmā purocitaḥ 
mṛgājine so 'yam iha pravaste dharmam ācaran  RamS 
adhārayad yo vividhāś citrāḥ sumanasas tadā 
so 'yaṃ jaṭābhāram imaṃ sahate rāghavaḥ katham  RamS 
yasya yajñair yathādiṣṭair yukto dharmasya saṃcayaḥ 
śarīrakleśasambhūtaṃ sa dharmaṃ parimārgate  RamS 
candanena mahārheṇa yasyāṅgam upasevitam 
malena tasyāṅgam idaṃ katham āryasya sevyate  RamS 
mannimittam idaṃ duḥkhaṃ prāpto rāmaḥ sukhocitaḥ 
dhig jīvitaṃ nṛśaṃsasya mama lokavigarhitam  RamS 
ity evaṃ vilapan dīnaḥ prasvinnamukhapaṅkajaḥ 
pādāv aprāpya rāmasya papāta bharato rudan  RamS 
duḥkhābhitapto bharato rājaputro mahābalaḥ 
uktvāryeti sakṛd dīnaṃ punar novāca kiṃcana  RamS 
bāṣpāpihitakaṇṭhaś ca prekṣya rāmaṃ yaśasvinam 
āryety evābhisaṃkruśya vyāhartuṃ nāśakat tataḥ  RamS 
śatrughnaś cāpi rāmasya vavande caraṇau rudan 
tāv ubhau sa samāliṅgya rāmo 'py aśrūṇy avartayat  RamS 
tataḥ sumantreṇa guhena caiva samīyatū rājasutāv araṇye 
divākaraś caiva niśākaraś ca yathāmbare śukrabṛhaspatibhyām  RamS 
tān pārthivān vāraṇayūthapābhān samāgatāṃs tatra mahaty araṇye 
vanaukasas te 'pi samīkṣya sarve 'py aśrūṇy amuñcan pravihāya harṣam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
āghrāya rāmas taṃ mūrdhni pariṣvajya ca rāghavaḥ 
aṅke bharatam āropya paryapṛcchat samāhitaḥ  RamS 
kva nu te 'bhūt pitā tāta yad araṇyaṃ tvam āgataḥ 
na hi tvaṃ jīvatas tasya vanam āgantum arhasi  RamS 
cirasya bata paśyāmi dūrād bharatam āgatam 
duṣpratīkam araṇye 'smin kiṃ tāta vanam āgataḥ  RamS 
kaccid daśaratho rājā kuśalī satyasaṃgaraḥ 
rājasūyāśvamedhānām āhartā dharmaniścayaḥ  RamS 
sa kaccid brāhmaṇo vidvān dharmanityo mahādyutiḥ 
ikṣvākūṇām upādhyāyo yathāvat tāta pūjyate  RamS 
tāta kaccic ca kausalyā sumitrā ca prajāvatī 
sukhinī kaccid āryā ca devī nandati kaikayī  RamS 
kaccid vinayasampannaḥ kulaputro bahuśrutaḥ 
anasūyur anudraṣṭā satkṛtas te purohitaḥ  RamS 
kaccid agniṣu te yukto vidhijño matimān ṛjuḥ 
hutaṃ ca hoṣyamāṇaṃ ca kāle vedayate sadā  RamS 
iṣvastravarasampannam arthaśāstraviśāradam 
sudhanvānam upādhyāyaṃ kaccit tvaṃ tāta manyase  RamS 
kaccid ātmasamāḥ śūrāḥ śrutavanto jitendriyāḥ 
kulīnāś ceṅgitajñāś ca kṛtās te tāta mantriṇaḥ  RamS 
mantro vijayamūlaṃ hi rājñāṃ bhavati rāghava 
susaṃvṛto mantradharair amātyaiḥ śāstrakovidaiḥ  RamS 
kaccin nidrāvaśaṃ naiṣi kaccit kāle vibudhyase 
kaccic cāpararātriṣu cintayasy arthanaipuṇam  RamS 
kaccin mantrayase naikaḥ kaccin na bahubhiḥ saha 
kaccit te mantrito mantro rāṣṭraṃ na paridhāvati  RamS 
kaccid arthaṃ viniścitya laghumūlaṃ mahodayam 
kṣipram ārabhase kartuṃ na dīrghayasi rāghava  RamS 
kaccit tu sukṛtāny eva kṛtarūpāṇi vā punaḥ 
vidus te sarvakāryāṇi na kartavyāni pārthivāḥ  RamS 
kaccin na tarkair yuktvā vā ye cāpy aparikīrtitāḥ 
tvayā vā tava vāmātyair budhyate tāta mantritam  RamS 
kaccit sahasrān mūrkhāṇām ekam icchasi paṇḍitam 
paṇḍito hy arthakṛcchreṣu kuryān niḥśreyasaṃ mahat  RamS 
sahasrāṇy api mūrkhāṇāṃ yady upāste mahīpatiḥ 
atha vāpy ayutāny eva nāsti teṣu sahāyatā  RamS 
eko 'py amātyo medhāvī śūro dakṣo vicakṣaṇaḥ 
rājānaṃ rājamātraṃ vā prāpayen mahatīṃ śriyam  RamS 
kaccin mukhyā mahatsv eva madhyameṣu ca madhyamāḥ 
jaghanyāś ca jaghanyeṣu bhṛtyāḥ karmasu yojitāḥ  RamS 
amātyān upadhātītān pitṛpaitāmahāñ śucīn 
śreṣṭhāñ śreṣṭheṣu kaccit tvaṃ niyojayasi karmasu  RamS 
kaccit tvāṃ nāvajānanti yājakāḥ patitaṃ yathā 
ugrapratigrahītāraṃ kāmayānam iva striyaḥ  RamS 
upāyakuśalaṃ vaidyaṃ bhṛtyasaṃdūṣaṇe ratam 
śūram aiśvaryakāmaṃ ca yo na hanti sa vadhyate  RamS 
kaccid dhṛṣṭaś ca śūraś ca dhṛtimān matimāñ śuciḥ 
kulīnaś cānuraktaś ca dakṣaḥ senāpatiḥ kṛtaḥ  RamS 
balavantaś ca kaccit te mukhyā yuddhaviśāradāḥ 
dṛṣṭāpadānā vikrāntās tvayā satkṛtya mānitāḥ  RamS 
kaccid balasya bhaktaṃ ca vetanaṃ ca yathocitam 
samprāptakālaṃ dātavyaṃ dadāsi na vilambase  RamS 
kālātikramaṇe hy eva bhaktavetanayor bhṛtāḥ 
bhartuḥ kupyanti duṣyanti so 'narthaḥ sumahān smṛtaḥ  RamS 
kaccit sarve 'nuraktās tvāṃ kulaputrāḥ pradhānataḥ 
kaccit prāṇāṃs tavārtheṣu saṃtyajanti samāhitāḥ  RamS 
kaccij jānapado vidvān dakṣiṇaḥ pratibhānavān 
yathoktavādī dūtas te kṛto bharata paṇḍitaḥ  RamS 
kaccid aṣṭādaśāny eṣu svapakṣe daśa pañca ca 
tribhis tribhir avijñātair vetsi tīrthāni cārakaiḥ  RamS 
kaccid vyapāstān ahitān pratiyātāṃś ca sarvadā 
durbalān anavajñāya vartase ripusūdana  RamS 
kaccin na lokāyatikān brāhmaṇāṃs tāta sevase 
anarthakuśalā hy ete bālāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ  RamS 
dharmaśāstreṣu mukhyeṣu vidyamāneṣu durbudhāḥ 
buddhimān vīkṣikīṃ prāpya nirarthaṃ pravadanti te  RamS 
vīrair adhyuṣitāṃ pūrvam asmākaṃ tāta pūrvakaiḥ 
satyanāmāṃ dṛḍhadvārāṃ hastyaśvarathasaṃkulām  RamS 
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ svakarmanirataiḥ sadā 
jitendriyair mahotsāhair vṛtām āryaiḥ sahasraśaḥ  RamS 
prāsādair vividhākārair vṛtāṃ vaidyajanākulām 
kaccit samuditāṃ sphītām ayodhyāṃ parirakṣasi  RamS 
kaccic caityaśatair juṣṭaḥ suniviṣṭajanākulaḥ 
devasthānaiḥ prapābhiś ca taḍāgaiś copaśobhitaḥ  RamS 
prahṛṣṭanaranārīkaḥ samājotsavaśobhitaḥ 
sukṛṣṭasīmā paśumān hiṃsābhir parivarjitaḥ  RamS 
adevamātṛko ramyaḥ śvāpadaiḥ parivarjitaḥ 
kaccij janapadaḥ sphītaḥ sukhaṃ vasati rāghava  RamS 
kaccit te dayitāḥ sarve kṛṣigorakṣajīvinaḥ 
vārttāyāṃ saṃśritas tāta loko hi sukham edhate  RamS 
teṣāṃ guptiparīhāraiḥ kaccit te bharaṇaṃ kṛtam 
rakṣyā hi rājñā dharmeṇa sarve viṣayavāsinaḥ  RamS 
kaccit striyaḥ sāntvayasi kaccit tāś ca surakṣitāḥ 
kaccin na śraddadhāsyāsāṃ kaccid guhyaṃ na bhāṣase  RamS 
kaccin nāgavanaṃ guptaṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca tṛpyasi 
kaccid darśayase nityaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ vibhūṣitam 
utthāyotthāya pūrvāhṇe rājaputro mahāpathe  RamS 
kaccit sarvāṇi durgāṇi dhanadhānyāyudhodakaiḥ 
yantraiś ca paripūrṇāni tathā śilpidhanurdharaiḥ  RamS 
āyas te vipulaḥ kaccit kaccid alpataro vyayaḥ 
apātreṣu na te kaccit kośo gacchati rāghava  RamS 
devatārthe ca pitrarthe brāhmaṇābhyāgateṣu ca 
yodheṣu mitravargeṣu kaccid gacchati te vyayaḥ  RamS 
kaccid āryo viśuddhātmākṣāritaś corakarmaṇā 
apṛṣṭaḥ śāstrakuśalair na lobhād badhyate śuciḥ  RamS 
gṛhītaś caiva pṛṣṭaś ca kāle dṛṣṭaḥ sakāraṇaḥ 
kaccin na mucyate coro dhanalobhān nararṣabha  RamS 
vyasane kaccid āḍhyasya durgatasya ca rāghava 
arthaṃ virāgāḥ paśyanti tavāmātyā bahuśrutāḥ  RamS 
yāni mithyābhiśastānāṃ patanty asrāṇi rāghava 
tāni putrapaśūn ghnanti prītyartham anuśāsataḥ  RamS 
kaccid vṛddhāṃś ca bālāṃś ca vaidyamukhyāṃś ca rāghava 
dānena manasā vācā tribhir etair bubhūṣase  RamS 
kaccid gurūṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca tāpasān devatātithīn 
caityāṃś ca sarvān siddhārthān brāhmaṇāṃś ca namasyasi  RamS 
kaccid arthena vā dharmaṃ dharmaṃ dharmeṇa vā punaḥ 
ubhau vā prītilobhena kāmena na vibādhase  RamS 
kaccid arthaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca jayatāṃ vara 
vibhajya kāle kālajña sarvān bharata sevase  RamS 
kaccit te brāhmaṇāḥ śarma sarvaśāstrārthakovidāḥ 
āśaṃsante mahāprājña paurajānapadaiḥ saha  RamS 
nāstikyam anṛtaṃ krodhaṃ pramādaṃ dīrghasūtratām 
adarśanaṃ jñānavatām ālasyaṃ pañcavṛttitām  RamS 
ekacintanam arthānām anarthajñaiś ca mantraṇam 
niścitānām anārambhaṃ mantrasyāparirakṣaṇam  RamS 
maṅgalasyāprayogaṃ ca pratyutthānaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ 
kaccit tvaṃ varjayasy etān rājadoṣāṃś caturdaśa  RamS 
kaccit svādukṛtaṃ bhojyam eko nāśnāsi rāghava 
kaccid āśaṃsamānebhyo mitrebhyaḥ samprayacchasi  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
rāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā bharataḥ pratyuvāca ha 
kiṃ me dharmād vihīnasya rājadharmaḥ kariṣyati  RamS 
śāśvato 'yaṃ sadā dharmaḥ sthito 'smāsu nararṣabha 
jyeṣṭhaputre sthite rājan na kanīyān bhaven nṛpaḥ  RamS 
sa samṛddhāṃ mayā sārdham ayodhyāṃ gaccha rāghava 
abhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ kulasyāsya bhavāya naḥ  RamS 
rājānaṃ mānuṣaṃ prāhur devatve saṃmato mama 
yasya dharmārthasahitaṃ vṛttam āhur amānuṣam  RamS 
kekayasthe ca mayi tu tvayi cāraṇyam āśrite 
divam ārya gato rājā yāyajūkaḥ satāṃ mataḥ  RamS 
uttiṣṭha puruṣavyāghra kriyatām udakaṃ pituḥ 
ahaṃ cāyaṃ ca śatrughnaḥ pūrvam eva kṛtodakau  RamS 
priyeṇa kila dattaṃ hi pitṛlokeṣu rāghava 
akṣayyaṃ bhavatīty āhur bhavāṃś caiva pituḥ priyaḥ  RamS 
tāṃ śrutvā karuṇāṃ vācaṃ pitur maraṇasaṃhitām 
rāghavo bharatenoktāṃ babhūva gatacetanaḥ  RamS 
vāgvajraṃ bharatenoktam amanojñaṃ paraṃtapaḥ 
pragṛhya bāhū rāmo vai puṣpitāgro yathā drumaḥ 
vane paraśunā kṛttas tathā bhuvi papāta ha  RamS 
tathā hi patitaṃ rāmaṃ jagatyāṃ jagatīpatim 
kūlaghātapariśrāntaṃ prasuptam iva kuñjaram  RamS 
bhrātaras te maheṣvāsaṃ sarvataḥ śokakarśitam 
rudantaḥ saha vaidehyā siṣicuḥ salilena vai  RamS 
sa tu saṃjñāṃ punar labdhvā netrābhyām āsram utsṛjan 
upākrāmata kākutsthaḥ kṛpaṇaṃ bahubhāṣitum  RamS 
kiṃ nu tasya mayā kāryaṃ durjātena mahātmanaḥ 
yo mṛto mama śokena na mayā cāpi saṃskṛtaḥ  RamS 
aho bharata siddhārtho yena rājā tvayānagha 
śatrugheṇa ca sarveṣu pretakṛtyeṣu satkṛtaḥ  RamS 
niṣpradhānām anekāgrāṃ narendreṇa vinākṛtām 
nivṛttavanavāso 'pi nāyodhyāṃ gantum utsahe  RamS 
samāptavanavāsaṃ mām ayodhyāyāṃ paraṃtapa 
ko nu śāsiṣyati punas tāte lokāntaraṃ gate  RamS 
purā prekṣya suvṛttaṃ māṃ pitā yāny āha sāntvayan 
vākyāni tāni śroṣyāmi kutaḥ karṇasukhāny aham  RamS 
evam uktvā sa bharataṃ bhāryām abhyetya rāghavaḥ 
uvāca śokasaṃtaptaḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanām  RamS 
sīte mṛtas te śvaśuraḥ pitrā hīno 'si lakṣmaṇa 
bharato duḥkham ācaṣṭe svargataṃ pṛthivīpatim  RamS 
sāntvayitvā tu tāṃ rāmo rudantīṃ janakātmajām 
uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ tatra duḥkhito duḥkhitaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
ānayeṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ cīram āhara cottaram 
jalakriyārthaṃ tātasya gamiṣyāmi mahātmanaḥ  RamS 
sītā purastād vrajatu tvam enām abhito vraja 
ahaṃ paścād gamiṣyāmi gatir hy eṣā sudāruṇā  RamS 
tato nityānugas teṣāṃ viditātmā mahāmatiḥ 
mṛdur dāntaś ca śāntaś ca rāme ca dṛḍhabhaktimān  RamS 
sumantras tair nṛpasutaiḥ sārdham āśvāsya rāghavam 
avātārayad ālambya nadīṃ mandākinīṃ śivām  RamS 
te sutīrthāṃ tataḥ kṛcchrād upāgamya yaśasvinaḥ 
nadīṃ mandākinīṃ ramyāṃ sadā puṣpitakānanām  RamS 
śīghrasrotasam āsādya tīrthaṃ śivam akardamam 
siṣicus tūdakaṃ rājñe tata etad bhavatv iti  RamS 
pragṛhya ca mahīpālo jalapūritam añjalim 
diśaṃ yāmyām abhimukho rudan vacanam abravīt  RamS 
etat te rājaśārdūla vimalaṃ toyam akṣayam 
pitṛlokagatasyādya maddattam upatiṣṭhatu  RamS 
tato mandākinītīrāt pratyuttīrya sa rāghavaḥ 
pituś cakāra tejasvī nivāpaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha  RamS 
aiṅgudaṃ badarīmiśraṃ piṇyākaṃ darbhasaṃstare 
nyasya rāmaḥ suduḥkhārto rudan vacanam abravīt  RamS 
idaṃ bhuṅkṣva mahārāja prīto yadaśanā vayam 
yadannaḥ puruṣo bhavati tadannās tasya devatāḥ  RamS 
tatas tenaiva mārgeṇa pratyuttīrya nadītaṭāt 
āruroha naravyāghro ramyasānuṃ mahīdharam  RamS 
tataḥ parṇakuṭīdvāram āsādya jagatīpatiḥ 
parijagrāha pāṇibhyām ubhau bharatalakṣmaṇau  RamS 
teṣāṃ tu rudatāṃ śabdāt pratiśrutkābhavad girau 
bhrātḥṇāṃ saha vaidehyā siṃhānāṃ nardatām iva  RamS 
vijñāya tumulaṃ śabdaṃ trastā bharatasainikāḥ 
abruvaṃś cāpi rāmeṇa bharataḥ saṃgato dhruvam 
teṣām eva mahāñ śabdaḥ śocatāṃ pitaraṃ mṛtam  RamS 
atha vāsān parityajya taṃ sarve 'bhimukhāḥ svanam 
apy ekamanaso jagmur yathāsthānaṃ pradhāvitāḥ  RamS 
hayair anye gajair anye rathair anye svalaṃkṛtaiḥ 
sukumārās tathaivānye padbhir eva narā yayuḥ  RamS 
aciraproṣitaṃ rāmaṃ ciraviproṣitaṃ yathā 
draṣṭukāmo janaḥ sarvo jagāma sahasāśramam  RamS 
bhrātḥṇāṃ tvaritās te tu draṣṭukāmāḥ samāgamam 
yayur bahuvidhair yānaiḥ khuranemisamākulaiḥ  RamS 
sā bhūmir bahubhir yānaiḥ khuranemisamāhatā 
mumoca tumulaṃ śabdaṃ dyaur ivābhrasamāgame  RamS 
tena vitrāsitā nāgāḥ kareṇuparivāritāḥ 
āvāsayanto gandhena jagmur anyad vanaṃ tataḥ  RamS 
varāhamṛgasiṃhāś ca mahiṣāḥ sarkṣavānarāḥ 
vyāghragokarṇagavayā vitreṣuḥ pṛṣataiḥ saha  RamS 
rathāṅgasāhvā natyūhā haṃsāḥ kāraṇḍavāḥ plavāḥ 
tathā puṃskokilāḥ krauñcā visaṃjñā bhejire diśaḥ  RamS 
tena śabdena vitrastair ākāśaṃ pakṣibhir vṛtam 
manuṣyair āvṛtā bhūmir ubhayaṃ prababhau tadā  RamS 
tān narān bāṣpapūrṇākṣān samīkṣyātha suduḥkhitān 
paryaṣvajata dharmajñaḥ pitṛvan mātṛvac ca saḥ  RamS 
sa tatra kāṃścit pariṣasvaje narān narāś ca kecit tu tam abhyavādayan 
cakāra sarvān savayasyabāndhavān yathārham āsādya tadā nṛpātmajaḥ  RamS 
tataḥ sa teṣāṃ rudatāṃ mahātmanāṃ bhuvaṃ ca khaṃ cānuvinādayan svanaḥ 
guhā girīṇāṃ ca diśaś ca saṃtataṃ mṛdaṅgaghoṣapratimo viśuśruve  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
vasiṣṭhaḥ purataḥ kṛtvā dārān daśarathasya ca 
abhicakrāma taṃ deśaṃ rāmadarśanatarṣitaḥ  RamS 
rājapatnyaś ca gacchantyo mandaṃ mandākinīṃ prati 
dadṛśus tatra tat tīrthaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇasevitam  RamS 
kausalyā bāṣpapūrṇena mukhena pariśuṣyatā 
sumitrām abravīd dīnā yāś cānyā rājayoṣitaḥ  RamS 
idaṃ teṣām anāthānāṃ kliṣṭam akliṣṭakarmaṇām 
vane prāk kevalaṃ tīrthaṃ ye te nirviṣayīkṛtāḥ  RamS 
itaḥ sumitre putras te sadā jalam atandritaḥ 
svayaṃ harati saumitrir mama putrasya kāraṇāt  RamS 
dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu sā dadarśa mahītale 
pitur iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ nyastam āyatalocanā  RamS 
taṃ bhūmau pitur ārtena nyastaṃ rāmeṇa vīkṣya sā 
uvāca devī kausalyā sarvā daśarathastriyaḥ  RamS 
idam ikṣvākunāthasya rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ 
rāghaveṇa pitur dattaṃ paśyataitad yathāvidhi  RamS 
tasya devasamānasya pārthivasya mahātmanaḥ 
naitad aupayikaṃ manye bhuktabhogasya bhojanam  RamS 
caturantāṃ mahīṃ bhuktvā mahendrasadṛśo vibhuḥ 
katham iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ sa bhuṅkte vasudhādhipaḥ  RamS 
ato duḥkhataraṃ loke na kiṃcit pratibhāti mā 
yatra rāmaḥ pitur dadyād iṅgudīkṣodam ṛddhimān  RamS 
rāmeṇeṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ pitur dattaṃ samīkṣya me 
kathaṃ duḥkhena hṛdayaṃ na sphoṭati sahasradhā  RamS 
evam ārtāṃ sapatnyas tā jagmur āśvāsya tāṃ tadā 
dadṛśuś cāśrame rāmaṃ svargāc cyutam ivāmaram  RamS 
sarvabhogaiḥ parityaktaṃ rāmaṃ samprekṣya mātaraḥ 
ārtā mumucur aśrūṇi sasvaraṃ śokakarśitāḥ  RamS 
tāsāṃ rāmaḥ samutthāya jagrāha caraṇāñ śubhān 
mātḥṇāṃ manujavyāghraḥ sarvāsāṃ satyasaṃgaraḥ  RamS 
tāḥ pāṇibhiḥ sukhasparśair mṛdvaṅgulitalaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
pramamārjū rajaḥ pṛṣṭhād rāmasyāyatalocanāḥ  RamS 
saumitrir api tāḥ sarvā mātḥn samprekṣya duḥkhitaḥ 
abhyavādayatāsaktaṃ śanai rāmād anantaram  RamS 
yathā rāme tathā tasmin sarvā vavṛtire striyaḥ 
vṛttiṃ daśarathāj jāte lakṣmaṇe śubhalakṣaṇe  RamS 
sītāpi caraṇāṃs tāsām upasaṃgṛhya duḥkhitā 
śvaśrūṇām aśrupūrṇākṣī sā babhūvāgrataḥ sthitā  RamS 
tāṃ pariṣvajya duḥkhārtāṃ mātā duhitaraṃ yathā 
vanavāsakṛśāṃ dīnāṃ kausalyā vākyam abravīt  RamS 
videharājasya sutā snuṣā daśarathasya ca 
rāmapatnī kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ samprāptā nirjane vane  RamS 
padmam ātapasaṃtaptaṃ parikliṣṭam ivotpalam 
kāñcanaṃ rajasā dhvastaṃ kliṣṭaṃ candram ivāmbudaiḥ  RamS 
mukhaṃ te prekṣya māṃ śoko dahaty agnir ivāśrayam 
bhṛśaṃ manasi vaidehi vyasanāraṇisambhavaḥ  RamS 
bruvantyām evam ārtāyāṃ jananyāṃ bharatāgrajaḥ 
pādāv āsādya jagrāha vasiṣṭhasya sa rāghavaḥ  RamS 
purohitasyāgnisamasya tasya vai bṛhaspater indra ivāmarādhipaḥ 
pragṛhya pādau susamṛddhatejasaḥ sahaiva tenopaviveśa rāghavaḥ  RamS 
tato jaghanyaṃ sahitaiḥ sa mantribhiḥ purapradhānaiś ca sahaiva sainikaiḥ 
janena dharmajñatamena dharmavān upopaviṣṭo bharatas tadāgrajam  RamS 
upopaviṣṭas tu tadā sa vīryavāṃs tapasviveṣeṇa samīkṣya rāghavam 
śriyā jvalantaṃ bharataḥ kṛtāñjalir yathā mahendraḥ prayataḥ prajāpatim  RamS 
kim eṣa vākyaṃ bharato 'dya rāghavaṃ praṇamya satkṛtya ca sādhu vakṣyati 
itīva tasyāryajanasya tattvato babhūva kautūhalam uttamaṃ tadā  RamS 
sa rāghavaḥ satyadhṛtiś ca lakṣmaṇo mahānubhāvo bharataś ca dhārmikaḥ 
vṛtāḥ suhṛdbhiś ca virejur adhvare yathā sadasyaiḥ sahitās trayo 'gnayaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
taṃ tu rāmaḥ samāśvāsya bhrātaraṃ guruvatsalam 
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame  RamS 
kim etad iccheyam ahaṃ śrotuṃ pravyāhṛtaṃ tvayā 
yasmāt tvam āgato deśam imaṃ cīrajaṭājinī  RamS 
yannimittam imaṃ deśaṃ kṛṣṇājinajaṭādharaḥ 
hitvā rājyaṃ praviṣṭas tvaṃ tat sarvaṃ vaktum arhasi  RamS 
ity uktaḥ kekayīputraḥ kākutsthena mahātmanā 
pragṛhya balavad bhūyaḥ prāñjalir vākyam abravīt  RamS 
āryaṃ tātaḥ parityajya kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram 
gataḥ svargaṃ mahābāhuḥ putraśokābhipīḍitaḥ  RamS 
striyā niyuktaḥ kaikeyyā mama mātrā paraṃtapa 
cakāra sumahat pāpam idam ātmayaśoharam  RamS 
sā rājyaphalam aprāpya vidhavā śokakarśitā 
patiṣyati mahāghore niraye jananī mama  RamS 
tasya me dāsabhūtasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi 
abhiṣiñcasva cādyaiva rājyena maghavān iva  RamS 
imāḥ prakṛtayaḥ sarvā vidhavā mātaraś ca yāḥ 
tvatsakāśam anuprāptāḥ prasādaṃ kartum arhasi  RamS 
tadānupūrvyā yuktaṃ ca yuktaṃ cātmani mānada 
rājyaṃ prāpnuhi dharmeṇa sakāmān suhṛdaḥ kuru  RamS 
bhavatv avidhavā bhūmiḥ samagrā patinā tvayā 
śaśinā vimaleneva śāradī rajanī yathā  RamS 
ebhiś ca sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ śirasā yācito mayā 
bhrātuḥ śiṣyasya dāsasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi  RamS 
tad idaṃ śāśvataṃ pitryaṃ sarvaṃ sacivamaṇḍalam 
pūjitaṃ puruṣavyāghra nātikramitum utsahe  RamS 
evam uktvā mahābāhuḥ sabāṣpaḥ kekayīsutaḥ 
rāmasya śirasā pādau jagrāha bharataḥ punaḥ  RamS 
taṃ mattam iva mātaṃgaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥ 
bhrātaraṃ bharataṃ rāmaḥ pariṣvajyedam abravīt  RamS 
kulīnaḥ sattvasampannas tejasvī caritavrataḥ 
rājyahetoḥ kathaṃ pāpam ācaret tvadvidho janaḥ  RamS 
na doṣaṃ tvayi paśyāmi sūkṣmam apy arisūdana 
na cāpi jananīṃ bālyāt tvaṃ vigarhitum arhasi  RamS 
yāvat pitari dharmajña gauravaṃ lokasatkṛte 
tāvad dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha jananyām api gauravam  RamS 
etābhyāṃ dharmaśīlābhyāṃ vanaṃ gaccheti rāghava 
mātāpitṛbhyām ukto 'haṃ katham anyat samācare  RamS 
tvayā rājyam ayodhyāyāṃ prāptavyaṃ lokasatkṛtam 
vastavyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇye mayā valkalavāsasā  RamS 
evaṃ kṛtvā mahārājo vibhāgaṃ lokasaṃnidhau 
vyādiśya ca mahātejā divaṃ daśaratho gataḥ  RamS 
sa ca pramāṇaṃ dharmātmā rājā lokagurus tava 
pitrā dattaṃ yathābhāgam upabhoktuṃ tvam arhasi  RamS 
caturdaśa samāḥ saumya daṇḍakāraṇyam āśritaḥ 
upabhokṣye tv ahaṃ dattaṃ bhāgaṃ pitrā mahātmanā  RamS 
yad abravīn māṃ naralokasatkṛtaḥ pitā mahātmā vibudhādhipopamaḥ 
tad eva manye paramātmano hitaṃ na sarvalokeśvarabhāvam avyayam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tataḥ puruṣasiṃhānāṃ vṛtānāṃ taiḥ suhṛdgaṇaiḥ 
śocatām eva rajanī duḥkhena vyatyavartata  RamS 
rajanyāṃ suprabhātāyāṃ bhrātaras te suhṛdvṛtāḥ 
mandākinyāṃ hutaṃ japyaṃ kṛtvā rāmam upāgaman  RamS 
tūṣṇīṃ te samupāsīnā na kaścit kiṃcid abravīt 
bharatas tu suhṛnmadhye rāmaṃ vacanam abravīt  RamS 
sāntvitā māmikā mātā dattaṃ rājyam idaṃ mama 
tad dadāmi tavaivāhaṃ bhuṅkṣva rājyam akaṇṭakam  RamS 
mahatevāmbuvegena bhinnaḥ setur jalāgame 
durāvāraṃ tvadanyena rājyakhaṇḍam idaṃ mahat  RamS 
gatiṃ khara ivāśvasya tārkṣyasyeva patatriṇaḥ 
anugantuṃ na śaktir me gatiṃ tava mahīpate  RamS 
sujīvaṃ nityaśas tasya yaḥ parair upajīvyate 
rāma tena tu durjīvaṃ yaḥ parān upajīvati  RamS 
yathā tu ropito vṛkṣaḥ puruṣeṇa vivardhitaḥ 
hrasvakena durāroho rūḍhaskandho mahādrumaḥ  RamS 
sa yadā puṣpito bhūtvā phalāni na vidarśayet 
sa tāṃ nānubhavet prītiṃ yasya hetoḥ prabhāvitaḥ  RamS 
eṣopamā mahābāho tvam arthaṃ vettum arhasi 
yadi tvam asmān ṛṣabho bhartā bhṛtyān na śādhi hi  RamS 
śreṇayas tvāṃ mahārāja paśyantv agryāś ca sarvaśaḥ 
pratapantam ivādityaṃ rājye sthitam ariṃdamam  RamS 
tavānuyāne kākutstha mattā nardantu kuñjarāḥ 
antaḥpuragatā nāryo nandantu susamāhitāḥ  RamS 
tasya sādhv ity amanyanta nāgarā vividhā janāḥ 
bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaṃ pratyanuyācataḥ  RamS 
tam evaṃ duḥkhitaṃ prekṣya vilapantaṃ yaśasvinam 
rāmaḥ kṛtātmā bharataṃ samāśvāsayad ātmavān  RamS 
nātmanaḥ kāmakāro 'sti puruṣo 'yam anīśvaraḥ 
itaś cetarataś cainaṃ kṛtāntaḥ parikarṣati  RamS 
sarve kṣayāntā nicayāḥ patanāntāḥ samucchrayāḥ 
saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ ca jīvitam  RamS 
yathā phalānāṃ pakvānāṃ nānyatra patanād bhayam 
evaṃ narasya jātasya nānyatra maraṇād bhayam  RamS 
yathāgāraṃ dṛḍhasthūṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ bhūtvāvasīdati 
tathāvasīdanti narā jarāmṛtyuvaśaṃ gatāḥ  RamS 
ahorātrāṇi gacchanti sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām iha 
āyūṃṣi kṣapayanty āśu grīṣme jalam ivāṃśavaḥ  RamS 
ātmānam anuśoca tvaṃ kim anyam anuśocasi 
āyus te hīyate yasya sthitasya ca gatasya ca  RamS 
sahaiva mṛtyur vrajati saha mṛtyur niṣīdati 
gatvā sudīrgham adhvānaṃ saha mṛtyur nivartate  RamS 
gātreṣu valayaḥ prāptāḥ śvetāś caiva śiroruhāḥ 
jarayā puruṣo jīrṇaḥ kiṃ hi kṛtvā prabhāvayet  RamS 
nandanty udita āditye nandanty astam ite ravau 
ātmano nāvabudhyante manuṣyā jīvitakṣayam  RamS 
hṛṣyanty ṛtumukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā navaṃ navam ihāgatam 
ṛtūnāṃ parivartena prāṇināṃ prāṇasaṃkṣayaḥ  RamS 
yathā kāṣṭhaṃ ca kāṣṭhaṃ ca sameyātāṃ mahārṇave 
sametya ca vyapeyātāṃ kālam āsādya kaṃcana  RamS 
evaṃ bhāryāś ca putrāś ca jñātayaś ca vasūni ca 
sametya vyavadhāvanti dhruvo hy eṣāṃ vinābhavaḥ  RamS 
nātra kaścid yathā bhāvaṃ prāṇī samabhivartate 
tena tasmin na sāmarthyaṃ pretasyāsty anuśocataḥ  RamS 
yathā hi sārthaṃ gacchantaṃ brūyāt kaścit pathi sthitaḥ 
aham apy āgamiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhato bhavatām iti  RamS 
evaṃ pūrvair gato mārgaḥ pitṛpaitāmaho dhruvaḥ 
tam āpannaḥ kathaṃ śoced yasya nāsti vyatikramaḥ  RamS 
vayasaḥ patamānasya srotaso vānivartinaḥ 
ātmā sukhe niyoktavyaḥ sukhabhājaḥ prajāḥ smṛtāḥ  RamS 
dharmātmā sa śubhaiḥ kṛtsnaiḥ kratubhiś cāptadakṣiṇaiḥ 
dhūtapāpo gataḥ svargaṃ pitā naḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  RamS 
bhṛtyānāṃ bharaṇāt samyak prajānāṃ paripālanāt 
arthādānāc ca dhārmeṇa pitā nas tridivaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
iṣṭvā bahuvidhair yajñair bhogāṃś cāvāpya puṣkalān 
uttamaṃ cāyur āsādya svar gataḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  RamS 
sa jīrṇaṃ mānuṣaṃ dehaṃ parityajya pitā hi naḥ 
daivīm ṛddhim anuprāpto brahmalokavihāriṇīm  RamS 
taṃ tu naivaṃvidhaḥ kaścit prājñaḥ śocitum arhati 
tvadvidho yadvidhaś cāpi śrutavān buddhimattaraḥ  RamS 
ete bahuvidhāḥ śokā vilāparudite tathā 
varjanīyā hi dhīreṇa sarvāvasthāsu dhīmatā  RamS 
sa svastho bhava mā śoco yātvā cāvasa tāṃ purīm 
tathā pitrā niyukto 'si vaśinā vadatāṃ vara  RamS 
yatrāham api tenaiva niyuktaḥ puṇyakarmaṇā 
tatraivāhaṃ kariṣyāmi pitur āryasya śāsanam  RamS 
na mayā śāsanaṃ tasya tyaktuṃ nyāyyam ariṃdama 
tat tvayāpi sadā mānyaṃ sa vai bandhuḥ sa naḥ pitā  RamS 
evam uktvā tu virate rāme vacanam arthavat 
uvāca bharataś citraṃ dhārmiko dhārmikaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
ko hi syād īdṛśo loke yādṛśas tvam ariṃdama 
na tvāṃ pravyathayed duḥkhaṃ prītir vā na praharṣayet  RamS 
saṃmataś cāsi vṛddhānāṃ tāṃś ca pṛcchasi saṃśayān 
yathā mṛtas tathā jīvan yathāsati tathā sati  RamS 
yasyaiṣa buddhilābhaḥ syāt paritapyeta kena saḥ 
sa evaṃ vyasanaṃ prāpya na viṣīditum arhati  RamS 
amaropamasattvas tvaṃ mahātmā satyasaṃgaraḥ 
sarvajñaḥ sarvadarśī ca buddhimāṃś cāsi rāghava  RamS 
na tvām evaṃ guṇair yuktaṃ prabhavābhavakovidam 
aviṣahyatamaṃ duḥkham āsādayitum arhati  RamS 
proṣite mayi yat pāpaṃ mātrā matkāraṇāt kṛtam 
kṣudrayā tad aniṣṭaṃ me prasīdatu bhavān mama  RamS 
dharmabandhena baddho 'smi tenemāṃ neha mātaram 
hanmi tīvreṇa daṇḍena daṇḍārhāṃ pāpakāriṇīm  RamS 
kathaṃ daśarathāj jātaḥ śuddhābhijanakarmaṇaḥ 
jānan dharmam adharmiṣṭhaṃ kuryāṃ karma jugupsitam  RamS 
guruḥ kriyāvān vṛddhaś ca rājā pretaḥ piteti ca 
tātaṃ na parigarheyaṃ daivataṃ ceti saṃsadi  RamS 
ko hi dharmārthayor hīnam īdṛśaṃ karma kilbiṣam 
striyāḥ priyacikīrṣuḥ san kuryād dharmajña dharmavit  RamS 
antakāle hi bhūtāni muhyantīti purāśrutiḥ 
rājñaivaṃ kurvatā loke pratyakṣā sā śrutiḥ kṛtā  RamS 
sādhvartham abhisaṃdhāya krodhān mohāc ca sāhasāt 
tātasya yad atikrāntaṃ pratyāharatu tad bhavān  RamS 
pitur hi samatikrāntaṃ putro yaḥ sādhu manyate 
tad apatyaṃ mataṃ loke viparītam ato 'nyathā  RamS 
tad apatyaṃ bhavān astu mā bhavān duṣkṛtaṃ pituḥ 
abhipattā kṛtaṃ karma loke dhīravigarhitam  RamS 
kaikeyīṃ māṃ ca tātaṃ ca suhṛdo bāndhavāṃś ca naḥ 
paurajānapadān sarvāṃs trātu sarvam idaṃ bhavān  RamS 
kva cāraṇyaṃ kva ca kṣātraṃ kva jaṭāḥ kva ca pālanam 
īdṛśaṃ vyāhataṃ karma na bhavān kartum arhati  RamS 
atha kleśajam eva tvaṃ dharmaṃ caritum icchasi 
dharmeṇa caturo varṇān pālayan kleśam āpnuhi  RamS 
caturṇām āśramāṇāṃ hi gārhasthyaṃ śreṣṭham āśramam 
āhur dharmajña dharmajñās taṃ kathaṃ tyaktum arhasi  RamS 
śrutena bālaḥ sthānena janmanā bhavato hy aham 
sa kathaṃ pālayiṣyāmi bhūmiṃ bhavati tiṣṭhati  RamS 
hīnabuddhiguṇo bālo hīnaḥ sthānena cāpy aham 
bhavatā ca vinā bhūto na vartayitum utsahe  RamS 
idaṃ nikhilam avyagraṃ pitryaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakam 
anuśādhi svadharmeṇa dharmajña saha bāndhavaiḥ  RamS 
ihaiva tvābhiṣiñcantu dharmajña saha bāndhavaiḥ 
ṛtvijaḥ savasiṣṭhāś ca mantravan mantrakovidāḥ  RamS 
abhiṣiktas tvam asmābhir ayodhyāṃ pālane vraja 
vijitya tarasā lokān marudbhir iva vāsavaḥ  RamS 
ṛṇāni trīṇy apākurvan durhṛdaḥ sādhu nirdahan 
suhṛdas tarpayan kāmais tvam evātrānuśādhi mām  RamS 
adyārya muditāḥ santu suhṛdas te 'bhiṣecane 
adya bhītāḥ pālayantāṃ durhṛdas te diśo daśa  RamS 
ākrośaṃ mama mātuś ca pramṛjya puruṣarṣabha 
adya tatra bhavantaṃ ca pitaraṃ rakṣa kilbiṣāt  RamS 
śirasā tvābhiyāce 'haṃ kuruṣva karuṇāṃ mayi 
bāndhaveṣu ca sarveṣu bhūteṣv iva maheśvaraḥ  RamS 
atha vā pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā vanam eva bhavān itaḥ 
gamiṣyati gamiṣyāmi bhavatā sārdham apy aham  RamS 
tathāpi rāmo bharatena tāmyatā prasādyamānaḥ śirasā mahīpatiḥ 
na caiva cakre gamanāya sattvavān matiṃ pitus tadvacane pratiṣṭhitaḥ  RamS 
tad adbhutaṃ sthairyam avekṣya rāghave samaṃ jano harṣam avāpa duḥkhitaḥ 
na yāty ayodhyām iti duḥkhito 'bhavat sthirapratijñatvam avekṣya harṣitaḥ  RamS 
tam ṛtvijo naigamayūthavallabhās tathā visaṃjñāśrukalāś ca mātaraḥ 
tathā bruvāṇaṃ bharataṃ pratuṣṭuvuḥ praṇamya rāmaṃ ca yayācire saha  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
punar evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tu bharataṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ 
pratyuvāca tataḥ śrīmāñ jñātimadhye 'tisatkṛtaḥ  RamS 
upapannam idaṃ vākyaṃ yat tvam evam abhāṣathāḥ 
jātaḥ putro daśarathāt kaikeyyāṃ rājasattamāt  RamS 
purā bhrātaḥ pitā naḥ sa mātaraṃ te samudvahan 
mātāmahe samāśrauṣīd rājyaśulkam anuttamam  RamS 
devāsure ca saṃgrāme jananyai tava pārthivaḥ 
samprahṛṣṭo dadau rājā varam ārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ  RamS 
tataḥ sā saṃpratiśrāvya tava mātā yaśasvinī 
ayācata naraśreṣṭhaṃ dvau varau varavarṇinī  RamS 
tava rājyaṃ naravyāghra mama pravrājanaṃ tathā 
tac ca rājā tathā tasyai niyuktaḥ pradadau varam  RamS 
tena pitrāham apy atra niyuktaḥ puruṣarṣabha 
caturdaśa vane vāsaṃ varṣāṇi varadānikam  RamS 
so 'haṃ vanam idaṃ prāpto nirjanaṃ lakṣmaṇānvitaḥ 
śītayā cāpratidvandvaḥ satyavāde sthitaḥ pituḥ  RamS 
bhavān api tathety eva pitaraṃ satyavādinam 
kartum arhati rājendraṃ kṣipram evābhiṣecanāt  RamS 
ṛṇān mocaya rājānaṃ matkṛte bharata prabhum 
pitaraṃ trāhi dharmajña mātaraṃ cābhinandaya  RamS 
śrūyate hi purā tāta śrutir gītā yaśasvinī 
gayena yajamānena gayeṣv eva pitḥn prati  RamS 
puṃnāmnā narakād yasmāt pitaraṃ trāyate sutaḥ 
tasmāt putra iti proktaḥ pitḥn yat pāti vā sutaḥ  RamS 
eṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrā guṇavanto bahuśrutāḥ 
teṣāṃ vai samavetānām api kaścid gayāṃ vrajet  RamS 
evaṃ rājarṣayaḥ sarve pratītā rājanandana 
tasmāt trāhi naraśreṣṭha pitaraṃ narakāt prabho  RamS 
ayodhyāṃ gaccha bharata prakṛtīr anurañjaya 
śatrughnasahito vīra saha sarvair dvijātibhiḥ  RamS 
pravekṣye daṇḍakāraṇyam aham apy avilambayan 
ābhyāṃ tu sahito rājan vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca  RamS 
tvaṃ rājā bhava bharata svayaṃ narāṇāṃ vanyānām aham api rājarāṇ mṛgāṇām 
gaccha tvaṃ puravaram adya samprahṛṣṭaḥ saṃhṛṣṭas tv aham api daṇḍakān pravekṣye 
chāyāṃ te dinakarabhāḥ prabādhamānaṃ varṣatraṃ bharata karotu mūrdhni śītām 
eteṣām aham api kānanadrumāṇāṃ chāyāṃ tām atiśayinīṃ sukhaṃ śrayiṣye  RamS 
śatrughnaḥ kuśalamatis tu te sahāyaḥ saumitrir mama viditaḥ pradhānamitram 
catvāras tanayavarā vayaṃ narendraṃ satyasthaṃ bharata carāma mā viṣādam  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
āśvāsayantaṃ bharataṃ jābālir brāhmaṇottamaḥ 
uvāca rāmaṃ dharmajñaṃ dharmāpetam idaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
sādhu rāghava mā bhūt te buddhir evaṃ nirarthakā 
prākṛtasya narasyeva āryabuddhes tapasvinaḥ  RamS 
kaḥ kasya puruṣo bandhuḥ kim āpyaṃ kasya kenacit 
yad eko jāyate jantur eka eva vinaśyati  RamS 
tasmān mātā pitā ceti rāma sajjeta yo naraḥ 
unmatta iva sa jñeyo nāsti kāciddhi kasyacit  RamS 
yathā grāmāntaraṃ gacchan naraḥ kaścit kvacid vaset 
utsṛjya ca tam āvāsaṃ pratiṣṭhetāpare 'hani  RamS 
evam eva manuṣyāṇāṃ pitā mātā gṛhaṃ vasu 
āvāsamātraṃ kākutstha sajjante nātra sajjanāḥ  RamS 
pitryaṃ rājyaṃ samutsṛjya sa nārhati narottama 
āsthātuṃ kāpathaṃ duḥkhaṃ viṣamaṃ bahukaṇṭakam  RamS 
samṛddhāyām ayodhyāyām ātmānam abhiṣecaya 
ekaveṇīdharā hi tvāṃ nagarī sampratīkṣate  RamS 
rājabhogān anubhavan mahārhān pārthivātmaja 
vihara tvam ayodhyāyāṃ yathā śakras triviṣṭape  RamS 
na te kaścid daśaratas tvaṃ ca tasya na kaścana 
anyo rājā tvam anyaś ca tasmāt kuru yad ucyate  RamS 
gataḥ sa nṛpatis tatra gantavyaṃ yatra tena vai 
pravṛttir eṣā martyānāṃ tvaṃ tu mithyā vihanyase  RamS 
arthadharmaparā ye ye tāṃs tāñ śocāmi netarān 
te hi duḥkham iha prāpya vināśaṃ pretya bhejire  RamS 
aṣṭakāpitṛdaivatyam ity ayaṃ prasṛto janaḥ 
annasyopadravaṃ paśya mṛto hi kim aśiṣyati  RamS 
yadi bhuktam ihānyena deham anyasya gacchati 
dadyāt pravasataḥ śrāddhaṃ na tat pathy aśanaṃ bhavet  RamS 
dānasaṃvananā hy ete granthā medhāvibhiḥ kṛtāḥ 
yajasva dehi dīkṣasva tapas tapyasva saṃtyaja  RamS 
sa nāsti param ity eva kuru buddhiṃ mahāmate 
pratyakṣaṃ yat tad ātiṣṭha parokṣaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kuru  RamS 
satāṃ buddhiṃ puraskṛtya sarvalokanidarśinīm 
rājyaṃ tvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva bharatena prasāditaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
jābāles tu vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaḥ satyātmanāṃ varaḥ 
uvāca parayā yuktyā svabuddhyā cāvipannayā  RamS 
bhavān me priyakāmārthaṃ vacanaṃ yad ihoktavān 
akāryaṃ kāryasaṃkāśam apathyaṃ pathyasaṃmitam  RamS 
nirmaryādas tu puruṣaḥ pāpācārasamanvitaḥ 
mānaṃ na labhate satsu bhinnacāritradarśanaḥ  RamS 
kulīnam akulīnaṃ vā vīraṃ puruṣamāninam 
cāritram eva vyākhyāti śuciṃ vā yadi vāśucim  RamS 
anāryas tv āryasaṃkāśaḥ śaucāddhīnas tathā śuciḥ 
lakṣaṇyavad alakṣaṇyo duḥśīlaḥ śīlavān iva  RamS 
adharmaṃ dharmaveṣeṇa yadīmaṃ lokasaṃkaram 
abhipatsye śubhaṃ hitvā kriyāvidhivivarjitam  RamS 
kaś cetayānaḥ puruṣaḥ kāryākāryavicakṣaṇaḥ 
bahu maṃsyati māṃ loke durvṛttaṃ lokadūṣaṇam  RamS 
kasya yāsyāmy ahaṃ vṛttaṃ kena vā svargam āpnuyām 
anayā vartamāno 'haṃ vṛttyā hīnapratijñayā  RamS 
kāmavṛttas tv ayaṃ lokaḥ kṛtsnaḥ samupavartate 
yadvṛttāḥ santi rājānas tadvṛttāḥ santi hi prajāḥ  RamS 
satyam evānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca rājavṛttaṃ sanātanam 
tasmāt satyātmakaṃ rājyaṃ satye lokaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  RamS 
ṛṣayaś caiva devāś ca satyam eva hi menire 
satyavādī hi loke 'smin paramaṃ gacchati kṣayam  RamS 
udvijante yathā sarpān narād anṛtavādinaḥ 
dharmaḥ satyaṃ paro loke mūlaṃ svargasya cocyate  RamS 
satyam eveśvaro loke satyaṃ padmā samāśritā 
satyamūlāni sarvāṇi satyān nāsti paraṃ padam  RamS 
dattam iṣṭaṃ hutaṃ caiva taptāni ca tapāṃsi ca 
vedāḥ satyapratiṣṭhānās tasmāt satyaparo bhavet  RamS 
ekaḥ pālayate lokam ekaḥ pālayate kulam 
majjaty eko hi niraya ekaḥ svarge mahīyate  RamS 
so 'haṃ pitur nideśaṃ tu kimarthaṃ nānupālaye 
satyapratiśravaḥ satyaṃ satyena samayīkṛtaḥ  RamS 
naiva lobhān na mohād vā na cājñānāt tamo'nvitaḥ 
setuṃ satyasya bhetsyāmi guroḥ satyapratiśravaḥ  RamS 
asatyasaṃdhasya sataś calasyāsthiracetasaḥ 
naiva devā na pitaraḥ pratīcchantīti naḥ śrutam  RamS 
pratyagātmam imaṃ dharmaṃ satyaṃ paśyāmy ahaṃ svayam 
bhāraḥ satpuruṣācīrṇas tadartham abhinandyate  RamS 
kṣātraṃ dharmam ahaṃ tyakṣye hy adharmaṃ dharmasaṃhitam 
kṣudrair nṛśaṃsair lubdhaiś ca sevitaṃ pāpakarmabhiḥ  RamS 
kāyena kurute pāpaṃ manasā sampradhārya ca 
anṛtaṃ jihvayā cāha trividhaṃ karma pātakam  RamS 
bhūmiḥ kīrtir yaśo lakṣmīḥ puruṣaṃ prārthayanti hi 
svargasthaṃ cānubadhnanti satyam eva bhajeta tat  RamS 
śreṣṭhaṃ hy anāryam eva syād yad bhavān avadhārya mām 
āha yuktikarair vākyair idaṃ bhadraṃ kuruṣva ha  RamS 
kathaṃ hy ahaṃ pratijñāya vanavāsam imaṃ guroḥ 
bharatasya kariṣyāmi vaco hitvā guror vacaḥ  RamS 
sthirā mayā pratijñātā pratijñā gurusaṃnidhau 
prahṛṣṭamānasā devī kaikeyī cābhavat tadā  RamS 
vanavāsaṃ vasann evaṃ śucir niyatabhojanaḥ 
mūlaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ puṇyaiḥ pitḥn devāṃś ca tarpayan  RamS 
saṃtuṣṭapañcavargo 'haṃ lokayātrāṃ pravartaye 
akuhaḥ śraddadhānaḥ san kāryākāryavicakṣaṇaḥ  RamS 
karmabhūmim imāṃ prāpya kartavyaṃ karma yac chubham 
agnir vāyuś ca somaś ca karmaṇāṃ phalabhāginaḥ  RamS 
śataṃ kratūnām āhṛtya devarāṭ tridivaṃ gataḥ 
tapāṃsy ugrāṇi cāsthāya divaṃ yātā maharṣayaḥ  RamS 
satyaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca parākramaṃ ca bhūtānukampāṃ priyavāditāṃ ca 
dvijātidevātithipūjanaṃ ca panthānam āhus tridivasya santaḥ  RamS 
dharme ratāḥ satpuruṣaiḥ sametās tejasvino dānaguṇapradhānāḥ 
ahiṃsakā vītamalāś ca loke bhavanti pūjyā munayaḥ pradhānāḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
kruddham ājñāya rāmaṃ tu vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyuvāca ha 
jābālir api jānīte lokasyāsya gatāgatim 
nivartayitukāmas tu tvām etad vākyam abravīt  RamS 
imāṃ lokasamutpattiṃ lokanātha nibodha me 
sarvaṃ salilam evāsīt pṛthivī yatra nirmitā 
tataḥ samabhavad brahmā svayambhūr daivataiḥ saha  RamS 
sa varāhas tato bhūtvā projjahāra vasuṃdharām 
asṛjac ca jagat sarvaṃ saha putraiḥ kṛtātmabhiḥ  RamS 
ākāśaprabhavo brahmā śāśvato nitya avyayaḥ 
tasmān marīciḥ saṃjajñe marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ sutaḥ  RamS 
vivasvān kaśyapāj jajñe manur vaivasvataḥ smṛtaḥ 
sa tu prajāpatiḥ pūrvam ikṣvākus tu manoḥ sutaḥ  RamS 
yasyeyaṃ prathamaṃ dattā samṛddhā manunā mahī 
tam ikṣvākum ayodhyāyāṃ rājānaṃ viddhi pūrvakam  RamS 
ikṣvākos tu sutaḥ śrīmān kukṣir eveti viśrutaḥ 
kukṣer athātmajo vīro vikukṣir udapadyata  RamS 
vikukṣes tu mahātejā bāṇaḥ putraḥ pratāpavān 
bāṇasya tu mahābāhur anaraṇyo mahāyaśāḥ  RamS 
nānāvṛṣṭir babhūvāsmin na durbhikṣaṃ satāṃ vare 
anaraṇye mahārāje taskaro vāpi kaścana  RamS 
anaraṇyān mahābāhuḥ pṛthū rājā babhūva ha 
tasmāt pṛthor mahārājas triśaṅkur udapadyata 
sa satyavacanād vīraḥ saśarīro divaṃ gataḥ  RamS 
triśaṅkor abhavat sūnur dhundhumāro mahāyaśāḥ 
dhundhumārān mahātejā yuvanāśvo vyajāyata  RamS 
yuvanāśvasutaḥ śrīmān māndhātā samapadyata 
māndhātus tu mahātejāḥ susaṃdhir udapadyata  RamS 
susaṃdher api putrau dvau dhruvasaṃdhiḥ prasenajit 
yaśasvī dhruvasaṃdhes tu bharato ripusūdanaḥ  RamS 
bharatāt tu mahābāhor asito nāma jāyata 
yasyaite pratirājāna udapadyanta śatravaḥ 
haihayās tālajaṅghāś ca śūrāś ca śaśabindavaḥ  RamS 
tāṃs tu sarvān prativyūhya yuddhe rājā pravāsitaḥ 
sa ca śailavare ramye babhūvābhirato muniḥ 
dve cāsya bhārye garbhiṇyau babhūvatur iti śrutiḥ  RamS 
bhārgavaś cyavano nāma himavantam upāśritaḥ 
tam ṛṣiṃ samupāgamya kālindī tv abhyavādayat  RamS 
sa tām abhyavadad vipro varepsuṃ putrajanmani 
tataḥ sā gṛham āgamya devī putraṃ vyajāyata  RamS 
sapatnyā tu garas tasyai datto garbhajighāṃsayā 
gareṇa saha tenaiva jātaḥ sa sagaro 'bhavat  RamS 
sa rājā sagaro nāma yaḥ samudram akhānayat 
iṣṭvā parvaṇi vegena trāsayantam imāḥ prajāḥ  RamS 
asamañjas tu putro 'bhūt sagarasyeti naḥ śrutam 
jīvann eva sa pitrā tu nirastaḥ pāpakarmakṛt  RamS 
aṃśumān iti putro 'bhūd asamañjasya vīryavān 
dilīpo 'ṃśumataḥ putro dilīpasya bhagīrathaḥ  RamS 
bhagīrathāt kakutsthas tu kākutsthā yena tu smṛtāḥ 
kakutsthasya tu putro 'bhūd raghur yena tu rāghavaḥ  RamS 
raghos tu putras tejasvī pravṛddhaḥ puruṣādakaḥ 
kalmāṣapādaḥ saudāsa ity evaṃ prathito bhuvi  RamS 
kalmāṣapādaputro 'bhūc chaṅkhaṇas tv iti viśrutaḥ 
yas tu tad vīryam āsādya sahaseno vyanīnaśat  RamS 
śaṅkhaṇasya tu putro 'bhūc chūraḥ śrīmān sudarśanaḥ 
sudarśanasyāgnivarṇa agnivarṇasya śīghragaḥ  RamS 
śīghragasya maruḥ putro maroḥ putraḥ praśuśrukaḥ 
praśuśrukasya putro 'bhūd ambarīṣo mahādyutiḥ  RamS 
ambarīṣasya putro 'bhūn nahuṣaḥ satyavikramaḥ 
nahuṣasya ca nābhāgaḥ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ  RamS 
ajaś ca suvrataś caiva nābhāgasya sutāv ubhau 
ajasya caiva dharmātmā rājā daśarathaḥ sutaḥ  RamS 
tasya jyeṣṭho 'si dāyādo rāma ity abhiviśrutaḥ 
tad gṛhāṇa svakaṃ rājyam avekṣasva jagan nṛpa  RamS 
ikṣvākūṇāṃ hi sarveṣāṃ rājā bhavati pūrvajaḥ 
pūrvajenāvaraḥ putro jyeṣṭho rājye 'bhiṣicyate  RamS 
sa rāghavāṇāṃ kuladharmam ātmanaḥ sanātanaṃ nādya vihātum arhasi 
prabhūtaratnām anuśādhi medinīṃ prabhūtarāṣṭrāṃ pitṛvan mahāyaśāḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
vasiṣṭhas tu tadā rāmam uktvā rājapurohitaḥ 
abravīd dharmasaṃyuktaṃ punar evāparaṃ vacaḥ  RamS 
puruṣasyeha jātasya bhavanti guravas trayaḥ 
ācāryaś caiva kākutstha pitā mātā ca rāghava  RamS 
pitā hy enaṃ janayati puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabha 
prajñāṃ dadāti cācāryas tasmāt sa gurur ucyate  RamS 
sa te 'haṃ pitur ācāryas tava caiva paraṃtapa 
mama tvaṃ vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  RamS 
imā hi te pariṣadaḥ śreṇayaś ca samāgatāḥ 
eṣu tāta caran dharmaṃ nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  RamS 
vṛddhāyā dharmaśīlāyā mātur nārhasy avartitum 
asyās tu vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  RamS 
bharatasya vacaḥ kurvan yācamānasya rāghava 
ātmānaṃ nātivartes tvaṃ satyadharmaparākrama  RamS 
evaṃ madhuram uktas tu guruṇā rāghavaḥ svayam 
pratyuvāca samāsīnaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ  RamS 
yan mātāpitarau vṛttaṃ tanaye kurutaḥ sadā 
na supratikaraṃ tat tu mātrā pitrā ca yat kṛtam  RamS 
yathāśakti pradānena snāpanāc chādanena ca 
nityaṃ ca priyavādena tathā saṃvardhanena ca  RamS 
sa hi rājā janayitā pitā daśaratho mama 
ājñātaṃ yan mayā tasya na tan mithyā bhaviṣyati  RamS 
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa bharataḥ pratyanantaram 
uvāca paramodāraḥ sūtaṃ paramadurmanāḥ  RamS 
iha me sthaṇḍile śīghraṃ kuśān āstara sārathe 
āryaṃ pratyupavekṣyāmi yāvan me na prasīdati  RamS 
anāhāro nirāloko dhanahīno yathā dvijaḥ 
śeṣye purastāc chālāyā yāvan na pratiyāsyati  RamS 
sa tu rāmam avekṣantaṃ sumantraṃ prekṣya durmanāḥ 
kuśottaram upasthāpya bhūmāv evāstarat svayam  RamS 
tam uvāca mahātejā rāmo rājarṣisattamāḥ 
kiṃ māṃ bharata kurvāṇaṃ tāta pratyupavekṣyasi  RamS 
brāhmaṇo hy ekapārśvena narān roddhum ihārhati 
na tu mūrdhāvasiktānāṃ vidhiḥ pratyupaveśane  RamS 
uttiṣṭha naraśārdūla hitvaitad dāruṇaṃ vratam 
puravaryām itaḥ kṣipram ayodhyāṃ yāhi rāghava  RamS 
āsīnas tv eva bharataḥ paurajānapadaṃ janam 
uvāca sarvataḥ prekṣya kim āryaṃ nānuśāsatha  RamS 
te tam ūcur mahātmānaṃ paurajānapadā janāḥ 
kākutstham abhijānīmaḥ samyag vadati rāghavaḥ  RamS 
eṣo 'pi hi mahābhāgaḥ pitur vacasi tiṣṭhati 
ata eva na śaktāḥ smo vyāvartayitum añjasā  RamS 
teṣām ājñāya vacanaṃ rāmo vacanam abravīt 
evaṃ nibodha vacanaṃ suhṛdāṃ dharmacakṣuṣām  RamS 
etac caivobhayaṃ śrutvā samyak saṃpaśya rāghava 
uttiṣṭha tvaṃ mahābāho māṃ ca spṛśa tathodakam  RamS 
athotthāya jalaṃ spṛṣṭvā bharato vākyam abravīt 
śṛṇvantu me pariṣado mantriṇaḥ śreṇayas tathā  RamS 
na yāce pitaraṃ rājyaṃ nānuśāsāmi mātaram 
āryaṃ paramadharmajñam abhijānāmi rāghavam  RamS 
yadi tv avaśyaṃ vastavyaṃ kartavyaṃ ca pitur vacaḥ 
aham eva nivatsyāmi caturdaśa vane samāḥ  RamS 
dharmātmā tasya tathyena bhrātur vākyena vismitaḥ 
uvāca rāmaḥ samprekṣya paurajānapadaṃ janam  RamS 
vikrītam āhitaṃ krītaṃ yat pitrā jīvatā mama 
na tal lopayituṃ śakyaṃ mayā vā bharatena vā  RamS 
upadhir na mayā kāryo vanavāse jugupsitaḥ 
yuktam uktaṃ ca kaikeyyā pitrā me sukṛtaṃ kṛtam  RamS 
jānāmi bharataṃ kṣāntaṃ gurusatkārakāriṇam 
sarvam evātra kalyāṇaṃ satyasaṃdhe mahātmani  RamS 
anena dharmaśīlena vanāt pratyāgataḥ punaḥ 
bhrātrā saha bhaviṣyāmi pṛthivyāḥ patir uttamaḥ  RamS 
vṛto rājā hi kaikeyyā mayā tadvacanaṃ kṛtam 
anṛtān mocayānena pitaraṃ taṃ mahīpatim  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tam apratimatejobhyāṃ bhrātṛbhyāṃ romaharṣaṇam 
vismitāḥ saṃgamaṃ prekṣya samavetā maharṣayaḥ  RamS 
antarhitās tv ṛṣigaṇāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ 
tau bhrātarau mahātmānau kākutsthau praśaśaṃsire  RamS 
sa dhanyo yasya putrau dvau dharmajñau dharmavikramau 
śrutvā vayaṃ hi sambhāṣām ubhayoḥ spṛhayāmahe  RamS 
tatas tv ṛṣigaṇāḥ kṣipraṃ daśagrīvavadhaiṣiṇaḥ 
bharataṃ rājaśārdūlam ity ūcuḥ saṃgatā vacaḥ  RamS 
kule jāta mahāprājña mahāvṛtta mahāyaśaḥ 
grāhyaṃ rāmasya vākyaṃ te pitaraṃ yady avekṣase  RamS 
sadānṛṇam imaṃ rāmaṃ vayam icchāmahe pituḥ 
anṛṇatvāc ca kaikeyyāḥ svargaṃ daśaratho gataḥ  RamS 
etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ gandharvāḥ samaharṣayaḥ 
rājarṣayaś caiva tathā sarve svāṃ svāṃ gatiṃ gatāḥ  RamS 
hlāditas tena vākyena śubhena śubhadarśanaḥ 
rāmaḥ saṃhṛṣṭavadanas tān ṛṣīn abhyapūjayat  RamS 
srastagātras tu bharataḥ sa vācā sajjamānayā 
kṛtāñjalir idaṃ vākyaṃ rāghavaṃ punar abravīt  RamS 
rājadharmam anuprekṣya kuladharmānusaṃtatim 
kartum arhasi kākutstha mama mātuś ca yācanām  RamS 
rakṣituṃ sumahad rājyam aham ekas tu notsahe 
paurajānapadāṃś cāpi raktān rañjayituṃ tathā  RamS 
jñātayaś ca hi yodhāś ca mitrāṇi suhṛdaś ca naḥ 
tvām eva pratikāṅkṣante parjanyam iva karṣakāḥ  RamS 
idaṃ rājyaṃ mahāprājña sthāpaya pratipadya hi 
śaktimān asi kākutstha lokasya paripālane  RamS 
ity uktvā nyapatad bhrātuḥ pādayor bharatas tadā 
bhṛśaṃ samprārthayāmāsa rāmam evaṃ priyaṃvadaḥ  RamS 
tam aṅke bhrātaraṃ kṛtvā rāmo vacanam abravīt 
śyāmaṃ nalinapattrākṣaṃ mattahaṃsasvaraṃ svayam  RamS 
āgatā tvām iyaṃ buddhiḥ svajā vainayikī ca yā 
bhṛśam utsahase tāta rakṣituṃ pṛthivīm api  RamS 
amātyaiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca buddhimadbhiś ca mantribhiḥ 
sarvakāryāṇi saṃmantrya sumahānty api kāraya  RamS 
lakṣmīś candrād apeyād vā himavān vā himaṃ tyajet 
atīyāt sāgaro velāṃ na pratijñām ahaṃ pituḥ  RamS 
kāmād vā tāta lobhād vā mātrā tubhyam idaṃ kṛtam 
na tan manasi kartavyaṃ vartitavyaṃ ca mātṛvat  RamS 
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ bharataḥ kausalyāsutam abravīt 
tejasādityasaṃkāśaṃ pratipaccandradarśanam  RamS 
adhirohārya pādābhyāṃ pāduke hemabhūṣite 
ete hi sarvalokasya yogakṣemaṃ vidhāsyataḥ  RamS 
so 'dhiruhya naravyāghraḥ pāduke hy avaruhya ca 
prāyacchat sumahātejā bharatāya mahātmane  RamS 
sa pāduke te bharataḥ pratāpavān svalaṃkṛte samparigṛhya dharmavit 
pradakṣiṇaṃ caiva cakāra rāghavaṃ cakāra caivottamanāgamūrdhani  RamS 
athānupūrvyāt pratipūjya taṃ janaṃ gurūṃś ca mantriprakṛtīs tathānujau 
vyasarjayad rāghavavaṃśavardhanaḥ sthitaḥ svadharme himavān ivācalaḥ  RamS 
taṃ mātaro bāṣpagṛhītakaṇṭhyo duḥkhena nāmantrayituṃ hi śekuḥ 
sa tv eva mātḥn abhivādya sarvā rudan kuṭīṃ svāṃ praviveśa rāmaḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tataḥ śirasi kṛtvā tu pāduke bharatas tadā 
āruroha rathaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ  RamS 
vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca jābāliś ca dṛḍhavrataḥ 
agrataḥ prayayuḥ sarve mantriṇo mantrapūjitāḥ  RamS 
mandākinīṃ nadīṃ ramyāṃ prāṅmukhās te yayus tadā 
pradakṣiṇaṃ ca kurvāṇāś citrakūṭaṃ mahāgirim  RamS 
paśyan dhātusahasrāṇi ramyāṇi vividhāni ca 
prayayau tasya pārśvena sasainyo bharatas tadā  RamS 
adūrāc citrakūṭasya dadarśa bharatas tadā 
āśramaṃ yatra sa munir bharadvājaḥ kṛtālayaḥ  RamS 
sa tam āśramam āgamya bharadvājasya buddhimān 
avatīrya rathāt pādau vavande kulanandanaḥ  RamS 
tato hṛṣṭo bharadvājo bharataṃ vākyam abravīt 
api kṛtyaṃ kṛtaṃ tāta rāmeṇa ca samāgatam  RamS 
evam uktas tu bharato bharadvājena dhīmatā 
pratyuvāca bharadvājaṃ bharato dharmavatsalaḥ  RamS 
sa yācyamāno guruṇā mayā ca dṛḍhavikramaḥ 
rāghavaḥ paramaprīto vasiṣṭhaṃ vākyam abravīt  RamS 
pituḥ pratijñāṃ tām eva pālayiṣyāmi tattvataḥ 
caturdaśa hi varṣāṇi yā pratijñā pitur mama  RamS 
evam ukto mahāprājño vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyuvāca ha 
vākyajño vākyakuśalaṃ rāghavaṃ vacanaṃ mahat  RamS 
ete prayaccha saṃhṛṣṭaḥ pāduke hemabhūṣite 
ayodhyāyāṃ mahāprājña yogakṣemakare tava  RamS 
evam ukto vasiṣṭhena rāghavaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ sthitaḥ 
pāduke hemavikṛte mama rājyāya te dadau  RamS 
nivṛtto 'ham anujñāto rāmeṇa sumahātmanā 
ayodhyām eva gacchāmi gṛhītvā pāduke śubhe  RamS 
etac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ bharatasya mahātmanaḥ 
bharadvājaḥ śubhataraṃ munir vākyam udāharat  RamS 
naitac citraṃ naravyāghra śīlavṛttavatāṃ vara 
yad āryaṃ tvayi tiṣṭhet tu nimne vṛṣṭim ivodakam  RamS 
amṛtaḥ sa mahābāhuḥ pitā daśarathas tava 
yasya tvam īdṛśaḥ putro dharmātmā dharmavatsalaḥ  RamS 
tam ṛṣiṃ tu mahātmānam uktavākyaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ 
āmantrayitum ārebhe caraṇāv upagṛhya ca  RamS 
tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā bharadvājaṃ punaḥ punaḥ 
bharatas tu yayau śrīmān ayodhyāṃ saha mantribhiḥ  RamS 
yānaiś ca śakaṭaiś caiva hayair nāgaiś ca sā camūḥ 
punar nivṛttā vistīrṇā bharatasyānuyāyinī  RamS 
tatas te yamunāṃ divyāṃ nadīṃ tīrtvormimālinīm 
dadṛśus tāṃ punaḥ sarve gaṅgāṃ śivajalāṃ nadīm  RamS 
tāṃ ramyajalasampūrṇāṃ saṃtīrya sahabāndhavaḥ 
śṛṅgaverapuraṃ ramyaṃ praviveśa sasainikaḥ  RamS 
śṛṅgaverapurād bhūya ayodhyāṃ saṃdadarśa ha 
bharato duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ sārathiṃ cedam abravīt  RamS 
sārathe paśya vidhvastā ayodhyā na prakāśate 
nirākārā nirānandā dīnā pratihatasvanā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
snigdhagambhīraghoṣeṇa syandanenopayān prabhuḥ 
ayodhyāṃ bharataḥ kṣipraṃ praviveśa mahāyaśāḥ  RamS 
biḍālolūkacaritām ālīnanaravāraṇām 
timirābhyāhatāṃ kālīm aprakāśāṃ niśām iva  RamS 
rāhuśatroḥ priyāṃ patnīṃ śriyā prajvalitaprabhām 
graheṇābhyutthitenaikāṃ rohiṇīm iva pīḍitām  RamS 
alpoṣṇakṣubdhasalilāṃ gharmottaptavihaṃgamām 
līnamīnajhaṣagrāhāṃ kṛśāṃ girinadīm iva  RamS 
vidhūmām iva hemābhām adhvarāgnisamutthitām 
havirabhyukṣitāṃ paścāc chikhāṃ vipralayaṃ gatām  RamS 
vidhvastakavacāṃ rugṇagajavājirathadhvajām 
hatapravīrām āpannāṃ camūm iva mahāhave  RamS 
saphenāṃ sasvanāṃ bhūtvā sāgarasya samutthitām 
praśāntamārutoddhūtāṃ jalormim iva niḥsvanām  RamS 
tyaktāṃ yajñāyudhaiḥ sarvair abhirūpaiś ca yājakaiḥ 
sutyākāle vinirvṛtte vediṃ gataravām iva  RamS 
goṣṭhamadhye sthitām ārtām acarantīṃ navaṃ tṛṇam 
govṛṣeṇa parityaktāṃ gavāṃ patnīm ivotsukām  RamS 
prabhākarālaiḥ susnigdhaiḥ prajvaladbhir ivottamaiḥ 
viyuktāṃ maṇibhir jātyair navāṃ muktāvalīm iva  RamS 
sahasā calitāṃ sthānān mahīṃ puṇyakṣayād gatām 
saṃhṛtadyutivistārāṃ tārām iva divaś cyutām  RamS 
puṣpanaddhāṃ vasantānte mattabhramaraśālinīm 
drutadāvāgnivipruṣṭāṃ klāntāṃ vanalatām iva  RamS 
saṃmūḍhanigamāṃ sarvāṃ saṃkṣiptavipaṇāpaṇām 
pracchannaśaśinakṣatrāṃ dyām ivāmbudharair vṛtām  RamS 
kṣīṇapānottamair bhinnaiḥ śarāvair abhisaṃvṛtām 
hataśauṇḍām ivākāśe pānabhūmim asaṃskṛtām  RamS 
vṛkṇabhūmitalāṃ nimnāṃ vṛkṇapātraiḥ samāvṛtām 
upayuktodakāṃ bhagnāṃ prapāṃ nipatitām iva  RamS 
vipulāṃ vitatāṃ caiva yuktapāśāṃ tarasvinām 
bhūmau bāṇair viniṣkṛttāṃ patitāṃ jyām ivāyudhāt  RamS 
sahasā yuddhaśauṇḍena hayāroheṇa vāhitām 
nikṣiptabhāṇḍām utsṛṣṭāṃ kiśorīm iva durbalām  RamS 
prāvṛṣi pravigāḍhāyāṃ praviṣṭasyābhramaṇḍalam 
pracchannāṃ nīlajīmūtair bhāskarasya prabhām iva  RamS 
bharatas tu rathasthaḥ sañ śrīmān daśarathātmajaḥ 
vāhayantaṃ rathaśreṣṭhaṃ sārathiṃ vākyam abravīt  RamS 
kiṃ nu khalv adya gambhīro mūrchito na niśamyate 
yathāpuram ayodhyāyāṃ gītavāditraniḥsvanaḥ  RamS 
vāruṇīmadagandhāś ca mālyagandhaś ca mūrchitaḥ 
dhūpitāgarugandhaś ca na pravāti samantataḥ  RamS 
yānapravaraghoṣaś ca snigdhaś ca hayaniḥsvanaḥ 
pramattagajanādaś ca mahāṃś ca rathaniḥsvanaḥ 
nedānīṃ śrūyate puryām asyāṃ rāme vivāsite  RamS 
taruṇaiś cāruveṣaiś ca narair unnatagāmibhiḥ 
saṃpatadbhir ayodhyāyāṃ na vibhānti mahāpathāḥ  RamS 
evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ jalpan viveśa vasatiṃ pituḥ 
tena hīnāṃ narendreṇa siṃhahīnāṃ guhām iva  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
tato nikṣipya mātḥn sa ayodhyāyāṃ dṛḍhavrataḥ 
bharataḥ śokasaṃtapto gurūn idam athābravīt  RamS 
nandigrāmaṃ gamiṣyāmi sarvān āmantraye 'dya vaḥ 
tatra duḥkham idaṃ sarvaṃ sahiṣye rāghavaṃ vinā  RamS 
gataś ca hi divaṃ rājā vanasthaś ca gurur mama 
rāmaṃ pratīkṣe rājyāya sa hi rājā mahāyaśāḥ  RamS 
etac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ bharatasya mahātmanaḥ 
abruvan mantriṇaḥ sarve vasiṣṭhaś ca purohitaḥ  RamS 
sadṛśaṃ ślāghanīyaṃ ca yad uktaṃ bharata tvayā 
vacanaṃ bhrātṛvātsalyād anurūpaṃ tavaiva tat  RamS 
nityaṃ te bandhulubdhasya tiṣṭhato bhrātṛsauhṛde 
āryamārgaṃ prapannasya nānumanyeta kaḥ pumān  RamS 
mantriṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā yathābhilaṣitaṃ priyam 
abravīt sārathiṃ vākyaṃ ratho me yujyatām iti  RamS 
prahṛṣṭavadanaḥ sarvā mātḥn samabhivādya saḥ 
āruroha rathaṃ śrīmāñ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ  RamS 
āruhya tu rathaṃ śīghraṃ śatrughnabharatāv ubhau 
yayatuḥ paramaprītau vṛtau mantripurohitaiḥ  RamS 
agrato guravas tatra vasiṣṭhapramukhā dvijāḥ 
prayayuḥ prāṅmukhāḥ sarve nandigrāmo yato 'bhavat  RamS 
balaṃ ca tad anāhūtaṃ gajāśvarathasaṃkulam 
prayayau bharate yāte sarve ca puravāsinaḥ  RamS 
rathasthaḥ sa tu dharmātmā bharato bhrātṛvatsalaḥ 
nandigrāmaṃ yayau tūrṇaṃ śirasy ādhāya pāduke  RamS 
tatas tu bharataḥ kṣipraṃ nandigrāmaṃ praviśya saḥ 
avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gurūn idam uvāca ha  RamS 
etad rājyaṃ mama bhrātrā dattaṃ saṃnyāsavat svayam 
yogakṣemavahe ceme pāduke hemabhūṣite 
tam imaṃ pālayiṣyāmi rāghavāgamanaṃ prati  RamS 
kṣipraṃ saṃyojayitvā tu rāghavasya punaḥ svayam 
caraṇau tau tu rāmasya drakṣyāmi sahapādukau  RamS 
tato nikṣiptabhāro 'haṃ rāghaveṇa samāgataḥ 
nivedya gurave rājyaṃ bhajiṣye guruvṛttitām  RamS 
rāghavāya ca saṃnyāsaṃ dattveme varapāduke 
rājyaṃ cedam ayodhyāṃ ca dhūtapāpo bhavāmi ca  RamS 
abhiṣikte tu kākutsthe prahṛṣṭamudite jane 
prītir mama yaśaś caiva bhaved rājyāc caturguṇam  RamS 
evaṃ tu vilapan dīno bharataḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ 
nandigrāme 'karod rājyaṃ duḥkhito mantribhiḥ saha  RamS 
sa valkalajaṭādhārī muniveṣadharaḥ prabhuḥ 
nandigrāme 'vasad vīraḥ sasainyo bharatas tadā  RamS 
rāmāgamanam ākāṅkṣan bharato bhrātṛvatsalaḥ 
bhrātur vacanakārī ca pratijñāpāragas tadā  RamS 
pāduke tv abhiṣicyātha nandigrāme 'vasat tadā 
bharataḥ śāsanaṃ sarvaṃ pādukābhyāṃ nyavedayat  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
pratiprayāte bharate vasan rāmas tapovane 
lakṣayāmāsa sodvegam athautsukyaṃ tapasvinām  RamS 
ye tatra citrakūṭasya purastāt tāpasāśrame 
rāmam āśritya niratās tān alakṣayad utsukān  RamS 
nayanair bhṛkuṭībhiś ca rāmaṃ nirdiśya śaṅkitāḥ 
anyonyam upajalpantaḥ śanaiś cakrur mithaḥ kathāḥ  RamS 
teṣām autsukyam ālakṣya rāmas tv ātmani śaṅkitaḥ 
kṛtāñjalir uvācedam ṛṣiṃ kulapatiṃ tataḥ  RamS 
na kaccid bhagavan kiṃcit pūrvavṛttam idaṃ mayi 
dṛśyate vikṛtaṃ yena vikriyante tapasvinaḥ  RamS 
pramādāc caritaṃ kaccit kiṃcin nāvarajasya me 
lakṣmaṇasyarṣibhir dṛṣṭaṃ nānurūpam ivātmanaḥ  RamS 
kaccic chuśrūṣamāṇā vaḥ śuśrūṣaṇaparā mayi 
pramadābhyucitāṃ vṛttiṃ sītā yuktaṃ na vartate  RamS 
atharṣir jarayā vṛddhas tapasā ca jarāṃ gataḥ 
vepamāna ivovāca rāmaṃ bhūtadayāparam  RamS 
kutaḥ kalyāṇasattvāyāḥ kalyāṇābhirates tathā 
calanaṃ tāta vaidehyās tapasviṣu viśeṣataḥ  RamS 
tvannimittam idaṃ tāvat tāpasān prati vartate 
rakṣobhyas tena saṃvignāḥ kathayanti mithaḥ kathāḥ  RamS 
rāvaṇāvarajaḥ kaścit kharo nāmeha rākṣasaḥ 
utpāṭya tāpasān sarvāñ janasthānaniketanān  RamS 
dhṛṣṭaś ca jitakāśī ca nṛśaṃsaḥ puruṣādakaḥ 
avaliptaś ca pāpaś ca tvāṃ ca tāta na mṛṣyate  RamS 
tvaṃ yadā prabhṛti hy asminn āśrame tāta vartase 
tadā prabhṛti rakṣāṃsi viprakurvanti tāpasān  RamS 
darśayanti hi bībhatsaiḥ krūrair bhīṣaṇakair api 
nānā rūpair virūpaiś ca rūpair asukhadarśanaiḥ  RamS 
apraśastair aśucibhiḥ saṃprayojya ca tāpasān 
pratighnanty aparān kṣipram anāryāḥ purataḥ sthitāḥ  RamS 
teṣu teṣv āśramasthāneṣv abuddham avalīya ca 
ramante tāpasāṃs tatra nāśayanto 'lpacetasaḥ  RamS 
apakṣipanti srugbhāṇḍān agnīn siñcanti vāriṇā 
kalaśāṃś ca pramṛdnanti havane samupasthite  RamS 
tair durātmabhir āviṣṭān āśramān prajihāsavaḥ 
gamanāyānyadeśasya codayanty ṛṣayo 'dya mām  RamS 
tat purā rāma śārīrām upahiṃsāṃ tapasviṣu 
darśayanti hi duṣṭās te tyakṣyāma imam āśramam  RamS 
bahumūlaphalaṃ citram avidūrād ito vanam 
purāṇāśramam evāhaṃ śrayiṣye sagaṇaḥ punaḥ  RamS 
kharas tvayy api cāyuktaṃ purā tāta pravartate 
sahāsmābhir ito gaccha yadi buddhiḥ pravartate  RamS 
sakalatrasya saṃdeho nityaṃ yat tasya rāghava 
samarthasyāpi hi sato vāso duḥkham ihādya te  RamS 
ity uktavantaṃ rāmas taṃ rājaputras tapasvinam 
na śaśākottarair vākyair avaroddhuṃ samutsukam  RamS 
abhinandya samāpṛcchya samādhāya ca rāghavam 
sa jagāmāśramaṃ tyaktvā kulaiḥ kulapatiḥ saha  RamS 
rāmaḥ saṃsādhya tv ṛṣigaṇam anugamanād deśāt tasmāt kulapatim abhivādyarṣim 
samyakprītais tair anumata upadiṣṭārthaḥ puṇyaṃ vāsāya svanilayam upasaṃpede  RamS 
āśramaṃ tv ṛṣivirahitaṃ prabhuḥ kṣaṇam api na jahau sa rāghavaḥ 
rāghavaṃ hi satatam anugatās tāpasāś cārṣacaritadhṛtaguṇāḥ  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
rāghavas tv apayāteṣu tapasviṣu vicintayan 
na tatrārocayad vāsaṃ kāraṇair bahubhis tadā  RamS 
iha me bharato dṛṣṭo mātaraś ca sanāgarāḥ 
sā ca me smṛtir anveti tān nityam anuśocataḥ  RamS 
skandhāvāraniveśena tena tasya mahātmanaḥ 
hayahastikarīṣaiś ca upamardaḥ kṛto bhṛśam  RamS 
tasmād anyatra gacchāma iti saṃcintya rāghavaḥ 
prātiṣṭhata sa vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca saṃgataḥ  RamS 
so 'trer āśramam āsādya taṃ vavande mahāyaśāḥ 
taṃ cāpi bhagavān atriḥ putravat pratyapadyata  RamS 
svayam ātithyam ādiśya sarvam asya susatkṛtam 
saumitriṃ ca mahābhāgāṃ sītāṃ ca samasāntvayat  RamS 
patnīṃ ca samanuprāptāṃ vṛddhām āmantrya satkṛtām 
sāntvayāmāsa dharmajñaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  RamS 
anasūyāṃ mahābhāgāṃ tāpasīṃ dharmacāriṇīm 
pratigṛhṇīṣva vaidehīm abravīd ṛṣisattamaḥ  RamS 
rāmāya cācacakṣe tāṃ tāpasīṃ dharmacāriṇīm 
daśa varṣāṇy anāvṛṣṭyā dagdhe loke nirantaram  RamS 
yayā mūlaphale sṛṣṭe jāhnavī ca pravartitā 
ugreṇa tapasā yuktā niyamaiś cāpy alaṃkṛtā  RamS 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi yayā taptaṃ mahat tapaḥ 
anasūyāvratais tāta pratyūhāś ca nibarhitāḥ  RamS 
devakāryanimittaṃ ca yayā saṃtvaramāṇayā 
daśarātraṃ kṛtvā rātriḥ seyaṃ māteva te 'nagha  RamS 
tām imāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ namaskāryāṃ yaśasvinīm 
abhigacchatu vaidehī vṛddhām akrodhanāṃ sadā  RamS 
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tam ṛṣiṃ tathety uktvā sa rāghavaḥ 
sītām uvāca dharmajñām idaṃ vacanam uttamam  RamS 
rājaputri śrutaṃ tv etan muner asya samīritam 
śreyo'rtham ātmanaḥ śīghram abhigaccha tapasvinīm  RamS 
anasūyeti yā loke karmabhiḥ khyātim āgatā 
tāṃ śīghram abhigaccha tvam abhigamyāṃ tapasvinīm  RamS 
sītā tv etad vacaḥ śrutvā rāghavasya hitaiṣiṇī 
tām atripatnīṃ dharmajñām abhicakrāma maithilī  RamS 
śithilāṃ valitāṃ vṛddhāṃ jarāpāṇḍuramūrdhajām 
satataṃ vepamānāṅgīṃ pravāte kadalī yathā  RamS 
tāṃ tu sītā mahābhāgām anasūyāṃ pativratām 
abhyavādayad avyagrā svaṃ nāma samudāharat  RamS 
abhivādya ca vaidehī tāpasīṃ tām aninditām 
baddhāñjalipuṭā hṛṣṭā paryapṛcchad anāmayam  RamS 
tataḥ sītāṃ mahābhāgāṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ dharmacāriṇīm 
sāntvayanty abravīd dhṛṣṭā diṣṭyā dharmam avekṣase  RamS 
tyaktvā jñātijanaṃ sīte mānam ṛddhiṃ ca mānini 
avaruddhaṃ vane rāmaṃ diṣṭyā tvam anugacchasi  RamS 
nagarastho vanastho vā pāpo vā yadi vāśubhaḥ 
yāsāṃ strīṇāṃ priyo bhartā tāsāṃ lokā mahodayāḥ  RamS 
duḥśīlaḥ kāmavṛtto vā dhanair vā parivarjitaḥ 
strīṇām āryasvabhāvānāṃ paramaṃ daivataṃ patiḥ  RamS 
nāto viśiṣṭaṃ paśyāmi bāndhavaṃ vimṛśanty aham 
sarvatra yogyaṃ vaidehi tapaḥ kṛtam ivāvyayam  RamS 
na tv evam avagacchanti guṇadoṣam asatstriyaḥ 
kāmavaktavyahṛdayā bhartṛnāthāś caranti yāḥ  RamS 
prāpnuvanty ayaśaś caiva dharmabhraṃśaṃ ca maithili 
akāryavaśam āpannāḥ striyo yāḥ khalu tadvidhāḥ  RamS 
tvadvidhās tu guṇair yuktā dṛṣṭalokaparāvarāḥ 
striyaḥ svarge cariṣyanti yathā puṇyakṛtas tathā  RamS 
Rāmāyaṇa Ayodhyākāṇḍa 
sā tv evam uktā vaidehī anasūyānasūyayā 
pratipūjya vaco mandaṃ pravaktum upacakrame  RamS 
naitad āścaryam āryāyā yan māṃ tvam anubhāṣase 
viditaṃ tu mamāpy etad yathā nāryāḥ patir guruḥ  RamS 
yady apy eṣa bhaved bhartā mamārye vṛttavarjitaḥ 
advaidham upacartavyas tathāpy eṣa mayā bhavet  RamS 
kiṃ punar yo guṇaślāghyaḥ sānukrośo jitendriyaḥ 
sthirānurāgo dharmātmā mātṛvartī pitṛpriyaḥ  RamS 
yāṃ vṛttiṃ vartate rāmaḥ kausalyāyāṃ mahābalaḥ 
tām eva nṛpanārīṇām anyāsām api vartate  RamS 
sakṛd dṛṣṭāsv api strīṣu nṛpeṇa nṛpavatsalaḥ 
mātṛvad vartate vīro mānam utsṛjya dharmavit  RamS 
āgacchantyāś ca vijanaṃ vanam evaṃ bhayāvaham 
samāhitaṃ hi me śvaśrvā hṛdaye yat sthitaṃ mama  RamS 
pāṇipradānakāle ca yat purā tv agnisaṃnidhau 
anuśiṣṭā jananyāsmi vākyaṃ tad api me dhṛtam  RamS 
navīkṛtaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ vākyais te dharmacāriṇi 
patiśuśrūṣaṇān nāryās tapo nānyad vidhīyate  RamS 
sāvitrī patiśuśrūṣāṃ kṛtvā svarge mahīyate 
tathā vṛttiś ca yātā tvaṃ patiśuśrūṣayā divam  RamS 
variṣṭhā sarvanārīṇām eṣā ca divi devatā 
rohiṇī ca vinā candraṃ muhūrtam api dṛśyate  RamS 
evaṃvidhāś ca pravarāḥ striyo bhartṛdṛḍhavratāḥ 
devaloke mahīyante puṇyena svena karmaṇā  RamS 
tato 'nasūyā saṃhṛṣṭā śrutvoktaṃ sītayā vacaḥ 
śirasy āghrāya covāca maithilīṃ harṣayanty uta  RamS 
niyamair vividhair āptaṃ tapo hi mahad asti me 
tat saṃśritya balaṃ sīte chandaye tvāṃ śucivrate  RamS 
upapannaṃ ca yuktaṃ ca vacanaṃ tava maithili 
prītā cāsmy ucitaṃ kiṃ te karavāṇi bravīhi me 
kṛtam ity abravīt sītā tapobalasamanvitām  RamS 
sā tv evam uktā dharmajñā tayā prītatarābhavat 
saphalaṃ ca praharṣaṃ te hanta sīte karomy aham  RamS 
idaṃ divyaṃ varaṃ mālyaṃ vastram ābharaṇāni ca 
aṅgarāgaṃ ca vaidehi mahārham anulepanam  RamS 
mayā dattam idaṃ sīte tava gātrāṇi śobhayet 
anurūpam asaṃkliṣṭaṃ nityam eva bhaviṣyati  RamS 
aṅgarāgeṇa divyena liptāṅgī janakātmaje 
śobhayiṣyāmi bhartāraṃ yathā śrīr viṣṇum avyayam  RamS 
sā vastram aṅgarāgaṃ ca bhūṣaṇāni srajas tathā 
maithilī pratijagrāha prītidānam anuttamam  RamS 
pratigṛhya ca tat sītā prītidānaṃ yaśasvinī 
śliṣṭāñjalipuṭā dhīrā samupāsta tapodhanām  RamS 
tathā sītām upāsīnām anasūyā dṛḍhavratā 
vacanaṃ praṣṭum ārebhe kathāṃ kāṃcid anupriyām  RamS 
svayaṃvare kila prāptā tvam anena yaśasvinā 
rāghaveṇeti me sīte kathā śrutim upāgatā  RamS 
tāṃ kathāṃ śrotum icchāmi vistareṇa ca maithili 
yathānubhūtaṃ kārtsnyena tan me tvaṃ vaktum arhasi  RamS 
evam uktā tu sā sītā tāṃ tato dharmacāriṇīm 
śrūyatām iti coktvā vai kathayāmāsa tāṃ kathām  RamS 
mithilādhipatir vīro janako nāma dharmavit 
kṣatradharmaṇy abhirato nyāyataḥ śāsti medinīm  RamS 
tasya lāṅgalahastasya karṣataḥ kṣetramaṇḍalam 
ahaṃ kilotthitā bhittvā jagatīṃ nṛpateḥ sutā  RamS 
sa māṃ dṛṣṭvā narapatir muṣṭivikṣepatatparaḥ 
pāṃśuguṇṭhitasarvāṅgīṃ vismito janako 'bhavat  RamS 
anapatyena ca snehād aṅkam āropya ca svayam 
mameyaṃ tanayety uktvā sneho mayi nipātitaḥ  RamS 
antarikṣe ca vāg uktāpratimāmānuṣī kila 
evam etan narapate dharmeṇa tanayā tava  RamS 
tataḥ prahṛṣṭo dharmātmā pitā me mithilādhipaḥ 
avāpto vipulām ṛddhiṃ mām avāpya narādhipaḥ  RamS
